Lou7-Ka Hok-Im

Te7 1 ChiuN

Su7-gian5:
	1) The5-o-hui-lo5 kok-ha7:
	I2-keng u7 chin-che7 lang5 chin7 in e5 lek8-liong7, chiong chai7 lan2 e5 tiong-kan sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3 ki3-liok8 chhut-lai5 a3.  2) In sou2 sia2 e5 loe7-iong5, si7 chiau3 thoan5 Hok-im e5 lang5 chiong in chu7 khi2-thau5 chhin-bak8 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 tai7-chi3 thoan5 loh8-lai5 hou7 lan2 e5.  3) Chiah-e5 tai7-chi3, goa2 i2-keng u7 chu7-thau5 kau3 boe2 siong5-se3 gian2-kiu3 koe3 a3, sou2-i2 koat-teng7 boeh chiau3 sun7-si7 sia2 chhut-lai5 hian3 hou7 kok-ha7,  4) thang hou7 kok-ha7 chai-iaN2 li2 sou2 nia2-siu7 e5 to7-li2 long2 si7 khak-sit8 e5.

I7-ko3 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 e5 tan3-seng:
	5) Hi-lut8 cho3 Iu5-thai3-ong5 e5 si5, u7 chit8 ui7 che3-si siok8 ti7 a-pi2-a e5 che3-si pan. I e5 mia5 kio3-cho3 Sat-ka-li7-a. I e5 bou2 kio3-cho3 I2-li7-sa-pek, si7 che3-si A-lun5 e5 hio7-tai7.  6) Siong7-chu2 jim7-teng7 in nng7 e5 si7 gi7-jin5; in u7 oan5-choan5 chun-siu2 Chu2 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7 kap kui-lut8.  7) Tan7-si7 in bo5 kiaN2, in-ui7 I2-li7-sa-pek be7 seN-kiaN2, iu7-koh in nng7-e5 long2 chin lau7 a7.
	8) U7 chit8 jit8 lun5-tioh8 Sat-ka-li7-a hit pan e5 che3-si, chai7 Seng3-tian7 teh chip-heng5 che3-si e5 chit-bu7.  9) In chiau3 che3-si e5 koan3-le7 liu khau-a2. I liu-tioh8 jip8-khi3 Chu2 e5 seng3-sou2 hian3-hiuN.  10) I teh hian3-hiuN e5 si5, u7 chit8 toa7 tin7 e5 hoe7-chiong3 ti7 goa7-tian7 teh ki5-to2.  11) U7 chit8 e5 Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 hian2-hian7 lai5 khia7 toa3 hiuN-toaN5 e5 chiaN3-peng5.  12) Sat-ka-li7-a chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 chiu7 sim-sin5 put-an, khi2 kiaN-hiaN5.  13) Tan7-si7 thian-sai3 ka7 i kong2: 몮Sat-ka-li-a, m7-bian2 kiaN, in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 i2-keng u7 chiap-lap8 li2 e5 ki5-to2 a3; li2 e5 bou2 I2-li7-sa-pek teh-boeh ka7 li2 seN chit8 e5 hau7-seN. Li2 tioh8 ka7 i ho7-cho3 Iok-han7.  14) Chit e5 gin2-na2 chhut-si3, e7 hou7 li2 chhiong-moa2 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, ia7 e7 hou7 chin-che7 lang5 chin toa7 hoaN-hi2.  15) Siong7-chu2 e7 khoaN3-tang7 i. I choat8-tui3 be7-eng7-tit lim phu5-to5-chiu2 kap kau7-chiu2. I iau2 ti7 bo2-thai e5 si5 chiu7 chin-che7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chu2-bin5 tng2-lai5 kui-hiong3 Chu2, in e5 Siong7-chu2.  17) I e7 eng7 tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-li7-a e5 cheng-sin5 kap leng5-lek8 lai5 cho3 Chu2 e5 sian-hong. I e7 hou7 lau7-pe7 kap kiaN2-ji5 ho5-kai2, hou7 poe7-gek8 e5 lang5 choan2-hiong3 lai5 kiaN5 cheng3-gi7 e5 lou7. I e7 ui7 Chu2 lai5 chun2-ppi7 Chu2 sou2 moa2-i3 e5 chu2-bin5.몯
	18) Sat-ka-li7-a ka7 thian-sai3 kong2, 몮Kam2 chiaN-sit8 u7-iaN2 e7 an2-ne? In-ui7 goa2 i2-keng lau7 a7, goa2 e5 bou2 ia7 chin-che7 hoe3 a3.몯  19) Thian-sai3 in3 i kong2: 몮Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ka-pek-liat8, teh su7-hau7 Siong7-chu2 e5. Goa2 hong7-beng7 lai5 ka7 li2 kong2, lai5 po3-ko3 li2 chit e5 ho2 siau-sit.  20) TaN li2 tioh8 chu3-i3 thiaN! In-ui7 li2 bo5 siong-sin3 goa2 e5 oe7, li2 e7 pian3-cho3 e2-kau2-e5, be7 kong2-oe7, it-tit8 kau3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 eng3-giam7 hit jit8. goa2 e5 oe7 kau3 si5 it-teng7 e7 sit8-hian7.몯
	21) Hit e5 tiong-kan hiah-e5 hoe7-chiong3 teh theng3-hau7 Sat-ka-li7-a. In-ui7 i jip8-khi3 seng3-sou2 hiah-nih8 ku2 long2 bo5 chhut-lai5, un kam2-kak chin ki5-koai3.  22) I chit8-e7 chhut-lai5, soah be7-tang3 tui3 in kong2-oe7, in chiah chai-iaN2 i ti7 seng3-sou2 e5 lai7-bin7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 i7-siong7. I chi2-u7 e7-hiau2 pi2-kha pi2-chhiu2, iau2 si7 long2 be7 kong2-oe7.
	23) Sat-ka-li7-a chai7 Seng3-tian7 hok8-bu7 e5 ki5-kan koe3 liau2-au7, chiu7 tng2-khi3 in chhu3.  24) Keng-koe3 bo5 loa7 ku2, i e5 bou2 I2-li7-sa-pek chiu7 u7-sin, gou7 goeh8-jit8 ku2 bih tiau5-tiau5, long2 bo5 chhut-mng5.  25) I2-li7-sa-pek kong2: 몮Chu2 ui7 goa2 an2-ne cho3, si7 tek8-piat8 khoaN3-kou3 goa2, hou7 goa2 m7-bian2 siu7 be7-seN-kiaN2 e5 thi2-jiok8!몯

I7-ko3 Ia5-sou e5 tan3-seng:
	26) I2-li7-sa-pek hoai5-in7 e5 te7 lak8 kou2-goeh8, Siong7-chu2 chhe-phai3 thian-sai3 Ka-pek-liat8, khi3 Ka-li7-li7 /seng2 e5 chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7, kio3-cho3 Na2-sat-lek8.  27) I khi3 chhoe7 chit8 ui7 chai7-sek-li2, chiu7-si7 Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN20sun Iok-sek e5 bi7-hun-chhe. Chit e5 chai7-sek-li2 e5 mia5 kio3-cho3 Ma2-li7-a.  28) Thian-sai3 chit8-e7 kau3 i hia, chiu7 tui3 Ma2-li7-a kong2, 몮Goan7 li2 peng5-an! Choe3 siu7 thiong2-ai3 e5, Siong7-chu2 kap li2 tong5-chai7.몯  29) Tan7-si7 Ma2-li7-a thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7, chiu7 sim-sin5 put-an, sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2 i an2-ne ka7 goa2 chheng-an, kiu3-keng3 si7 sim2-mih i3-su3.  30) Thian-sai3 ka7 i kong2: 몮Ma2-li7-a. m7-bian2 kiaN! In-ui7 li2 u7 tit-tioh8 Siong7-chu2 e5 thiong2-ai3.  31) Li2 e7 hoai5-in7 seN chit8 e5 hau7-seN. Li2 tioh8 ka7 I ho7-cho3 Ia5-sou.  32) I e7 hou7 lang5 khoaN3-tang7, e7 hou7 lang5 chheng-hou cho3 몬Chi3-ko Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2.몭 Chu2, Siong7-chu2 ia7 e7 chiong I e5 chou2-sian Tai7-pit8 e5 ong5-ui7 siuN2-su3 I.  33) I ia7 e7 eng2-oan2 thong2-ti7 Nga2-kok e5 kiaN2-sun. I e5 ong5-kok e7 bu5-kiong5 bu5-chin7.몯
	34) Ma2-li7-a chiu7 tui3 thian-sai3 kong2, 몮Goa2 iau2 si7 chai7-sek-li2. An2-choaN3 e7 u7 chit khoan2 e5 tia7-chi3?몯  35) Thian-sai3 in3 i kong2: 몮Seng3 Leng5 e7 kang3-lim5 toa3 li2 e5 sin. Chi3-ko-chia2 e5 koan5-leng5 e7 ti3-im3 li2. In-ui7 an2-ne hit e5 teh-boeh chhut-si3 e5 Gin2-na2 e7 hou7 lang5 chheng-hou cho3 Seng3-chia2, 몬Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2.몭  36) Li2 khoaN3! Li2 e5 chhin-chhek I2-li7-sa-pek sui-jian5 hiah-nih8 lau7 a7, i ia7 i2-keng hoai5-in7 chit8 e5 cha-pou-kiaN2. Lang5 kong2 i be7 seN, tan7-si7 i hian7-chai7 hoai5-in7 lak8 kou2-goah8 a7.  37) In-ui7 Siong7-chu2 bo5 chit8 hang7 tai7-chi3 cho3 be7 lai5.몯  38) Ma2-li7-a kong2, 몮Goa2 si7 Chu2 e5 li2-pi7. Goan7 chiau3 li2 e5 oe7 lai5 ka7 goa2 seng5-choan5.몯 Thian-sai3 chiu7 li7-khui i.

Ma2-li7-a hong2-bun7 I2-li7-sa-pek:
	39) Keng-koe3 bo5 loa7 ku2, Ma2-li7-a chiu7 koaN2-kin2 chhut-hoat khi3-kau3 chit8 e5 Iu5-thai3 soaN-te7 e5 siaN5-chhi7.  40) I jip8-khi3 Sat-ka-li7-a e5 chhu3, chiu7 ka7 I2-li7-sa-pek chheng2-an.  41) I-li7-sa-pek chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 Ma2-li7-a e5 chheng2-an, thai-ji5 chiu7 chai7 i e5 pak-tou2 lai7 tio5-thiau3. I2-li7-sa-pek ia7 chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5.  42) I chiu7 toa7-siaN kong2: 몮Hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, li2 si7 siong7 u7 hok-khi3 e5! Li2 e5 thai-ji5 ia7-si7 siong7 u7 hok-khi3 e5!  43) Goa2 na7 e7 kham-tit hou7 goa2 e5 Chu2 e5 bo2-chhin lai5 hong2-bun7 goa2?  44) In-ui7 goa2 chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 li2 chheng2-an e5 siaN, goa2 e5 thai-ji5 chiu7 hoaN-hi2 tio5-thiau3.  45) Li2 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3! In-ui7 li2 u7 sin3 Chu2 ka7 li2 kong2 e5 oe7 it-teng7 e7 seng5-chiu7!몯

Ma2-li7-a e5 chan3-bi2-si:
46) Ma2-li7-a2 kong2:
몮Goa2 e5 sim-leng5 chan3-iong5 Chu2,
47) Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 ui7 Sion7-chu2 goa3 e5 Kiu3-chu2 lai5 toa7 hoaN-hi2.
48) In-ui7 Chu2 i2-keng u7 khoaN3-kou3 tioh8 I pi-chian7 e5 li2-pi7. I2-au7, se3-se3 tai7-tai7 e5 lang5, long2 e7 chheng-hou goa2 si7 u7 hok-khi3 e5!
49) In-ui7 Choan5-leng5-chia2 i2-keng ui7 goa2 cho3-chhut ui2-tai7 e5 su7. I e5 mia5 si7 몬Seng3 e5몭!
50) I e5 lin5-bin2, se3-se3 tai7-tai7 siuN2-su3 hou7 keng3-ui3 I e5 lang5.
51) I e5 chhiu2 hian2-chhut tai7-leng5, khu-tiok8 lai7-sim kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5.
52) I chiong thong2-ti7-chia2 tui3 ong5-ui7 thoa loh8-lai5, chiong pi-bi5 e5 lang5 the5-seng.
53) I eng7 ho2-mih8 hou7 iau-go7 e5 lang5 chiah8 kah pa2, koaN2 hu3-ju7 e5 lang5 khang-chhiu2 chhut-khi3.
54) Chiau3 I tui3 lan2 e5 chou2-sian sou2 eng3-un2 e5, I lai5 kiu3-chou7 I e5 pok8-jin5 I2-sek-liat8,
55) E7-ki3-tit siuN2-su3 jin5-chu5 hou7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kap I it-chhe3 e5 kiaN2-sun, kau3 ban7-se3 ban7-tai7.몯
56) Ma2-li7-a kap I2-li7-sa-pek cho3-hoe2 toa3 chha-put-to saN goeh8-jit8, chiah tng2-khi3 in chhu3.

Si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 e5 tan3-seng:
	57) I2-li7-sa-pek i2-keng kau3-goeh8, chiu7 seN chit8 e5 hau7-seN.  58) I e5 chhu3-piN kap chhin-chhek chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 kong2 Chu2 siuN2-su3 i toa7 jin5-chu5, chiu7 kap i cho3-hoe2 hoaN-hi2.
	59) EN-a2 chhut-si3 chit8 le2-pai3 liau2-au7, in lai5 ka7 i si-heng5 kat-le2, ia7 boeh chiau3 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 mia5 ka7 i ho7-cho3 Sat-ka-li7-a.  60) Tan7-si7 i e5 lau7-bo2 kong2, 몮M7-thang an2-ne! I e5 mia5 tioh8 ho7-cho3 Iok-han7.몯  61) In chiu7 tui3 i kong2, 몮Li2 e5 chhin-chhek tiong bo5 lang5 ho7 chit e5 mia5.몯  62) In chiu7 eng7 chhiu2 pi2, lai5 mng7 Sat-ka-li7-a, khoaN3 i boeh ka7 i e5 kiaN2 ho7 sim2-mih mia5.  63) Sat-ka-li7-a chiu7 tho2 chit8 te3 sia2-ji7-pang, sia2 kong2, 몮I e5 mia5 si7 Iok-han7.몯 Tai7-ke long2 chin tioh8-kiaN.  64) Hit e5 si5 Sat-ka-li7-a sui5-si5 koh-chai3 e7 kong2-oe7, khai-si2 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2.  65) Chhu3-piN e5 lang5 long2 toa7 tioh8-kiaN, choan5 Iu5-thai3 e5 soaN-te7 long2 si7 teh hoe7 chit chan5 tai7-chi3.  66) ThiaN-kiN3 chit chan5 tai7-chi3 e5 lang5, long2 ti7 sim-lai7 teh siuN7 kong2, 몮Chit e5 eN-a2 chiong-lai5 e7 cho3 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 lang5?몯 In-ui7 beng5-beng5 u7 Chu2 e7 tai7-leng5 kap i tong5-chai7.

Sat-ka-li7-a e5 i7-gian5:
	67) I e5 lau7-pe7 Sat-ka-li7-a chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5, chiu7 i7-gian5 kong2:
68) 몮Tioh8 chan3-bi2 Chu2, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-chu2!
In-ui7 I lai5 kiu3-siok8 I e5 peh-seN3, hou7 in tit-tioh8 chu7-iu5.
69) Tui3 I e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8-ke, ka7 lan2 lip8 chit8 ui7 tai7-leng5 e5 Kiu3-chu2.
70) Chiau3 I kou2-cha2 chioh I sin5-seng3 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 chhui3 sou2 eng3-un2 kong2:
71) I boeh kiu3 lan2 thoat-li7 lan2 e5 tek8-jin5, hou7 lan2 thoat-li7 oan3-hun7 lan2 e5 lang5 e5 koan5-se3.
72) I eng3-un2 boeh siuN2-su3 jin5-chu5 hou7 lan2 e5 chou2-sian, e7-ki3-tit I sou2 lip8 e5 sin5-seng3 e5 beng5-iok.
73) Che chiu7-si7 I tui3 lan2 e5 chou2-sian A-pek-lah8-han2 sou2 lip8 e5 se3-iok.
74) I boeh kiu3 lan2 thoat-li7 tek8-jin5 e5 koan5-se3, hou7 lan2 bo5-kiaN-bo5-hiaN5,
75) E7-tang3 it-seng toa3 I e5 bin7-cheng5, eng7 seng3-kiat kap kong-gi7 lai5 su7-hong7 I.
76) goa2 e5 kiaN2 a3, Li2 e7 hou7 lang5 chheng-hou7 cho3 몬Chi3-ko Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5몭,
in-ui7 li2 e7 cho3 Chu2 e5 sian-hong, lai5 chun2-pi7 I e5 to7-lou7,
77) Hou7 I e5 chu2-bin5 chai-iaN2 Siong7-chu2 sia3-bian2 in e5 choe7, lai5 hou7 in tit-tioh8 chin2-kiu3.
78) Lan2 e5 Siong7-chu2 chhiong-moa2 chu5-pi. I e7 tui3 thiN-teng2 hou7 chin2-kiu3 e5 jit8 lai5 chio3 lan2,
79) Lai5 chio3 hiah-e5 toa3 ti7 ou-am3 kap si2-bong5 e5 ou-iaN2 tiong e5 lang5, in2-chhoa7 lan2 e5 kha kiaN5 jip8-khi3 peng5-an e5 lou7.몯
	80) Chit e5 gin2-na2 tiong2-seng5 khi2-lai5, sim-leng5 chap8-hun hoat-tat8. I toa3 khong3-ia2, it-tit8 toa3 kau3 chai7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 kong-khai chhut-hian7 hit chit8 jit8.

Te7 2 ChiuN

Ia5-sou e5 tan3-seng: (Ma2 1:18-25)
	1) Hit e5 si5, Hong5-te3 A-kou2-su7-tok hoat-chhut beng7-leng7, kio3 choan5 Lo5-ma2 te3-kok e5 jin5-bin5 long2 tioh8 teng-ki3 hou7-khau2.  2) Chit e5 thau5 chit8 pai2 e5 hou7-khau2 tiau-cha, si7 Ku-li2-liu2 cho3 Su7-li7-a chong2-tok e5 si5 sit8-si e5.  3) Sou2-i2 cheng3-lang5 chiu7 long2 tng2-khi3 in ka-ti7 e5 kou3-hiong teng-ki3 hou7 khau2.
	4) Iok-sek tui3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 e5 Na2-sat-lek8-siaN5 khi3-kau3 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 Pek-li7-heng5-siaN5, chiu7-si7 Tai7-pit8 chhut-si3 e5 siaN5-chhi7. Iok-sek khi3 hia teng-ki3, in-ui7 i si7 Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun.  5) Iok-sek kap i e5 bi7-hun-chhe Ma2-li7-a cho3-hoe2 khi3 teng-ki3. Hit e5 si5, Ma2-li7-a i2-keng u7 sin-in7 a7.  6) In toa3 ti7 Pek-li7-heng5 e5 si5, Ma2-li7-a i2-keng kau3-goeh8 a7.  7) chiu7 seN thau5-the e5 cha-pou-kiaN2. Ma2-li7-a eng7 pou3 ka7 I pau khi2-lai5, ka7 I khng3 toa3 be2-cho5 lai7; in-ui7 li2-koan2 bo5 sou2-chai7 thang hou7 in toa3.

Bok8-tong5 kap thian-sai3:
	8) Hit e5 te7-hng u7 chit8-koa2 bok8-tong5 ti7 ia2-goa7 keh-me5, lun5-liu5 teh khoaN3-kou3 in e5 iuN5-kun5.  9) U7 chit8 ui7 Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 chhut-hian7 hou7 in khoaN3, Chu2 e5 kong-iau7 chio3 in e5 si3-piN. In chiu7 toa7 tioh8-kiaN.  10) Hit ui7 thian-sai3 ka7 in kong2: 몮M7-bian2 kiaN! Goa2 lai5 boeh ka7 lin2 po3 chit8 e5 toa7 hoaN-hi2 e5 ho2 siau-sit, si7 boeh hou7 ban7-bin5 e5 ho2 siau-sit.  11) Kin-na2-jit8 ti7 Tai7-pit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7, i2-keng u7 chit8 ui7 Kiu3-chu2 ui7 lin2 tan3-seng a. I chiu7-si7 chu2 Ki-tok!  12) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2 chit8 e5 ki3-jin7; lin2 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 EN-a2, eng7 pou3 pau le, to2 ti7 be2-cho5 lai7.몯
	13) Hut-jian5-kan u7 chit8 toa7 tin7 e5 thian-kun kap hit ui7 thian-sai3, tang5-che5 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, kong2:
14) 몮chai7 chi3-ko chi thian, eng5-iau7 kui Siong7-chu2!
Chai7 te7-siong7 peng5-an kui I sou2 keng2-soan2 e5 lang5!몯
	15) chiah-e5 thian-sai3 li7-khui in, tng2-khi3 thiN-teng2 liau2-au7, bok8-tong5 chiu7 hou7-siong kong2, 몮Lan2 lai5-khi3 Pek-li7-heng5 khoaN3 Chu2 ka7 lan2 kong2 chit hang7 i2-keng hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3.몯  16) In chiu7 koaN2-kin2 khi3, chhoe7-tioh8 Ma2-li7-a kap Iok-sek, i2-kip8 to2 ti7 be2-cho5 lai7 hit e5 Ang-eN-a2.  17) Bok8-tong5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 EN-a2, chiu7 chiong thian-sai3 sou2 kong2 koan-he7 chit e5 EN-a2 tai7-chi3,  siong5-se3 kong2 hou7 in thiaN.  18) ThiaN-tioh8 bok8-tong5 kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 e5 lang5, tai7-ke long2 tioh8-kiaN.  19) Tan7-si7 Ma2-li7-a chiong chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 long2 khng3 toa3 sim-lai7, put-si5 teh siuN7-khi2 chit e5 tai7-chi3.  20) Bok8-tong5 chiu7 tng2-khi3, na2 kiaN5 na2 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, in-ui7 in sou2 thiaN-kiN3, sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 it-chhe3 tu2 kap thian-sai3 sou2 kong2 e5 oan5-choan5 kang7-khoan2.

Ka7 몮Ia5-sou몯 ho7-mia5:
	21) Kau3 te7-peh jit8, ka7 EN-a2 si-heng5 kat-le2 e5 si5 kau3 a3, chiu7 ka7 I ho7-cho3 Ia5-sou. Chit e5 mia5 si7 Ma2-li7-a iau2-boe7 hoai5-in7 i2-cheng5, thian-sai3 ka7 I ho7 e5.

Pho7 Ia5-sou khi3 Seng3-tian7 hong7-hian3:
	22) Chiiau3 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat, ki2-heng5 kiat-cheng7-le2 e5 jit8 chit8-e7 kau3, Ma2-li7-a kap Iok-sek chiu7 pho7 EN-a2 khi3-kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, boeh chiong I hian3 hou7 Siong7-chu2.  23) In-ui7 chiau3 Chu2 e5 Lut8-hoat: 몮Mui2 chit8 e5 thau5 chit8 the e5 cha-pou-kiaN2, long2 tioh8 hong7-hian3 hou7 Chu2.몯  24) In ia7 chiau3 Chu2 e5 Lut8-hoat sou2 kui-teng7 hian3 몮Chit8 tui3 pan-kah a2-si7 nng7 chiah hun2-chiau2-a2 kiaN2몯 cho3 seng-le2.
	25) Ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 mia5 kio3-cho3 Se-bian7. chit e5 lang5 si7 gi7-jin5, ia7-si7 khian5-seng5 e5 lang5. I put-si5 teh ki5-thai7 I2-sek-liat8 bin5-chok8 e5 hok8-heng. Seng3 Leng5 ia7 kap i tong5-chai7.  26) Seng3 Leng5 u7 khe2-si7 hou7 i chai-iaN2 i iau2-boe7 si2 i2-cheng5, it-teng7 e7 khoaN3-tioh8 Chu2 sou2 eng3-un2 e5 Bi2-sai3-a.  27) Seng3 Leng5 in2-chhoa7 Se-bian7 jip8-khi3 Seng3-tian7. Hit e5 si5, EN-a2 Ia5-sou e5 pe7-bo2 ia7 pho7 I jip8-khi3 Seng3-tian7, boeh ka7 I ki2-heng5 Lut8-hoat sou2 kui-teng7 e5 gi5-sek.  28) Se-bian7 eng7 siang chhiu2 pho7 hit e5 EN-a2, chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2 kong2:
29) 몮Choan5-leng5 e5 Chu2 a3, Li2 sou2 eng3-un2 e5 oe7, i2-keng eng3-giam7 aTaN7 hou7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 peng5-peng5 an-an li7-khui se3-kan.
30) In-ui7 goa2 i2-keng chhin-bak8 khoaN3-tioh8 Li2 e5 chin2-kiu3.
31) Che si7 Li2 ui7-tioh8 ban7-bin5 sou2 chun2-pi7 e5,
32) Si7 boeh khe2-si7 goa7-pang-lang5 e5 kng, Si7 Li2 e5 chu2-bin5 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 kong-eng5.몯
	33) Ia5-sou e5 pe7-bo2 thiaN-kiN3 Se-bian7 kong2 hoan-he7 EN-a2 chiah-e5 oe7, chin tioh8-kiaN.  34-35) Se-bian7 ka7 in chiok-hok, ia7 tui3 I e5 lau7-bo2 Ma2-li7-a kong2:
몮Chit e5 EN-a2 chu3-tiaN7 tioh8 chiaN5-cho3 hou7 cheng3-lang5 khi3-choat8 e5 ki3-ho7. Li2 e5 sim ia7 e7 chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 lai7-kiam3 chhak8 thau3-koe3. chin-che7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e7 in-ui7 I lai5 tit-kiu3 a2-si7 biat8-bong5, an2-ne lai5 hou7 cheng3-lang5 sim-lai7 e5 pi3-bit8 hian2-lou7 chhut-lai5.몯
	36) Ia7 u7 chit8 ui7 cha-bou2 tai7-gian5-jin5, kio3-cho3 A-na2. I siok8 A-siat e5 chi-phai3, si7 Hoat-loe7-lek8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2. I si7 chit8 e5 lau7 hu7-jin5-lang5. I siau3-lian5 e5 si5 chhut-ke3, kiat-hun chhit-ni5,  37) tiong7-hu chiu7 si2-khi3, jian5-au7 i chiu7 chiu2-koaN2 kau3 hian7-chai7, i2-keng peh-chap8-si3 hoe3 a3. I me5-jit8 kim3-chiah8 ki5-to2, su7-hong7 Siong7-chu2, long2 bo5 li7-khui Seng3-tian7.  38) Tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5, i ia7 lai5 kam2-sia7 Siong7-chu2, tui3 hiah-e5 it-chhe3 teh ki5-thai7 Siong7-chu2 lai5 kiu3-siok8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 lang5 kong2-khi2 chit e5 EN-a2 e5 tai7-chi3.

Tng2-khi3 Na2-sat-lek8-siaN5:
	39) In oan5-seng5 Chu2 e5 Lut8-hoat sou2 kui-teng7 it-chhe3 e5 gi5-sek liau2-au7, chiu7 tng2-khi3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2, kau3 in e5 kou3-hiong Na2-sat-lek8-siaN5.  40) Chit e5 Gin2-na2 tiong2-seng5 khi2-lai5, sin-the2 kian-kiong5, chhiong-moa2 ti3-hui7. Siong7-chu2 e5 in-hui7 kap i tong5-chai7.

Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou chai7 Seng3-tian7 lai7:
	41) Ia5-sou e5 pe7-bo2 tak8 ni5 to khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 koe3 PoaN5-koe3-cheh.  42) Ia5-sou chap8-ji7 hoe3 e5 si5, in chiau3 koan3-le7 khi3 koe3-cheh.  43) cheh-ki5 chit8-e7 koe3, in chhut-hoat boeh to3-tng2-khi3 chhu3-nih e5 si5, Gin2-na2 Ia-sou iau2 lau5 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2. I e5 pe7-bo2 m7 chai-iaN2 an2-ne.  44) In siuN7-cho3 I si7 lam7 ti7 kang7 hit e5 tiau5-seng3-thoan5 e5 lai7-bin7. KiaN5 chit8 jit8 e5 lou7-cham7 liau2-au7, in chiah khi3 chhin-chhek kap sek8-sai7-lang5 hia chhoe7 I.  45) In chhoe7 bo5 Ia5-sou, chiu7 koh to3-tng2-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chhoe7 I.  46) SaN jit8 au7 in chiah ti7 Seng3-tian7 lai7 chhoe7 tioh8 I. I che7 ti7 kau3-su e5 tiong-kan na2 teh thiaN in kong2, ia7 na2 teh ka7 in mng7.  47) ThiaN-tioh8 I teh kong2-oe7 e5 lang5, chin kam2-than3 I e5 ti3-hui7 kap in3-tap.  48) I e5 pe7-bo2 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 I, ia7 chin tioh8-kiaN. I e5 lau7-bo2 tui3 I kong2: 몮KiaN2 a3! Li2 an3-choaN2 e7 cho3 chit khoan2 tai7-chi3? Li2 khoaN3, Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 kap goa2 chin hoan5-lo2, it-tit8 teh chhoe7 Li2!몯  49) Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 an3-choaN2 tioh8 chhoe7 Goa2? Lin2 kam2 m7 chai-iaN2 Goa2 tioh8-ai3 toa3 Goa2 e5 Hu7-chhin e5 chhu3?몯  50) Tan7-si7 in be7-tang3 liau2-kai2 I sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.
	51) Ia5-sou chiu7 kap in cho3-hoe2 tng2-khi3 Na2-sat-lek8-siaN5, toa3 hia hau3-sun7 in. I e5 lau7-bo2 chiong chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 long2 khng3 toa3 sim-lai7.  52) Ia5-sou lu2 toa7-han3, ti3-sek kap sin-the2 ia7 lu2 hoat-tat8, lu2 tit-tioh8 Siong7-chu2 kap lang5 e5 thiong2-ai3.

Te7 3 ChiuN

Si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 e5 thoan5-to7: (Ma2 3:1-12; Kho2 1:1-8; Iok 1:19-28)
	1) Hong5-te3 The5-pi2-liu5 che7 ui7 e5 te7 chap8-gou7 ni5, Pun2-tiu Pi2-liap8-to teh cho3 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 e5 chong2-tok, Hi-lut8 teh cho3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 hun-hong e5 ong5, i e5 sio2-ti7 Hui-lek8 teh cho3 I-thou2-li7-a kap Tek-liap8-kho2-ni5 te7-hng hun-hong e5 ong5, Lu7-sat-liap8 teh cho3 A-pi2-li7-ni5 e5 hun-hong e5 ong5,  2) A-na2 kap Kai-a-hoat teh cho3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 toa7 che3-si. Hit e5 si5 Sat-ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-han7 ti7 khong3-ia2 nia2-siu7 tioh8 Siong7-chu2 e5 oe7.  3) Iok-han7 chiu7 khi3-kau3 Iok-tan3-ho5 it-tai3 e5 kok te7-hng soan-kang2 kong2: 몮Tioh8 hoe3-kai2, tioh8 nia2-siu7 se2-le2. Siong7-chu2 it-teng7 e7 sia3-bian2 lin2 e5 choe7.몯  4) An2-ne si7 chiau3 tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-sai3-a ti7 i e5 chheh sou2 ki3-chai3, kong2:
몮Ti7 khong3-ia2 u7 lang5 teh hoah kong2:
몬Tioh8 ui7 chu2 chun2-pi7 to7-lou7,
Siu-tit I sou2 boeh kiaN5 e5 sio2-lou7!
5) It-chhe3 e5 chhim-kheN long2 tioh8 thun7 hou7 tiN7,
Sou2 u7 toa7-sio2 e5 soaN long2 tioh8 siah hou7 peN5;
Oan-oan-oat-oat e5 lou7 tioh8 siu hou7 tit8,
KHam-kham-khiat8-khiat8 e5 lou7 tioh8 siu hou7 peN5.
6) Ban7-bin5 long2 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-chu2 e5 chin2-kiu3.몭몯
	7) Iok-han7 tui3 hiah-e5 lai5 boeh tui3 i nia2-siu7 se2-le2 e5 kun5-chiong3 kong2: 몮Lin2 chiah-e5 tok8-choa5 a3! Sim2-mih lang5 keng2-ko3 lin2 siam2-pi7 Siong7-chu2 teh-boeh hoat e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 a3?  8) TaN lin2 tioh8 eng7 lin2 e5 seng-oah8 lai5 cheng3-beng5 lin2 chin-chiaN3 u7 hoe3-kai2! M7-thang ka-ti7 siuN7 kong2, 몬a-pek-lah8-han2 si7 goan2 chou2-sian.몭 goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, Siong7-chu2 e7-tang3 tui3 chiah-e5 chioh8-thau5 lai5 seN-chhut A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kiaN2-sun.  9) Pou2-thau5 i2-keng tui3-chun2 chhiu7-thau5 a7. Na7 bo5 kiat ho2 koe2-chi2 e5, long2 e7 chho3 khi2-lai5 hiat loh8-khi3 hoe2-nih.몯
	10) Cheng3-lang5 mng7 Iok-han7 kong2, 몮Na7-si7 an2-ne, goan2 tioh8 an3-choaN2 cho3 chiah ho2?몯  11) I in3 in kong2, 몮Na7 u7 nng7 nia2 saN e5 lang5, tioh8 pun chit8 nia2 hou7 bo5 saN thang chheng7 e5 lang5; na7 u7 chiah8-mih8 e5 lang5, ia7 tioh8 an2-ne pun hou7 bo5 thang chiah8 e5 lang5.몯  12) U7 chit8-koa2 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 ia7 lai5 boeh nia2-siu7 se2-le2, In mng7 Iok-han7 kong2, 몮Lau7-su, goan2 tioh8 an3-choaN2 cho3 chiah ho2?몯  13) I chiu7 ka7 in kong2, 몮Kui-teng7 i2-goa7 e5 soe3-kim, m7-thang ka7 lang5 thiu.몯  14) U7 chit8-koa2 kun-jin5 ia7 mng7 i kong2, 몮Goan2 tioh8 an3-choaN2 cho3 chiah ho2?몯 I chiu7 ka7 in kong2, 몮M7-thang ka7 lang5 khiong2-hat; m7-thang ka7 lang5 kha3-iu5; tui3 lin2 sou2 nia2 e5 sin-sui2 tioh8-ai3 ti-chiok.몯
15) Cheng3-lang5 chin jiat8-chhiat teh ki5-thai7 Bi2-sai3-a, sou2-i2 ti7 sim-lai7 long2 teh siuN7 kong2 Iok-han7 bo5 tiaN7-tioh8 si7 Bi2-sai3-a.  16) Iok-han7 chiu7 tui3 in cheng3-lang5 kong2: 몮goa2 eng7 chui2 ka7 lin2 se2-le2; tan7-si7 u7 chit8 ui7 pi2 goa2 khah u7 koan5-leng5 e5 teh-boeh lai5. Goa2 lian5 thau2 I e5 e5-toa3 ia7 be7 kham-tit. I e7 eng7 Seng3 Leng5 kap hoe2 ka7 lin2 se2-le2.  17) I chhiu2-nih theh chhiah-ki, boeh chiong tiu7-tiaN5 long2 put hou7 chheng-khi3. I e7 siu7 chhek-a2 jip8-khi3 I e5 chhek-chhng, eng7 be7 hoa-khi3 e5 hoe2 chiong chhau2-khou3 sio-tiau7.몯
18) Iok-han7 teh thoan5 Hok-im e5 si5, eng7 chin-che7 bo5 kang7-khoan2 e5 kong2-hoat lai5 khou2-khng3 cheng3-lang5.  19) Tan7-si7 Iok-han7 chek-pi7 hun-hong e5 ong5 Hi-lut8, in-ui7 i chhoa7 in sio2-ti7 e5 bou2 Hi-lo5-ti2 lai5 cho3 bou2. Ki5-tha ia7 u7 cho3 chin-che7 phaiN2 tai7-chi3.  20) TaN Hi-lut8 iu7-koh ke cho3 chit8 hang7 koh-khah phaiN2 e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7-si7 chiong Iok-han7 koaiN loh8 kaN-gak8.

Ia5-sou siu7 se2-le2: (Ma2 3:13-17; Kho2 1:9-11)
21) Cheng3-lang5 nia2-siu7 se2-le2 liau2-au7, Ia5-sou ia7 nia2-siu7 se2-le2. I teh ki5-to2 e5 si5, thiN chiu7 khui.  22) Seng3 Leng5 chiu7 hian2-sin chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 chiah hun2-chiau2, kang3 loh8-lai5 hioh toa3 I e5 seng-khu, iu7-koh u7 siaN tui3 thiN-teng2 lai5, kong2:
몮Li2 si7 Goa2 sim-ai3 e5 KiaN2; Goa2 chin-chiaN3 kah-i3 Li2.몯

Ia5-sou e5 chok8-phou2: (Ma2 1:1-17)
	23) Ia5-sou khai-si2 thoan5-kau3 e5 si5, chha-put-to si7 saN-chap8 hoe3. Cheng3-lang5 siuN7 kong2 I si7 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2. Iok-sek si7 Hi-li2 e5 kiaN2.  24) Hi-li2 si7 Ma2-thap e5 kiaN2. Ma2-thap si7 Li7-bi7 e5 kiaN2. Li7-bi7 si7 Bek8-ki e5 kiaN2. Bek8-ki si7 Nga2-na2 e5 kiaN2. Nga2-na2 si7 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2.  25) Iok-sek si7 Ma2-tai7-the5-a e5 kiaN2. Ma2-tai7-the5-a si7 A-mou5-su7 e5 kiaN2. A-mou5-su7 si7 Na2-ong e5 kiaN2. Na2-ong si7 I2-sul7i e5 kiaN2. I2-su7-li2 si7 Na2-kai e5 kiaN2.  26) Na2-kai si7 Ma2-ap e5 kiaN2. Ma2-ap si7 Ma2-tai7-the5-a e5 kiaN2. Ma2-tai7-the5-a si7 Se-bi2 e5 kiaN2. Se-bi2 si7 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2. Iok-sek si7 Iu5-tai7 e5 kiaN2.  27) Iu5-tai7 si7 Iok-a-na2 e5 kiaN2. Iok-a-na2 si7 Li7-sat e5 kiaN2. Li7-sat si7 Sou2-lo5-pa-pek e5 kiaN2. Sou2-lo5-pa-pek si7 Sat-liap8-thiat e5 kiaN2. Sat--liap8-thiat si7 Ni5-li7 e5 kiaN2.  28) Ni5-li7 si7 Bek8-ki e5 kiaN2. Bek8-ki si7 A-ti2 e5 kiaN2. A-ti2 si7 Ko-song e5 kiaN2. Ko-song si7 I2-mou5-tong5 e5 kiaN2. I2-mou5-tong5 si7 JiN2 e5 kiaN2.  29) JiN2 si7 Iok-se3 e5 kiaN2. Iok-se3 si7 I2-liat8-sat e5 kiaN2. I2-liat8-sat si7 Iok-leng7 e5 kiaN2. Iok-leng7 si7 Ma2-thap e5 kiaN2. Ma2-thap si7 Li7-bi7 e5 kiaN2.  30) Li7-bi7 si7 Se-bian7 e5 kiaN2. Se-bian7 si7 Iu5-tai7 e5 kiaN2. Iu5-tai7 si7 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2. Iok-sek si7 Iok-lam5 e5 kiaN2. Iok-lam5 si7 I2-li7-a-kim e5 kiaN2.  31) I2-li7-a-kim si7 Bi2-li7-a e5 kiaN2. Bi2-li7-a si7 Mai2-lam5 e5 kiaN2. Mai2-lam5 si7 Ma2-tat8-thaN e5 kiaN2. Ma2-tat8-thaN si7 Na2-tan e5 kiaN2. Na2-tan si7 Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2.  32) Tai-pit8 si7 Ia5-se e5 kiaN2. Ia5-se si7 O-pek e5 kiaN2. O-pek si7 Pho-su7 e5 kiaN2. Pho-su7 si7 Sat-bun5 e5 kiaN2. Sat-bun5 si7 Na2-sun7 e5 kiaN2.  33) Na2-sun7 si7 A-bi2-na2-tat8 e5 kiaN2. A-bi2-na2-tat8 si7 A-lan5 e5 kiaN2. A-lan5 si7 A-ni e5 kiaN2. A-ni si7 I2-su7-lun5 e5 kiaN2. I2-su7-lun5 si7 Hoat-lek8-su7 e5 kiaN2. Hoat-lek8-su7 si7 Iu5-tai7 e5 kiaN2.  34) Iu5-tai7 si7 Nga2-kok e5 kiaN2. Nga2-kok si7 I2-sat e5 kiaN2. I2-sat si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kiaN2. a-pek-lah8-han2 si7 ThaN-lah8 e5 kiaN2. ThaN-lah8 si7 Na2-hok8 e5 kiaN2.  35) Na2-hok8 si7 Sat-lok8 e5 kiaN2. Sat-loh8 si7 Liap8-kou2 e5 kiaN2. Liap8-kou2 si7 Hoat-lek8 e5 kiaN2. Hoat-lek8 si7 Hi-pek e5 kiaN2. Hi-pek si7 Sat-liap8 e5 kiaN2.  36) Sat-liap8 si7 Kai-lam5 e5 kiaN2. Kai-lam5 si7 A-hoat-sat e5 kiaN2. A-hoat-sat si7 siam2 e5 kiaN2. Siam2 si7 Na2-a e5 kiaN2. Na2-a si7 Lah8-bek e5 kiaN2.  37) Lah8-bek8 si7 Ma2-thou2-sat-lah8 e5 kiaN2. Ma2-thou2-sat-lah8 si7 I2-lok8 e5 kiaN2. I2-lok8 si7 Nga2-liat8 e5 kiaN2. Nga2-liat8 si7 Ma2-lek8-liat8 e5 kiaN2. Ma2-lek8-liat8 si7 Kai-lam5 e5 kiaN2.  38) Kai-lam5 si7 I2-na2-su7 e5 kiaN2. I2-na2-su7 si7 Siat e5 kiaN2. siat si7 A-tong e5 kiaN2. A-tong si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 kiaN2.

Te7 4 ChiuN

Ia5-sou siu7 chhi3-tham3: (Ma2 4:1-11; Kho2 1:12-13)
	1) Ia5-sou chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5, tui3 Iok-tan3-ho5 tng2-lai5. Seng3 Leng5 chhoa7 I jip8-khi3 khong3-ia2.  2) ti7 hia si3-chap8 jit8 ku2, siu7 Mou5-kui2 e5 chhi3-tham3. Hit e5 tiong-kan I long2 bo5 chiah8 sim2-mih. Hiah-e5 jit8-chi2 koe3 liau2-au7, I chiu7 pak-tou2 iau.
	3) Mou5-kui2 chiu7 tui3 I kong2, 몮Li2 na7-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2, beng7-leng7 chit liap8 chioh8-thau5 pian3-cho3 mi7-pau.몯  4) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, 몮Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, 몬Lang5 m7-si7 kan-taN oa2-kho3 mi7-pau lai5 oah8.몭몯
	5) Jian5-au7 Mou5-kui2 chiu7 chhoa7 Ia5-sou khit-khi3 chin koan5 e5 sou2-chai7. chit8 bak8-nih-a2 e5 tiong-kan chiong se3-kai3 ban7-kok po3 I khoaN3.  6) I ka7 Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Chiah-e5 ban7-kok it-chhe3 e5 koan5-se3 kap eng5-hoa5, goa2 long2 boeh hou7 Li2; in-ui7 che it-chhe3 i2-keng long2 kau ti7 goa2 e5 chhiu2-thau5 a7. chhut-chai7 goa2 khoaN3 boeh kau hou7 sim2-mih lang5.  7) sou2-i2 Li2 na7 kui7 loh8-khi3 pai3 goa2, chiah-e5 it-chhe3 long2 boeh hou7 Li2.몯  8) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, 몮Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, 몬Li2 tioh8-ai3 keng3-pai3 Chu2, li2 e5 Siong7-chu2, chi2-u7 tioh8 su7-hong7 I.몭몯
	9) Choe3-au7 Mou5-kui2 koh chhoa7 Ia5-sou khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5, hou7 I khia7 toa3 Seng3-tian7 siong7 koan5 e5 sou2-chai7, ka7 I kong2: 몮Li2 na7-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2, tui3 chia thiau3 loh8-khi3.  10) In-ui7 Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, 몬Siong7-chu2 e7 beng7-leng7 I e5 thian-sai3 lai5 po2-hou7 Li2.몭  11) Iu7-koh kong2, 몬In e7 eng7 chhiu2 ka7 Li2 hu5 le7, hou7 Li2 e5 kha be7 khi3 pong7-tioh8 chioh8-thau5.몭몯  12) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2: 몮Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2,몭Li2 m7-thang chhi3-tham3 Chu2, li2 e5 Siong7-chu2.몭몯  13) Mou5-kui2 eng7 chin7 sou2 u7 e5 ke3-ti3 chhi3-tham3 Ia5-sou liau2-au7, chiu7 li7-khui Ia5-sou, lai5 siong3 leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 ki-hoe7.

Ia5-sou chai7 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 khai-si2 thoan5-kau3: (Ma2 4:12-17; Kho2 1:14-15)
	14) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5 e5 koan5-leng5, tng2-khi3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2. I e5 mia5-siaN chiu7 thoan5 khi3-kau3 si3-ui5 e5 kok te7-hng.  15) I toa3 kok sou2-chai7 e5 hoe7-tng5 kau3-hun3 lang5, siu7 cheng3-lang5 e5 chheng-chan3.

Ia5-sou chai7 Na2-sat-lek8 pi7 khi3-choat8: (Ma2 13:53-58; Kho2 6:1-6)
	16) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou lai5-kau3 I ti7 hia tiong2-seng5 e5 Na2-sat-lek8-siaN5, chiau3 I e5 sip8-koan3, chai7 An-hioh-jit8 jip8-khi3 hoe7-tng5. I khia7 khi2-lai5 boeh thak8 Seng3-keng.  17) U7 lang5 theh8 chit8 kng2 tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-sai3-a e5 chheh hou7 I. I chiu7 thi2-khui, khoaN3-tioh8 chit8 e5 sou2-chai7 ki3-chai3 kong2:
18) 몮Chu2 siuN2-su3 I e5 Seng3 Leng5 hou7 Goa2. Chu2 eng7 iu5 ka7 Goa2 boah, hou7 Goa2 thang tui3 san3-chhiah-lang5 thoan5 Hok-im. I chhe-phai3 Goa2 lai5 soan-pou3: hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3-e5 tit-tioh8 sek-hong3, chheN-me5-e5 koh-chai3 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, siu7 ap-pek-e5 tit-tioh8 chu7-iu5,  19) soan-pou3 Chu2 si-in e5 ni5.몯
	20) Ia5-sou chiong hit kng2 chheh koh kng2 khi2-lai5, heng5 hou7 hoe7-tng5 e5 su-hoe7-chia2, chiu7 che7 loh8-khi3. Hoe7-tng5 lai7 e5 cheng3-lang5 long2 kim-kim teh ka7 I khoaN3.  21) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 in kong2: 몮Chit toaN7 Seng3-keng , lin2 teh thiaN Goa2 thak8 e5 tiong-kan, kin-na2-jit8 i2-keng eng3-giam7 a7.몯  22) Cheng3-lang5 long2 chin chheng-chan3 I; thiaN-kiN3 I kong2 chiah-e5 o3-biau7 e5 oe7, tai7-ke chin kam2-tong7. In kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 kam2 m7-si7 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2?몯  23) Ia5-sou chiu7 tui3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 it-teng7 e7 in2-iong7 chit8 ku3 siok8-gi2 ka7 Goa2 kong2, 몬I-seng a3, Li2 tioh8 seng i-ti7 Li2 ka-ti7.몭 Lin2 ia7 e7 tui3 Goa2 kong2, 몬Goan2 thiaN-kiN3 Li2 ti7 Ka-pek-long5 sou2 cho3 e5, Li2 ia7 tioh8 toa3 Li2 ka-ti7 e5 kou2-hiong cho3.몭몯  24) Ia5-sou koh ke3-siok8 kong2: 몮Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2: bo5 chit8 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 ti7 ka7-ti7 e5 kou3-hiong siu7 hoan-geng5.  25) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2 sit8-chai7 oe7: I2-li7-a e5 si5-tai7, khong3-han7 saN ni5 poaN3 ku2, choan5-kok tak8 sou2-chai7 toa7 ki-hng, hit e5 si5 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 tiong-kan u7 chin-che7 koaN2-hu7.  26) Siong7-chu2 bo5 chhe-phai3 I2-li7-a khi3 in hia, kan-taN chhe-phai3 i khi3 Se-tun3 e5 Sat-lek8-tai7 chhoe7 chit8 e5 koaN2-hu7.  27) Iu7-koh tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-li7-a e5 si5, I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 tiong-kan u7 chin-che7 ba5-hong peN7-lang5, ki-tiong bo5 kah chit8 e5 hou7 i i-ho2, chi2-u7 Su7-li7-a-lang5 Nai2-ban7 hou7 i i-ho2 nia7-nia7.몯  28) Ti7 hoe7-tng5 lai7 e5 cheng3-lang5 chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7, long2 troa7 siu7-khi3;  29) in chiu7 khia7 khi2-lai5 ka7 I koaN2 chhut-khi3 siaN5-goa7, thoa I khi3-kau3 chit8 e5 soaN-kham3, boeh ka7 I chhia loh8-khi3 kham3-kha, in-ui7 in e5 siaN5-chhi7 si7 kian3-siat ti7 chit8 e5 soaN-teng2.  30) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou tui3 in e5 tiong-kan tit8-tit8 kiaN5-koe3, cho3 I khi3.

I-ho2 tioh8-iau e5 lang5: (Kho2 1:21-28)
	31) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou loh8-khi3 Ka-pek-long5-siaN5, si7 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 e5 chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7, An-hioh-jit8 toa3 hia ka3-si7 lang5.  32) Cheng3-lang5 thiaN-tioh8 I e5 ka3-si7 long2 chin kam2-tong7, in-ui7 I kong2 e5 oe7 chin u7 koan5-ui.  33) Hit e5 si5, ti7 hoe7-tng5 lai7 tu2 u7 chit8 e5 tioh8-iau e5 lang5, toa7 siaN hoah kong2:  34) 몮Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou, Li2 ho5-pit lai5 kan-siap8 goan2? Li2 lai5 boeh hui2-biat8 goan2 si7 bo5? Goa2 chai-iaN2 Li2 si7 sim2-mih lang5; Li2 si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Seng3-chia2!몯  35) Ia5-sou chek-pi7 iau-mou5 kong2: 몮Tiam7-khi3! Tui3 chit e5 lang5 chhut-khi3!몯 Iau-mou5 ka7 hit e5 lang5 siak-to2 toa3 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, chiu7 tui3 hit e5 lang5 chhut-khi3, long2 bo5 ka7 i siong-hai7 tioh8.  36) Cheng3-lang5 long2 tioh8-kiaN, hou7-siong kong2: 몮An3-choaN2 I chit ku3 oe7 chiah li7-hai7! I eng7 koan5-ui kap leng5-lek8 chit8-e7 beng7-leng7 sia5-mou5, sia5-mou5 chiu7 chhut-khi3.몯  37) An2-ne Ia5-sou e5 mia5-siaN chiu7 thoan5 khi3-kau3 chiu-ui5 e5 kok te7-hng.

Ia5-sou i-ho2 chin-che7 peN7-lang5: (Ma2 8:14-17; Kho2 1:29-34)
	38) Ia5-sou li7-khui hit e5 hoe7-tng5, chiu7 jip8-khi3 Se-bun5 e5 chhu3-nih. Se-bun5 e5 tiuN7-m2 hoat-jiat8, chin sio; u7 lang5 chiong chit e5 tai7-chi3 lai5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2.  39) Ia5-sou khia7 oa2-khi3, aN3 loh8-khi3 beng7-leng7 jiat8 the3, jiat8 chiu7 the3-khi3; hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chek-si5 khi2-lai5 khai-si2 chiap-thai7 in.
	40) Jit8 loh8 liau2-au7, cheng3-lang5 chhoa7 in kok-chiong2 e5 peN7-lang5 lai5 chhoe7 Ia5-sou. Ia5-sou eng7 chhiu2 chit8-e5 chit8-e5 ka7 in bong, long2 ka7 in i ho2-khi3.  41) Ia7 u7 sia5-mou5 tui3 chin-che7 lang5 e5 seng-khu chhut-lai5, toa7 siaN hoah kong2, 몮Li2 si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2!몯 in-ui7 chiah-e5 sia5-mou5 chai-iaN2 I si7 bi2-sai3-a, sou2-i2 Ia5-sou ka7 in chek-pi7, ia7 m7 chun2 in kong2.

Ia5-sou chai7 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 thoan5-to7: (Kho2 1:35-39)
	42) ThiN chit8-e7 kng, Ia5-sou chiu7 li7-khui hit e5 siaN5-chhi7, khi3-kau3 chit8 e5 phian-phiah e5 sou2-chai7. Cheng3-lang5 chiu7 si3-ke3 khi3 chhoe7 I, chhoe7-tioh8 Ia5-sou chiu7 it-tit8 ka7 I lau5, chhiaN2 I m7-thang li7-khui in.  43) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2, 몮Goa2 ia7 tioh8 khi3 pat8 e5 siaN5-chhi7 thoan5 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 Hok-im, in-ui7 che chiu7-si7 Siong7-chu2 chhe-phai3 Goa2 lai5 e5 bok8-tek.몯  44) I chiu7 chai7 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 e5 kok hoe7-tng5 ke3-siok8 thoan5-kau3.

Te7 5 ChiuN

Ia5-sou keng2-tiau3 te7-it phe e5 bun5-tou5: (Ma2 4:18-22; Kho2 1:16-20)
1) U7 chit8 pai2, Ia5-sou khia7 ti7 Kek-ni5-sat-lek8 ou5-piN e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 kheh oa2-khi3 Ia5-sou hia, boeh thiaN I kong2 Siong7-chu2 e5 to7-li2.  2) I khoaN3-kiN3 nng7 chiah chun5-a2 kho3 ti7 hoaN7-nih8. Hiah-e5 hi5-hu li7-khui chun5 teh se2 bang7.  3) Ia5-sou peh khit-khi3 hit tiong-kan e5 chit8 chiah chun5 (chiu7-si7 Se-bun5 e5 chun5), kio3 Se-bun5 ko3 chhut-khi3 li7-khui hoaN7 bo5 loa7 hng7 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7 che7 toa3 chun5-lai5 ka3-si7 kun5-chiong3.
	4) Ia5-sou chit8-e7 kong2 soah, chiu7 ka7 Se-bun5 kong2, 몮Ko3 chhut-khi3 kau3 khah chhim e5 sou2-chai7, pha-bang7 loh8-khi3 liah8-hi5.몯  5) Se-bun5 in3 I kong2: 몮Lau7-su a3, goan2 i2-keng lo5-khou2 kui me5 liah8 bo5 poaN3 boe2 hi5, tan7-si7 Li2 kah-si7 an2-ne kong2, goa2 chiu7 lai5 pha-bang7.몯  6) In bang7 chit8-e7 pha loh8-khi3, pha tioh8 chin-che7 hi5, in e5 bang7 soah giong7 boeh phoa3-khi3.  7) In chiu7 iat8-chhiu2 kio3 iau2 chit8 chiah chun5 e5 liah8-hi5-phoaN7 lai5 ka7 in tau3-kha-chhiu2. In chiu7 lai5, nng7 chiah chun5 te2 hi5 te2 kah moa2-moa2-moa2, soah giong7-giong7 boeh tim5 loh8-khi3.  8) Se-bun5 Pi2-tek chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne, chiu7 kui7 loh8-khi3 Ia5-sou e5 kha-cheng5 kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, chhiaN2 li7-khui goa2! In-ui7 goa2 si7 choe7-jin5.몯  9) Se-bun5 kap i e5 tang5-phoaN7, in-ui7 in chit8-e7 pha-bang7 chiu7 liah8 tioh8 hiah-che7 hi5, chiu7 toa7 tioh8-kiaN;  10) Se-bun5 e5 tang5-phoaN7 Se-pi2-thai3 e5 kiaN2 Nga2-kok kap Iok-han7 ia7 toa7 tioh8-kiaN. Ia5-sou ka7 Se-bun5 kong2, 몮M7-bian2 kiaN. Tui3 hian7-chai7 khi2, li2 e7 chhin-chhiuN7 hi5-hu teh liah8-hi5 an2-ne in2-chhoa7 lang5 lai5 sin3 Siong7-chu2.몯  11) In chiu7 thoa chun5 khi2-lai5 phiaN5-teng2, pang3-sak it-chhe3, lai5 kin-toe3 Ia5-sou.

Ia5-sou i-ho2 ba5-hong-peN7 e5 lang5: (Ma2 8:1-4; Kho2 1:40-45)
	12) U7 chit8 jit8, Ia5-sou toa3 ti7 chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7 e5 si5, ti7 hia tu2 u7 chit8 e5 lang5, ba5-hong-peN7 thoaN3 kah kui seng-khu. I chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou, chiu7 phak loh8-khi3 thou5-kha, kiu5 I kong2, 몮Sin-seN a3, Li2 na7 kheng2, chiu7 e7-tang3 i-ho2 goa2 e5 peN7."몯 13) Ia5-sou chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 ka7 i bong, kong2, 몮Goa2 tong-jian5 kheng2; hou7 li2 ho2-khi3.  14) Ia5-sou hoan-hu3 i kong2: 몮M7-thang ka7 pat8-lang5 kong2 chit e5 tai7-chi3, tan7-si7 tioh8 khi3 hou7 che3-si giam7; jian5-au7 ia7 tioh8 khi3 hian3 Mou5-se sou2 kui-teng7 e5 che3-phin2, tui3 cheng3-lang5 lai5 cheng3-beng5 li2 i2-keng ho2-khi3 a3.몯  15) Ia5-sou e5 mia5-siaN lu2 thoan5 lu2 khoah, kui toa7 tin7 lang5 it-tit8 lai5 boeh thiaN I e5 kau3-hun3, ia7 boeh lai5 kiu5 I i-peN7.  16) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou tiaN7-tiaN7 ai3 the3-khi3 phian-phiah e5 sou2-chai7, toa3 hia ki5-to2.

Ia5-sou i-ho2 poan3-sui7 e5: (Ma2 9:1-8; Kho2 2:1-12)
	17) U7 chit8 jit8, Ia5-sou tu2 teh kau3-hun3 lang5 e5 si5, u7 chit8-koa2 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 kap Lut8-hoat e5 lau7-su ti7 hia teh che7. In si7 tui3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 kap Iu5-thai3 Seng2 e5 kok hiong-chhoan i2-kip8 tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5 lai5 e5. Chu2 e5 koan5-leng5 kap Ia5-sou tong5-chai7, hou7 I i-ho2 peN7-lang5.  18) Hit e5 si5, u7 chit8-koa2 lang5 eng7 chhng5-phou kng chit8 e5 poan3-sui7 e5 lai5, siuN7 boeh ka7 i kng jip8-khi3 chhu3-lai7, khng3 toa3 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-cheng5.  19) Tan7-si7 in-ui7 lang5 chin-che7, bo5 hoat-tou7 thang kng jip8-khi3; chiu7 ka7 i kng khit-khi3 chhu3-teng2, tui3 chhu3-teng2 thiah chit8 khang, chiong poan3-sui7 e5 lian5 chhng5-phou lui7 loh8-khi3 cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, khng3 toa3 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-cheng5.  20) Ia5-sou chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 in chiah-nih8 u7 sin3-sim, chiu7 ka7 paon3-sui7-e5 kong2, 몮Peng5-iu2 a3! Li2 e5 choe7 i2-keng tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2 a3.몯  21) Hiah-e5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 chiu7 khai-si2 gi7-lun7 kong2: 몮Chit e5 teh siat-tok8 Siong7-chu2 e5 lang5, kiu3-keng3 si7 sim2-mih lang5? Siong7-chu2 i2-goa7, sim2-mih lang5 e7-tang3 sia3-choe7?몯  22) Ia5-sou chai-iaN2 in teh gi7-lun7 sim2-mih, chiu7 tui3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 sim-lai7 thai2 e7 siuN7 chit khoan2 tai7-chi3?  23) Si7 kong2, 몬Li2 e5 choe7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2 a3,몭 a2-si7 kong2, 몬Li2 peh khi2-lai5 kiaN5,몭 tah chit8 hang7 khah iong5-i3?  24) Goa2 boeh hou7 lin2 chai-iaN2 Jin5-chu2 chai7 te7-siong7 u7 sia3-choe7 e5 koan5.몯 Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 chit e5 poan3-sui7-e5 kong2, 몮Goa2 ka7 li2 kong2, khi2-lai5, gia5 li2 e5 chhng5-phou, tng2-khi3 lin2 chhu3!몯  25) Hit e5 lang5 chiu7 peh khi2-lai5, toa3 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 sui5-si5 gia5 i teh to2 e5 chhng5-phou khi2-lai5, na2 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, na2 kiaN5 tng2-khi3 in chhu3.  26) Cheng3-lang5 long2 chin tioh8-kiaN, chiu7 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, sim-lai7 chhiong-moa2 keng3-ui3, kong2, 몮Goan2 kin-na2-jit8 u7 khoaN3-tioh8 hui-siong5 ki5-biau7 e5 tai7-chi3!몯

Ia5-sou keng2-tiau3 Li7-bi7: (Ma2 9:9-13; Kho2 2:13-17)
	27) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou chiu7 chhut-khi3, khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5, kio3-cho3 Li7-bi7, che7 ti7 soe3-koan teh pan7-kong. Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 i kong2, 몮Lai5 toe3 Goa2!몯  28) Li7-bi7 chiu7 peh khi2-lai5, pang3-sak it-chhe3, toe3 Ia5-sou khi3.
	29) Jian5-au7 Li7-bi7 ti7 in chhu3, khui toa7 ian3-hoe7 lai5 chhiaN2 Ia5-sou. Ti7 hia u7 chin-che7 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 kap ki5-tha e5 lang5, kap Ia5-sou cho3-hoe2 che7-toh.  30) U7 chit8-koa2 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 kap siok8 in hit phai3 e5 keng-hak8-chia2, tui3 Ia5-sou e5 bun5-tou5 phau7 put-peng5, kong2, 몮Lin2 an3-choaN2 chham thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 kap choe7-jin5 cho3-hoe2 lim-chiah8?몯  31) Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: 몮Kian7-khong e5 lang5 bo5 khiam3-eng7 i-seng, tan7-si7 u7 peN7 e5 lang5 chiah u7 su-iau3.  32) goa2 lai5 se3-kan e5 bok8-tek m7-si7 boeh keng2-tiau3 gi7-jin5, si7 boeh keng2-tiau3 choe7-jin5, lai5 hou7 in hoe3-kai2.

Koan-he7 kim3-chiah8 e5 bun7-te5: (Ma2 9:14-17; Kho2 2:18-22)
	U7 lang5 tui3 Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Iok-han7 e5 bun5-tou5 siong5-siong5 kim3-chiah8 ki5-to2. Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 bun5-tou5 ia7-si7 an2-ne; tan7-si7 Li2 e5 bun5-tou5 cho3 in chiah8 cho3 in lim.몯  34) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Chham-ka hun-ian3 e5 lang5-kheh, sin-long5 iau2 kap in cho3-hoe2 e5 si5, in kam2 e7 kim3-chiah8? Tong-jian5 be7 an2-ne.  35) Tan7-si7 sin-long5 e7 tui3 in e5 tiong-kan hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3, an2-ne in chiu7 e7 kim3-chiah8. Hit e5 si5, teh-boeh kau3 a3.몯
	36) Ia5-sou iu7-koh eng7 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7 ka7 in kong2: 몮Bo5 lang5 tui3 iau2-boe7 kiu-chui2 e5 sin saN, li3 chit8 te3 khi2-lai5 pou2 ku7 saN. Na7 an2-ne cho3, i m7-na7 kan-taN e7 li3-phoa3 hit nia2 sin saN, ji5-chhiaN2 tui3 sin saN li3 khi2-lai5 hit te3 pou3 ia7 kap ku7 saN be7 hah8.  37) Ia7 bo5 lang5 chjiong sin chiu2 te2 toa3 ku7 phoe5-te7-a2 lai7; na7 an2-ne cho3, sin chiu2 e7 hou7 ku7 phoe5-te7-a2 piak phoa3-khi3, chiu2 e7 lau5 chhut-lai5, phoe5-te7-a2 ia7 e7 sun2-hai7 khi3.  38) Sou2-i2 sin chiu2 it-teng7 tioh8 te2 toa3 sin e5 phoe5-te7-a2.  39) Lang5 na7 lim ku7-chiu2 liau2-au7, chiu7 bo5 ai3 lim sin chiu2, in-ui7 i e7 kong2, 몬Ku7 e5 chiu2 khah ho2.몭몯

Te7 6 ChiuN

Koan-he7 An-hioh-jit8 e5 bun7-te5: (Ma2 12:1-8; Kho2 2:23-28)
	1) U7 chit8 e5 An-hioh-jit8, Ia5-sou tui3 beh8-a2-hng5 keng-koe3. I e5 bun5-tou5 tiah beh8-a2-sui7, eng7 chhiu2 joe5-joe5 le3, chiu7 theh8 khi2-lai5 chiah8.  2) U7 kui2-na7 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 ka7 in kong2, 몮Lin2 an3-choaN2 cho3 An-hioh-jit8 sou2 m7 eng-kai cho3 e5 tai7-chi3?몯  3) Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 kam2 m7-bat thak8-tioh8 koan-he7 Tai7-pit8 sou2 cho3 e5 tai7-chi3?  4) I jip8-khi3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Seng3-tian7, chiah8 che3-toaN5-teng2 e5 mi7-pau, ia7 pun hou7 i e5 pou7-ha7 chiah8. chiau3 Lut8-hoat chi2-u7 che3-si chiah u7 chu-keh thang chiah8 hian3-che3 e5 mi7-pau.몯  5) Ia5-sou iu7-koh ka7 in kong2, 몮Jin5-chu2 si7 An-hioh-jit8 e5 Chu2.몯

Ia5-sou i-ho2 khoe5-chhiu2 e5: (Ma2 12:9-14; Kho2 3:1-6)
	6) Iu7-koh u7 chit8 e5 An-hioh-jit8, Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 hoe7-tng5 ka3-si7 lang5, u7 chit8 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 khoe5-chhiu2 e5 lang5 ti7 hia.  7) U7 chit8-koa2 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, teh tng-tan2 khoaN3 Ia5-sou chai7 An-hioh-jit8 u7 boeh ka7 lang5 i-ti7 a2 bo5, thang chhoe7 khang-phang7 lai5 ko3 I.  8) Ia5-sou chai-iaN2 in sim-lai7 teh siuN7 sim2-mih; chiu7 ka7 hit e5 khoe5-chhiu2 e5 lang5 kong2, 몮 Khi2-lai5, lai5 khia7 toa3 thiong-ng.몯 I chiu7 chhut-lai5 khia7 toa3 hia.  9) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou tui3 in kong2: 몮Goa2 mng7 lin2: An-hioh-jit8 cho3 ho2 tai7-chi3 a2-si7 cho3 phaiN2 tai7-chi3, kiu3 lang5 e5 seN-mia7 a2-si7 hai7-si2 lang5 e5 seN3-mia7, tah chit8 hang7 khah hap8-hoat?몯  10) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 hit e5 khoe5-chhiu2-e5 kong2, 몮Chhiu2 chhun chhut-lai5.몯 I chit8-e7 chhun chhut-khi3, chhiu2 chiu7 oan5-choan5 hok8-goan5.  11) Hiah-e5 lang5 moa2-sim toa7 siu7-khi3, hou7-siong gi7-lun7 khoaN3 boeh an3-choaN2 lai5 tui3-hu3 Ia5-sou.

Ia5-sou keng2-soan2 chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5: (Ma2 10:1-4; Kho2 3:13-19)
	12) Chha-put-to hit kui2 jit8 tiong, u7 chit8 pai2, Ia5-sou peh khit-khi3 soaN-teng2 ki5-to2, kui me5 toa3 hia ki5-kiu5 Siong7-chu2.  13) ThiN-kng e5 si5, I chiu7 kio3 I e5 bun5-tou5 lai5 I hia, tui3 in e5 tiong-kan keng2-soan2 chap8-ji7 e5, ka7 in kio3-cho3 Su3-tou5, chiu7-si7:
14) Se-bun5, (Piat8-ho7 Pi2-tek); i e5 sio2-ti7 An-tek-liat8; Nga2-kok kap Iok-han7; Hui-lek8 kap Pa-to-lo5-mai2;  15) Ma2-thai3 kap To-ma2; A-lek8-hui e5 kiaN2 Nga2-kok; Se-bun5 (i si7 Se-lo5-ti2 tong2-oan5);  16) Nga2-kok e5 kiaN2 Iu5-tai7; kap au7-lai5 chhut-be7 Ia5-sou hit e5 Ka-liok8 e5 Iu5-tai7.

Ia5-sou e5 kau3-hun3 kap i-peN7: (Ma2 4:23-25)
	17) Ia5-sou kap in tui3 soaN-teng2 cho3-hoe2 loh8-lai5 khia7 toa3 khah peN5 e5 sou2-chai7. Ti7 hia u7 chit8 toa7 tin7 I e5 bun5-tou5, ia7 u7 chin toa7 tin7 e5 bin5-chiong3. Chiah-e5 lang5 si7 tui3 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 tak8 sou2-chai7 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5 i2-kip8 Chhui-lo5, Se-tun3 it-tai3 e5 hai2-piN lai5 e5.  18) In lai5 boeh thiaN I kong2 to7-li2, ia7 boeh hou7 I i-peN7. Hiah-e5 tioh8-iau e5 lang5 ia7 long2 hou7 I i-ho2 khi3.  19) Cheng3-lang5 long2 siuN7-boeh khi3 bong I, in-ui7 u7 koan5-leng5 tui3 Ia5-sou chhut-lai5, long2 ka7 in i-ho2 khi3.

Hok-khi3 kap chai-ho7: (Ma2 5:1-12)
	20) Ia5-sou kim-kim khoaN3 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: 
몮Lin2 u7 su-iau3 Siong7-chu2 e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok si7 lin2 e5!  21) Lin2 hian7-chai7 pak-tou2 iau e5 lang5 , sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 e7 hou7 lin2 chiah8 kah pa2! Lin2 hian7-chai7 teh khau3 e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 e7 hou7 lin2 chhio3!몯
	22) 몮Ui7-tioh8 Jin5-chu2 se3-kan-lang5 lai5 oan3-hin7 lin2, khi3-choat8-lin2, bu2-jiok8 lin2, khoaN3 lin2 cho3 phaiN2-lang5 ka7 lin2 pai5-thek e5 si5, lin2 sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3!  23) Hit e5 si5, lin2 tioh8 hoaN-hi2 peh khi2-lai5 thiau3, in-ui7 ti7 thiN-teng2 u7 chin hong-hu3 e5 po3-siuN2 boeh hou7 lin2. In e5 chou2-sian ia7-si7 an2-ne lai5 tui3-thai7 tai7-gian5-jin5.몯
24) 몮Tan7-si7 lin2 ho2-giah8 e5 lang5 tioh8 u7 chai-ho7, in-ui7 lin2 i2-keng hiong2-siu7 tioh8 an-lok8 e5 seng-oah8 a7!  25) Lin2 hian7-chai7 chiah8 kah chin pa2 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7, in-ui7 au7-lai5 Siong7-chu2 e7 hou7 lin2 iau-go7! Lin2 hian7-chai7 teh chhio3 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7, in-ui7 au7-lai5 Siong7-chu2 e7 hou7 lin2 pi-siong thi5-khau3!몯
	26) 몮Cheng3-lang5 long2 teh o-lo2 lin2 e5 si5, lin2 tioh8 u7 chai-ho7, in-ui7 in e5 chou2-sian ia7 an2-ne tui3-thai7 ke2 tai7-gian5-jin5.몯

Ai3 tek8-jin5: (Ma2 5:38-48; 7:12a)
	27) 몮Lin2 chiah-e5 teh thiaN e5 lang5, taN Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: Tioh8 ai3 lin2 e5 tek8-jin5; tioh8 ho2-ho2 khoan2-thai7 oan3-hin7 lin2 e5 lang5.  28) Tioh8 chiok-hok phaiN2-chhui3 me7 lin2 e5 lang5, tioh8 ui7 gek8-thai7 lin2 e5 lang5 ki5-to2.  29) Na7 u7 lang5 sian3 li2 e5 chhui3-phe2, tioh8 koh oat8 iau2 chit8 peng5 e5 chhui3-phe2 hou7 i sian3; na7 u7 lang5 pak li2 e5 goa7-saN khi3, lian5 lai7-saN ia7 tioh8 sun7-soa3 hou7 i.  30) Na7 u7 lang5 ka7 li2 kiu5 sim2-mih, tioh8 hou7 i; na7 u7 lang5 chhiuN2 li2 e5 mih8-kiaN7 khi3, m7-thang koh ka7 i tho2.  31) Lin2 ai3 pat8-lang5 an3-choaN2 lai5 tui3-thai7 lin2, lin2 ia7 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ne lai5 tui3-thai7 pat8-lang5.몯
	32) 몮Lin2 na7 kan-taN ai3 hiah-e5 ai3 lin2 e5 lang5, an2-ne u7 sim2-mih kong-tek? In-ui7 lian5 hiah-e5 choe7-jin5, ia7 e7 ai3 hiah-e5 ai3 in e5 lang5.  33) Lin2 na7 kan-taN ho2-i3 tui3-thai7 hiah-e5 tui3 lin2 ho2 e5 lang5, an2-ne u7 sim2-mih kong-tek? In-ui7 lian5 hiah-e5 choe7-jin5 ia7-si7 an2-ne cho3.  34) Lin2 na7 kan-taN chiN5 chioh hou7 hiah-e5 e7 heng5 lin2 e5 lang5, an2-ne u7 sim2-mih kong-tek? Chioh lang5 e5 chiN5 na7 e7-tang3 long2 tho2 tng2-lai5, lian5 choe7-jin5 ia7 kaN2 chiN5 chioh hou7 choe7-jin5.  35) Tan7-si7 lin2 tioh8 ai3 lin2 e5 tek8-jin5, ho2-i3 tui3-thai7 in, chioh lang5 ia7 m7-thang siuN7 boeh tho2 tng2-lai5. An2-ne lin2 e5 po3-siuN2 chiu7 e7 chin hong-hu3. Lin2 e7 chiaN5-cho3 Chi3-ko-chia2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, in-ui7 I pun2-sin tui3 bong5-in  poe7-gi7 sia5-ok e5 lang5 chin jin5-chu5.  36) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 chhin-chhiuN7 lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 hiah-nih8 chu5-pi.몯

Phe-pheng5 pat8-lang5: (Ma2 7:1-5)
	37) 몮M7-thang phe-pheng5 pat8-lang5, lin2 chiah be7 siu7 phe-pheng5; m7-thang ka7 lang5 phoaN3 choe7, lin2 chiah be7 siu7 phoaN3 choe7. Tioh8 sia3-bian2 lang5, lin2 chiah e7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2.  38) Tioh8 hou7 lang5, lin2 chiah etit7-tioh8. Ji5-chhiaN2 e7 tit-tioh8 kah chin chhiong-chiok, ka7 lin2 chhih8 kah chat8-chat8-chat8, io5 kah tiN7-tiN7-tiN7, to3 loh8-khi3 lin2 e5 saN-a2-phe3 to3 kah moa2 chhut-lai5. Lin2 eng7 sim2-mih chhun3-chhioh niu5 hou7 lang5, ia7 e7 eng7 kang7-khoan2 e5 chhun-chhioh niu5 hou7 lin2.몯
	39) Ia5-sou iu7-koh eng7 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7 ka7 in kong2: 몮ChheN-me5-e5 be7-tang3 khan chheN-me5-e5. Na7 an2-ne cho3, nng7 e5 long2 e7 poah8 loh8-khi3 kau-a2 lai7.  40) Hak8-seng be7 pi2 lau7-su khah gau, tan7-si7 mui2 chit8 e5 hak8-seng na7 oh8 u7 khi2, chiu7 e7 kap i e5 lau7-su kang7-khoan2.몯
	41) 몮Li2 an3-choaN2 kan-taN teh khoaN3 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 bak8-chiu lai7 e5 chhau2-sap-a2, iah bo5 chu3-i3 tioh8 li2 ka-ti7 bak8-chiu lai7 e5 toa7 ki sam-a2-khou?  42) Li2 ki3-jian5 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 ka-ti7 bak8-chiu7 lai7 e5 sam-a2-khou, an3-choaN2 e7-tang3 ka7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, 몬HiaN-ti7 a3, goa2 lai5 ka7 li2 theh8 bak8-chiu lai7 e5 chhau2-sap-a2 chhut-lai5.몭 Gui7-sian7-chia2 a3! Li2 tioh8 tai7-seng chiong li2 bak8-chiu lai7 e5 toa7 ki sam-a2-khou theh8 chhut-lai5, jian5-au7 li2 chiah e7-tang3 khoaN3 kah beng5-beng5-beng5, thang theh8 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 bak8-chiu lai7 e5 chhau2-sap-a2 chhut-lai5.몯

Chhiu7 kap koe2-chi2: (Ma2 7:16-20; 12:33-35)
	43) 몮Ho2 chhiu7 be7 kiat phaiN2 koe2-chi2, phaiN2 chhiu7 ia7 be7 kiat ho2 koe2-chi2.  44) KhoaN3 koe2-chi2 chiu7 e7 chai-iaN2 hit chang5 chhiu7 e5 ho2-phaiN2. Tui3 chhi3-phe3 be7-tang3 ban2 bu5-hoa-ko2, tui3 chhi3-a2-tin5 be7-tang3 siu phu5-to5.  45) Ho2-lang5 tui3 i ka-ti7 e5 sim-lai7 sou2 chek-chun5 e5 liong5-sian7, hian2-chhut liong5-sian7; phaiN2-lang5 tui3 i ka-ti7 sou2 siu-chun5 e5 sia5-ok, lou7-chhut sia5-ok. In-ui7 lang5 sou2 kong2 chhut-lai5 e5 oe7, long2 si7 tui3 i e5 sim-lai7 thou3-lou7 chhut-lai5 e5.몯

Nng7 chiong2 e5 te7-ki: (Ma2 7:24-27)
	46) 몮Lin2 an3-choaN2 chheng-hou Goa2 kong2, 몬Chu2 a3, Chu2 a3!몭, iah m7 chiau3 Goa2 sou2 kong2 e5 khi3 cho3?  47) Goa2 boeh ka7 lin2 kong2, mui2 chit8 e5 lai5 chhoe7 Goa2, thiaN Goa2 chiah-e5 oe7, iu7-koh chiau3 an2-ne khi3 sit8-heng5 e5 lang5, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 lang5.  48) I chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 khi2-chhu3 e5 lang5; kut8 thou3-kha kut8 chin chhim, phah te7-ki toa3 chioh8-poaN5 teng2; sui-jian5 toa7-chui2 lai5, chhiong-tioh8 hit keng chhu3, tan7-si7 ia7 long2 bo5 chun3-bun7 tioh8, in-ui7 khi2-liau2 chin kian-kou3.  49) Tan7-si7 kan-taN thiaN Goa2 chiah-e5 oe7, bo5 chiau3 an2-ne khi3 sit8-heng5 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 khi2 chhu3 toa3 thou5-kha bo5 phah te7-ki; toa7-chui2 chit8-e7 chhiong-tioh8, hit keng chhu3 sui5-si5 chiu7 to2-khi3, to2 kah peN5-peN5-peN5.몯

Te7 7 ChiuN

Ia5-sou i-ho2 lian5-tiuN2 e5 lou5-pok8: (Ma2 8:5-13)
	1) Ia5-sou chiong chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3 kau3-hun3 cheng3-lang5 liau2-au7, chiu7 jip8-khi3 Ka-pek-long5-siaN5.  2) U7 chit8 e5 Lo5-ma2 e5 lian5-tiuN2, i sou2 tiong7-iong7 e5 lou5-pok8 phoa3-peN7 kah teh-boeh si2-khi3 a3.  3) I thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-sou e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 chhiaN2 kui2-na7 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 khi3 Ia5-sou hia, kiu5 Ia5-sou i-ti7 i e5 lou5-pok8.  4) Chiah-e5 tiuN2-lo2 lai5-kau3 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-cheng5, seng5-khun2 kiu5 I kong2: "몮hit e5 lang5 e7-kham-tit Li2 ka7 i pang-chan7.  5) In-ui7 i ai3-hou7 lan2 e5 peh-seN3, ia7 u7 ka7 lan2 khi2 hoe7-tng5.몯  6) Ia5-sou chiu7 kap in khi3. Ia5-sou lai5-kau3 li7 in chhu3 bo5 loa7 hng7 e5 si5, hit e5 lian5-tiuN2 chhe kui2-na7 e5 peng5-iu2 lai5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Sin-seN a3, m7-thang lo5-hoan5 Li2. Goa2 be7-kham-tit hou7 Li2 lai5-kau3 goan2 tau.  7) Goa2 ka-ti7 ia7 siuN7 kong2 be7-kham-tit chhin-sin lai5 kiN3 Li2. Li2 kan-taN kong2 chit8 ku3 oe7, goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 chiu7 e7 ho2-khi3.  8) In-ui7 goa2 ia7-si7 chit8 e5 teng2-bin7 u7 siong7-si, e7-bin7 u7 peng-a2 e5 lang5. Goa2 ka7 chit e5 kong2, 몬Li2 khi3몭, i chiu7 khi3; ka7 hit e5 kong2, 몬Li2 lai5몭, i chiu7 lai5; ka7 goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 kong2, 몬Li2 an2-ne cho3몭, i chiu7 an2-ne cho3.몯  9) Ia5-sou thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7 chiu7 chin kam2-sim i, oat8 koe3-khi3 ka7 kin-toe3 I e5 cheng3-lang5 kong2: 몮Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, lian5 chai7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, Goa2 ia7 m7-bat khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 e5 sin3-sim.몯  10) Hiah-e5 su3-chia2 chit8-e7 tng2-khi3 kau3 lian5-tiuN2 e5 chhu3-nih, chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 lou5-pok8 i2-keng long2 ho2-khi3 a3.

Ia5-sou hou7 koaN2-hu7 e5 kiaN2 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5:
	11) Keng-koe3 bo5 loa7 ku2, Ia5-sou khi3 chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7, mia5 kio3-cho3 Na2-in. I e5 bun5-tou5 kap kui toa7 tin7 lang5 toe3 I khi3.  12) Ia5-sou lai5 teh-boeh kau3 siaN5-mng5 e5 si5, tu2 u7 lang5 kng chit8 e5 si2-lang5 boeh chhut-khi3 bai5-chong3 --- hit e5 si2-lang5 si7 chit8 e5 koaN2-hu7 e5 kou-kiaN2.  U7 chin toa7 tin7 siaN5-lai7 e5 lang5 teh sang3-chong3.  13) Chu2 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, chiu7 lin5-bin2 i, ka7 i kong2, 몮M7-bian2 khau3.몯  14) Ia5-sou chiu7 kiaN5 oa2-khi3 bong koaN-chha5. Kng koaN-chha5 e5 lang5 chiu7 theng5-kha. Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Siau3-lian5-lang5 a3, goa2 beng7-leng7 li2 khi2-lai5!몯  15) Hit e5 si2-khi3 e5 lang5 chiu7 peh khi2-lai5 che7, khai-si2 kong2-oe7. Ia5-sou chiu7 chiong i kau hou7 in lau7-bo2.  16) Cheng3-lang5 long2 khi2 tioh8-kiaN, chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2 kong2: 몮Lan2 e5 tiong-kan chhut-hian7 chit8 ui7 ui2-tai7 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 lou3!몯 In iu7-koh kong2, 몮Siong7-chu2 i2-keng u7 lai5 khoaN3-kou3 I e5 peh-seN3 a3!몯  17) Koan-he7 Ia5-sou chit e5 siau-sit chiu7 thoan5 kau3 Iu5-thai3 choan5 kok kap hu-kin7 e5 kok te7-hng khi3.

Si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 e5 Su3-chia2: (Ma2 11:2-19)
	18) Iok-han7 e5 bun5-tou5 chiong chiah-e5 siau-sit long2 khi3 ka7 Iok-han7 po3-ko3.  19) Iok-han7 chiu7 kio3 i nng7 e5 bun5-tou5 lai5, chhe in khi3 mng7 Chu2, kong2, 몮Li2 chiu7-si7 teh-boeh lai5 hit ui7 a2-si7 goan2 tioh8 koh tan2 leng7-goa7 chit8 ui7?몯  20) Chiah-e5 lang5 lai5-kau3 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-cheng5, chiu7 kong2: 몮Si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 chhe goan2 lai5 mng7 Li2 kong2, 몬Li2 chiu7-si7 teh-boeh lai5 hit ui7 a2-si7 goan2 tioh8 koh tan2 leng7-goa7 chit8 ui7?몭몯  21) Tu2 hit e5 si5-chun7, Ia5-sou u7 i-ho2 chin-che7 sin2-khou2 peN7-thiaN3 e5 lang5, tioh8-iau e5 lang5, ia7 hou7 chin-che7 chheN-me5-e5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3.  22) Ia5-sou chiu7 in3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 tng2-khi3 ka7 Iok-han7 po3-ko3 lin2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5, sou2 thiaN-kiN3 e5; chiu7-si7 chheN-me5-e5 koh-chai3 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, pai2-kha-e5 e7 kiaN5-lou7, ba5-hong-peN7 e5 lang5 long2 ho2-khi3, chhau3-hiN7-lang5 u7 thiaN-kiN3, si2-lang5 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, iu7-koh chheng-pin5 e5 lang5 thiaN-tioh8 Hok-im a.  23) Bo5 hoai5-gi5 goa2 e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3!몯
	24) Iok-han7 e5 su3-chia2 li7-khui liau2-au7, Ia5-sou khai-si2 tui3 cheng3-lang5 kong2-khi2 Iok-han7 e5 tia7-chi3. I kong2: 몮Lin2 chhut-khi3 khong3-ia2 si7 boeh khoaN3 sim2-mih? si7 hou7 hong chhoe7 tin2-tang7 e5 lou5-tek a2 m7-si7?  25) Lin2 kiu3-keng3 si7 chhut-khi3 khoaN3 sim2-mih? Si7 khi3 khoaN3 chheng7 chhia-hoa e5 i-hok8 e5 lang5 a2 m7-si7? Na7-si7 chheng7 chit khoan2 chhia-hoa e5 i-hok8, seng-oah8 chin chhia-chhi2 e5 lang5 si7 toa3 ti7 ong5-kiong lai7.  26) An2-ne, lin2 kiu3-keng3 si7 chhut-khi3 khoaN3 sim2-mih? si7 boeh khoaN3 tai7-gian5-jin5 a2 m7-si7? Si7 la3! Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, i pi2 tai7-gian5-jin5 koh-khah ui2-tai7.  27) Koan-he7 Iok-han7, Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2:
몬Lin2 khoaN3, Goa2 boeh chhe Goa2 e5 su3-chia2 cho3 Li2 e5 thau5-cheng5. I boeh cho3 Li2 e5 sian-hong chun2-pi7 Li2 e5 to7-lou7.몭
28) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, iu2-su2 i2-lai5 m7-bat u7 chit8 e5 lang5 pi2 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 koh-khah ui2-tai7, tan7-si7 chai7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok, siong7 se3 e5 iau2 pi2 i koh-khah ui2-tai7.몯
	29) ThiaN-tioh8 chiah-e5 oe7 e5 cheng3-lang5, lian5 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 ia7 pau-ham5 chai7-lai7, long2 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, in-ui7 in u7 nia2-siu7 Iok-han7 e5 se2-le2.  30) Tan7-si7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 kap Lut8-hoat e5 choan-ka, khi3-choat8 Siong7-chu2 ui7-tioh8 in sou2 an-pai5 e5, in-ui7 in bo5 ai3 nia2-siu7 Iok-han7 e5 se2-le2.
	31) 몮TaN chit e5 se3-tai7 e5 lang5 Goa2 tau3-te2 tioh8 eng7 sim2-mih lai5 pi2-pheng7? In si7 chhin-chhiuN7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 lang5?  32) In tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 tin7 gin2-na2 che7 ti7 chhi7-tiuN5 lai7 teh tui3 in e5 tang-phoaN7 hoah kong2:
몬goan2 ui7-tioh8 lin2 chau3 kiat-hun e5 im-gak8, lin2 ia7 bo5 boeh thiau3-bu2! Goan2 ui7-tioh8 lin2 chhiuN3 chong3-sek e5 ai-koa, lin2 ia7 bo5 boeh pi-siong!몭
33) Si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 lai5, i ia7 bo5 chiah8 mi7-pau ia7 bo5 lim-chiu2, lin2 chiu7 kong2, 몬I teh khi2-siau2!몭  34) Jin5-chu2 lai5, ia7 u7 chiah8 ia7 u7 lim, lin2 chiu7 kong2, 몬Li2 khoaN3! Chit e5 tham-chiah8 houN3-chiu2 e5 lang5, si7 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 kap choe7-jin5 e5 peng5-iu2!몭  35) Tan7-si7 chiap-siu7 Siong7-chu2 e5 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5, cheng3-beng5 Siong7-chu2 e5 ti3-hui7 si7 chin-sit8 e5.몯

Ia5-sou ti7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, Se-bun5 e5 chhu3:
	36) U7 chit8 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 chhiaN2 Ia5-sou kap i chiah8-png7. Ia5-sou chiu7 jip8-khi3 hit e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 e5 chhu3-nih che7-toh.  37) Hit e5 siaN5-chhi7 u7 chit8 e5 phaiN2 cha-bou2. I chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-sou ti7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 e5 chhu3-nih teh chiah8-png7, chiu7 koaN7 chit8 koan3 te2 phang-iu5 e5 chioh8-ko-pan5 jip8-lai5, 38) khia7 toa3 Ia5-sou e5 au7-bin7, oa2-khi3 kha-piN na2 khau3 na2 lau5 bak8-sai2 tih toa3 Ia5-sou e5 kha. I koh eng7 ka-ti7 e5 thau5-mng5 ka7 I chhit hou7 ta; it-tit8 chimIa5-sou e5 kha, koh eng7 phang-iu5 ka7 I boah kha.  39) Hit e5 chhiaN2 Ia5-sou e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne, chiu7 sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2: 몮Chit e5 lang5 na7 sit8-chai7 si7 tai7-gian5-jin5, it-teng7 e7 chai-iaN2 chit e5 teh ka7 I bong e5 si7 sim2-mih lang5, si7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 cha-bou2-lang5! I it-teng7 ia7 e7 chai-iaN2 i si7 phaiN2 cha-bou2.몯  40) Ia5-sou chiu7 tui3 i kong2, 몮Se-bun5, Goa2 u7 oe7 boeh ka7 li2 kong2.몯 Se-bun5 kong2, 몮Lau7-su, chhiaN2 Li2 kong2.몯  41) Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Khah-cha2 u7 nng7 e5 lang5 khiam3 che3-chu2 e5 chiN5, chit e5 khiam3 i gou7-pah e5 gin5-oan5, iau2 chit8 e5 khiam3 i gou7-chap8 e5 gin5-oan5.  42) In-ui7 in nng7 e5 long2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang heng5-che3; che3-chu2 chiu7 bian2-ti5 in e5 che3-bu7. An2-ne, tah chit8 e5 e7 khah ai3 hit e5 che3-chu2?몯  43) Se-bun5 in3 kong2, 몮Goa2 siuN7 si7 hit e5 hou7 i sia3-bian2 khah che7 e5.몯 Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2, 몮Li2 in3 an2-ne tioh8.몯  44) Jian5-au7 I oah8 koe3-khi3 khoaN3 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, chiu7 ka7 Se-bun5 kong2: 몮Li2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 bo5? Goa2 jip8-lai5 li2 e5 chhu3-nih, li2 bo5 iuN2 chui2 hou7 Goa2 se2 kha; tan7-si7 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 eng7 i e5 bak8-sai2 ka7 Goa2 se2 kha, iu7-koh eng7 i e5 thau5-mng5 ka7 goa2 chhit kha.  45) Li2 bo5 ka7 Goa2 chim lai5 hoan-geng5 Goa2; tan7-si7 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chu7 Goa2 jip8-lai5, chiu7 it-tit8 chim Goa2 e5 kha chim bo5 hioh-khun3.  46) Li2 bo5 eng7 iu5 boah Goa2 e5 thau5-khak; tan7-si7 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 eng7 phang-iu5 boah Goa2 e5 kha.  47) Sou2-i2 Goa2 ka7 li2 kong2: i chin-che7 e5 choe7-ko3 it-teng7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2 a3. Na7 bo5, i be7 piau2-si7 chiah-nih8 toa7 e5 ai3-cheng5. Lang5 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 sia3-bian2 na7 chio2, i sou2 piau2-si7 chhut-lai5 e5 ai3-cheng5 ia7 chio2.몯  48) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou ka7 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, 몮Li2 e5 choe7 i2-keng tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2 a3.몯  49) Kang7 toh e5 lang5 sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 kiu3-keng3 si7 sim2-mih lang5? I sim7-chi3 sia3-bian2 lang5 e5 choe7.몯  50) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, 몮Li2 e5 sin3-sim kiu3-tioh8 li2 a3, an-sim tng2-khi3.몯

Te7 8 ChiuN

Hong-su7 Ia5-sou e5 hu7-jin5-lang5:
	1) Au7-lai5, Ia5-sou sun5-hoe5 chit8 siaN5-chhi7 koe3 chit8 siaN5-chhi7, chit8 hiong-chhoan koe3 chit8 hiong-chhoan, kong2 to7-li2, soan-iong5 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 Hok-im. Hit chap8-ji7 e5 Su3-tou5 ia7 kap I cho3-tin7,  2) ia7 u7 kui2-na7 e5 i2-cheng5 tioh8-iau a2-si7 tioh8-peN7 hou7 Ia5-sou i-ho2 khi3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, ia7 kap I cho3-hoe2 khi3. Chiah-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7-si7 Ia5-sou bat tui3 i e5 seng-khu koaN2 chhit e5 kui2 chhut-khi3 e5 Boat8-tai7-liap8 e5 Ma2-li7-a;  3) Hi-lut8 e5 koan2-ke Khou2-sat e5 bou2 Iok-a-na2; kap Sou-sat-na2, i2-kip8 ki5-tha chin-che7 hu7-jin5-lang5. In long2 eng7 ka-ti7 e5 chiN5-chai5 lai5 hong7-thai7 Ia5-sou kap I e5 bun5-tou5.

Ia7 cheng2-chi2 e5 phi3-ju7: (Ma2 13:1-9; Kho2 4:1-9)
	4) Kun5-chiong3 ke3-siok8 tui3 kok siaN5-chhi7 it-tit8 chip8 oa2-lai5 Ia-sou hia; I chiu7 eng7 phi3-ju7 ka7 in kong2:
	5) 몮U7 chit8 e5 long5-hu chhut-khi3 ia7 cheng2-chi2. I teh ia7 cheng2-chi2 e5 si5, u7-e5 ka-lauh8 ti7 lou7-piN, hou7 koe3-lou7-lang5 tah8, hou7 poe-chiau2 chiah8-khi3.  6) U7-e5 ka-lauh8 ti7 chioh8-poaN5 teng2; in-ui7 bo5 chui2-khi3, cheng2-chi2 chit8-e7 puh-ge5 chiu7 ta-khi3.  7) U7-e5 ka-lauh8 ti7 chhi3-a2 lai7, kap chhi3-a2 tang5-che5 toa7-chang5 khi2-lai5, soah hou7 chhi3-a2 hip-si2.  8) U7-e5 ka-lauh8 ti7 ho2 thou5-bah; seng5-tiong2 khi2-lai5, chiu7 kiat-sit8 kiat chit8-pah poe7.몯 I chiah-e5 oe7 kong2 soah chiu7 toa7 siaN kong2, 몮U7 hiN7-khang thang thiaN e5 lang5, tioh8 thiaN!몯

Ia5-sou eng7 phi3-ju7 e5 bok8-tek: (Ma2 13:10-17; Kho2 4:10-12)
	9) I e5 bun5-tou5 chiu7 mng7 I chit e5 phi3-ju7 si7 sim2-mih i3-su3.  10) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Siong7-chu2 u7 siuN2-su3 lin2 tek8-koan5 lai5 jim7-sek Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 o3-pi3, tan7-si7 tui3 pat8-lang5 chi2-u7 eng7 phi3-ju7, thang hou7 in khoaN3 ia7 khoaN3 be7 beng5-pek8, thiaN ia7 thiaN be7 liau2-kai2.몯

Ia5-sou kai2-sek ia7 cheng2-chi2 e5 phi3-ju7: (Ma2 13:18-23; Kho2 4:13-20)
	11) 몮Chit e5 phi3-ju7 e5 i3-su3 si7 an2-ne: cheng2-chi2 chiu7-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 to7-li2.  12) Ka-lauh8 ti7 lou7-piN e5 cheng2-chi2 si7 teh phi3-ju7 lang5 thiaN tioh8 to7-li2, jian5-au7 Mou5-kui2 lai5, tui3 in e5 sim-tiong chhiuN2 hiah-e5 to7-li2 khi3, hou7 in be7-tang3 sin3, ia7 be7-tang3 tit-tioh8 kiu3.  13) Ka-lauh8 ti7 chioh8-poaN5-teng2 e5 cheng2-chi2 si7 teh phi3-ju7 lang5 chit8-e7 thiaN tioh8 to7-li2, chiu7 hoaN-hi2 chiap-siu7. Tan7-si7 to7-li2 bo5 teng3-kin toa3 i e5 sim-lai7; in chi2-u7 chiam7-si5 sin3, chit8-e7 tu2-tioh8 chhi3-lian7 chiu7 pang3-tiau7 khi3 .  14) Ka-lauh8 ti7 chhi3-a2 lai7 e5 cheng2-chi2, si7 teh phi3-ju7 lang5 thiaN-tioh8 to7-li2, tan7-si7 siu7-tioh8 se3-kan e5 khoa3-li7, chiN5-chai5 kap khoai3-lok8 e5 chou2-gai7, to7-li2 soah be7 seng5-tiong2 kiat-sit8.  15) Ka-lauh8 ti7 ho2 thou5-bah e5 cheng2-chi2, si7 teh phi3-ju7 hioah-e5 thiaN-tioh8 to7-li2 e5 lang5, chiong to7-li2 po2-chun5 toa3 in sian7-liong5 seng5-sit8 e5 sim-lai7, kian-chhi5 kau3 tit-tioh8 siu-seng5.몯

Bi2-tau2-e7 e5 teng-hoe2: (Kho2 4:21-25)
	16) 몮Bo5 lang5 tiam2-teng eng7 bi2-tau2 kham3 khi2-lai5, a2-si7 ka7 i khng3 toa3 bin5-chhng5 kha. Long2 ka7 i khngt3oa teng-hoe2-tai5-teng2, thang hou7 jip8-lai5 e5 lang5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 kng.  17) In-ui7 it-chhe3 un2-chong5 e5 tai7-chi3 long2 e7 lou7-hian7, it-chhe3 pi2-bit8 e5 tai7-chi3 long2 e7 hian2-lou7 chhut-lai5.몯
	18) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 chu3-i3 khoaN3 boeh an3-choaN2 lai5 thiaN; in-ui7 tui3 u7 e5 lang5, Siong7-chu2 e7 siuN2-su3 i koh-khah che7, tan7-si7 tui3 bo5 e5 lang5, lian5 i siuN7-cho3 i u7 e5 chit8-sut-la2, ia7 e7 ka7 i chhiuN2-toat8 khi3.몯

Ia5-sou e5 bo2-chhin kap hiaN-ti7: (Ma2 12:46-50; Kho2 3:31-35)
	19) U7 chit8 pai2 Ia5-sou e5 lau7-bo2 kap I e5 hiaN-ti7 lai5 chhoe7 I, tan7-si7 in-ui7 lang5 chin-che7, be7-tang3 oa2-khi3 I hia.  20) U7 lang5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Li2 e5 lau7-bo2 kap hiaN-ti7 khia7 ti7 goa7-bin7 teh tan2 boeh kiN3 Li2.몯  21) Ia5-sou tui3 in kong2: 몮ThiaN Siong7-chu2 e5 to7-li2, chiau3 an2-ne khi3 sit8-heng5 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 Goa2 e5 lau7-bo2, goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7.몯

Ia5-sou tin3-ap hong-eng2: (Ma2 8:23-27; Kho2 4:35-41)
	22) U7 chit8 jit8, Ia5-sou kap I e5 bun5-tou5 che7 loh8-khi3 chun5-nih8 e5 si5, I ka7 in kong2, 몮Lan2 koe3 lai5-khi3 ou5 e5 hit peng5 hoaN7.몯 In chiu7 khui chun5 khi3.  23) Chun5 teh kiaN5 e5 si5, Ia5-sou khun3-khi3. Hut-jian5-kan kiong5-liat8 e5 hong sau3 loh8-lai5 ou5-nih8, chun5 chiu7 khai-si2 it-tit8 jip8-chui2 jip8 kah giong7 boeh tiN7 khi2-lai5, chin gui5-hiam2.  24) Bun5-tou5 chong5 lai5 kio3 chheN2 Ia5-sou, hoah kong2, 몮Lau7-su a3, Lau7-su a3! Lan2 teh-boeh bo5 mia7 lou3!몯 I chiu7 chheN2 khi3-lai5, chek-pi7 hong kap toa7-eng2, hong-eng2 chiu7 tiam7, chiu7 long2 peng5-cheng7 khi3.  25) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2, 몮Lin2 e5 sin3-sim ti7 tah-ui7?몯 In ia7 tioh8-kiaN ia7 gong7-ngiah8, hou7-siong kong2: 몮Chit e5 lang5 tau3-te2 si7 sim2-mih lang5? An3-choaN2 I chit-e7 beng7-leng7, lian5 hong-eng2 ia7 hok8-chiong5 I?몯

Ia5-sou i-ho2 tioh8-iau e5 lang5: (Ma2 8:28-34; Kho2 5:1-20)
	26) Ia5-sou kap bun5-tou5 sou2 che7 e5 chun5 khi3-kau3 Ka-li7-li7 ou5 e5 tui3-hoaN7, Kek-lah-sim-lang5 e5 te7-hng.  27) Ia5-sou chit8-e7 peh khit-khi3 hoaN7-teng2, u7 chit8 e5 lang5 tui3 siaN5-chhi7 lai5 kiN3 I. Chit e5 lang5 tioh8-iau, chin ku2 bo5 chheng7 saN, ia7 bo5 toa3 ti7 chhu3-lai7, long2 toa3 ti7 bong7-nih8.  28) I chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou, chiu7 hoah-hiu, phak toa3 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-cheng5 toa7-siaN kong2: 몮Chi3-ko Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2 Ia5-sou! Li2 ho5-pit lai5 kan-siap8 goa2? Goa2 khun2-kiu5 Li2, m7-thang chek-hoat8 goa2.몯  29) I kong2 an2-ne si7 in-ui7 Ia5-sou i2-keng u7 beng7-leng7 sia5-sin5 tui3 hit e5 lang5 chhut-khi3. In-ui7 sia5-sin5 chin-che7 pai2 tui3 hit e5 lang5 liah8 tiau5-tiau5, lang5 sui-jian5 eng7 kha-khau3 ka7 i khau3-le3, eng7 lian7-a2 ka7 i lian7-le7, ia7 tiaN7-tiaN7 ka7 i koaiN tiau5 le7, i long2 chhoah-tng7 lian7-a2, sia5-sin5 hou7 i chong5 chhut-khi3 khong3-ia2.  30) Ia5-sou mng7 i kong2, 몮Li2 ho7-cho3 sim2-mih mia5?몯 I in3 kong2, 몮Kun-thoan5몯 --- in-ui7 u7 chin-che7 sia5-mou5 ka7 i hu7-sin.  31) TaN hiah-e5 sia5-mou5 chiu7 khun2-kiu5 Ia5-sou m7-thang beng7-leng7 in jip8-khi3 bo5-te2 chhim-kheN.
	32) Ti7 hia tu2 u7 chit8 toa7 tin7 ti pang3 ti7 soaN-phiaN5 teh tho2-chiah8; hiah-e5 sia5-mou5 chiu7 khun2-kiu5 Ia5-sou, chun2 in jip8-khi3 hiah-e5 ti e5 lai7-bin7. Ia5-sou chiu7 in2-chun2 in.  33) Hiah-e5 sia5-mou5 chiu7 tui3 hit e5 lang5 chhut-khi3, jip8-khi3 ti e5 lai7-bin7; hit tin7 ti chiu7 sui5-si5 tui3 soaN-phiaN5 chong5 loh8-khi3 ou5-nih8, hou7 chui2 kek-si2.
	34) Chhi7-ti e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 e5 si5, chiu7 chau2 khi3 hu7-kin7 e5 siaN5-chhi7 kap hiong-chhoan, po3-ko3 hou7 lang5 chai.  35) Lang5 chiu7 long2 chhut-lai5 boeh khoaN3 si7 sim2-mih tai7-chi3. In lai5-kau3 Ia5-sou hia, khoaN3-kiN3 sia5-mou5 i2-keng tui3 hit e5 lang5 chhut-khi3 a3. I u7 chheng7 saN-khou3, cheng-sin5 ia7 chin cheng3-siong5, che7 ti7 Ia5-sou e5 kha-piN. In chiu7 long2 toa7 tioh8-kiaN.  36) Chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 tai7-chi3 e5 lang5, chiu7 chiong Ia5-sou an3-choaN2 i-ho2 hit e5 tioh8-iau e5 lang5 e5 tai7-chi3 ka7 in po3-ko3.  37) Hit e5 si5, Kek-lah-sim kap hu7-kin7 kok te7-hng e5 lang5 long2 kiu5 Ia5-sou li7-khui in hia, in-ui7 in khi2 toa7 khiong2-hong5.  Ia5-sou chiu7 che7 chun5 to3 tng2-khi3.  38) Thoat-li7 sia5-mou5 hit e5 lang5 khun2-kiu5 boeh toe3 Ia5-sou khi3. Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou kio3 i tng2-khi3, kong2:  39) 몮Li2 tng2-khi3 chhu3-nih, chiong Siong7-chu2 tui3 li2 sou2 cho3 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3 kong2 hou7 cheng3-lang5 chai.몯 Hit e5 lang5 chiu7 tng2-khi3, chiong Ia5-sou ui7 i sou2 cho3 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3, kui ke-a2 soan-thoan5 thau3-thau3.

I-ho2 Gai5-lou2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 kap hiat-lau7-peN7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5: (Ma2 9:18-26; Kho2 5:21-43)
	40) Ia5-sou tng2-lai5 e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 long2 chin ka7 I hoan-geng5; in-ui7 in long2 it-tit8 teh theng3-hau7 I.  41) Hit e5 si5 u7 chit8 e5 kio3-cho3 Gai5-lou2 e5 lang5 lai5; i si7 hoe7-tng5-tiuN2. I lai5 phak toa3 Ia5-sou e5 kha-cheng5, khun2-kiu5 I khi3 in chhu3,  42) in-ui7 i chi2-u7 chit8 e5 chap8-ji7 hoe3 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 nia7-nia7. Hit e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 giong7-boeh si2-khi3 a3.
	Ia5-sou boeh khi3 e5 si5, ian5-lou7 chin-che7 lang5 cho3 chit8-e7 ka I chiN oa2-lai5.  43) U7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 hoan7-tioh8 hiat-lau7-peN7 i2-keng chap8-ji7 ni5 ku2. Sui-jian5 kheng-ke tong7-san2 chhiaN2 i-seng lai5 ka7 i i-peN7, tan7-si7 bo5 lang5 e7-tang3 ka7 i i-hokh2i.  44) I kiaN5 oa2-lai5 Ia5-sou e5 au7-bin7, bong Ia5-sou e5 saN-a2-ki e5 chhiu, i e5 hiat-lau7 chiu7 chek-si5 chi2.  45) Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Sim2-mih lang5 ka7 Goa2 bong?몯 Tai7-ke long2 kong2 bo5. Pi2-tek chiu7 kong2, 몮Lau7-su a3, si7 chiu-ui5 e5 cheng3-lang5 teh ka7 Li2 kheh-lai5 kheh-khi3!몯  46) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮U7 lang5 ka7 Goa2 bong-tioh8; in-ui7 Goa2 chai koan5-leng5 tui3 Goa2 e5 seng-khu chhut-khi3.몯  47) Hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chit8-e7 chai-iaN2 kham3 be7 bat, chiu7 kiaN kah phih8-phih8-chhoah, lai5 phak toa3 Ia5-sou e5 kha-cheng5. Hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 soat-beng5 ui7 sim2-mih i e7 lai5 bong Ia5-sou, i e5 an3-choaN2 chek-si5 ho2-khi3.  48) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2. 몮Hu7-jin5-lang5 a3! Li2 e5 sin3-sim hou7 li2 ho2-khi3 a3. Thang an-sim tng2-khi3.몯
	49) Ia5-sou iau2 teh kong2-oe7 e5 si5, u7 lang5 tui3 chhu3-nih lai5 ka7 hoe7-tng5-tiuN2 Gai5-lou2 kong2, 몮Li2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 i2-keng si2-khi3 a3, ho5-pit tioh8 koh lo5-hoan5 Lau7-su.몯  50) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou thiaN-kiN3 an2-ne chiu7 tui3 Gai5-lou2 kong2, 몮M7-bian2 kiaN, chi2-u7 tioh8 sin3, i chiu7 e7 ho2-khi3.몯  51) Ia5-sou khi3-kau3 in chhu3 e5 si5, Pi2-tek, Nga2-kok, Iok-han7 kap gin2-na2 e5 pe7-bo2 i2-goa7, m7-chun2 pat8-lang5 kap i cho3-hoe2 jip8-khi3.  52) Tai7-ke long2 ui7-tioh8 chit e5 si2-khi3 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 teh thi5-khau3 pi-siong. Ia5-sou kong2. 몮M7-thang khau3, in-ui7 i m7-si7 si2-khi3, si7 teh khun3 na7-tiaN7.몯  53) In-ui7 in long2 chai-iaN2 hit e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 i2-keng si2-khi3 a3, chiu7 ka7 I thi2-chhio3.  54) Ia5-sou khan cha-bou2-gin2-na2 e5 chhiu2, toa7 siaN kong2. 몮Cha-bou2-gin2-na2, khi2-lai5!몯  55) I chiu7 hoe5-hun5, chek-si5 peh khi2-lai5.  Ia5-sou hoan-hu3 lang5 tioh8 phang5 chiah8-mih8 hou7 i chiah8.  56) I e5 pe7-bo2 kiaN kah gang7-gang7 khi3. Ia5-sou beng7-leng7 in m7-thang ka7 lang5 kong2 khi2 chit e5 tai7-chi3.

Te7 9 ChiuN

Ia5-sou chhe-phai3 chap8-ji7 e5 Su3-tou5: (Ma2 10:5-15; Kho2 6:7-13)
	Ia5-sou kio3 chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 oa2-lai5, siuN2-su3 in leng5-lek8 kap koan5-peng3 thang che3-hok8 it-chhe3 e5 Mou5-kui2 kap i-ti7 it-chhe3 e5 peN7-cheng3.  2) Jian5-au7 I chhe-phai3 in chhut-khi3 soan-kang2 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok kap i-ho2 peN7-lang5.  3) I kau-tai3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 chhut-mng5 m7-thang toa3 sim2-mih : m7-thang toa3 koai2-a2, m7-thang toa3 li2-heng5 te7, m7-thang toa3 mi7-pau, m7-thang toa3 chiN5, ia7 m7-thang ke toa3 lai7-saN.  4) Lin2 bo5-lun7 jip8-khi3 tah chit8 keng chhu3, tioh8 toa3 hia, toa3 kau3 lin2 li7-khui hit e5 siaN5-chhi7.  5) Lang5 na7 bo5 hoan-geng5 lin2, boeh li7-khui hit e5 siaN5-chhi7 e5 si5, kha e5 thou5-hun2 tioh8 poaN7 hou7 chheng-khi3, lai5 ka7 in keng2-kou3.몯  6) Bun5-tou5 chiu7 chhut-hoat, khi3 chit8 hiong-chhoan koe3 chit8 hiong-chhoan, soan-kang2 Hok-im, ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7 i-ho2 peN7-lang5.

Hi-lut8-ong5 e5 put-an: (Ma2 14:1-12; Kho2 6:14-29)
	7) Hun-hong e5 ong5 Hi-lut8 thiaN-kiN3 sou2 hoat-seng it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3, soah sim-lai7 khi2 put-an, in-ui7 u7 lang5 kong2 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 tui3 si2-lang5 e5 tiong-kan koh-oah8 khi2-lai5 a3;  8) ia7 u7 lang5 kong2 si7 chit8 ui7 kou2-cha2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 chai3-se3.  9) Hi-lut8 kong2: 몮Iok-han7 --- goa2 i2-keng ka7 i thai5-thau5 a7; tan7-si7 lin2 sou2 po3-ko3 chit e5 lang5 kiu3-keng3 si7 sim2-mih lang5?몯 I chiu7 chin ai3 boeh kiN3 Ia5-sou.

Ia5-sou hou7 gou7-chheng lang5 chiah8 kah pa2: (Ma2 14:13-21; Kho2 6:30-44; Iok 6:1-14)
	10) Chiah-e5 Su3-tou5 tng2-lai5, chiong in sou2 cho3 e5 tai7-chi3 long2 ka7 Ia5-sou po3-ko3. Ia5-sou chiu7 chi2-u7 chhoa7 in siam2-pi7 khi3-kau3 chit8 e5 kio3-cho3 Pek-sai3-tai7 e5 siaN5-chhi7.  11) Cheng3-lang5 chit8-e7 chai-iaN2, chiu7 toe3 I khi3. Ia5-sou hoan-geng5 in, kong2 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 tai7-chi3 hou7 in thiaN, i-ho2 hiah-e5 su-iau3 ti7-liau5 e5 lang5.
	12) ThiN boeh am3 e5 si5, chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 lai5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2: 몮ChhiaN2 kai2-san3 cheng3-lang5, thang hou7 in khi3 chiu-ui5 e5 hiong-chhoan chhoe7 sou2-chai7 thang toa3, chhoe7 chiah8-mih8 thang chiah8; in-ui7 chia si7 phian-phiah e5 sou2-chai7.몯  13) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou in3 kong2, 몮Lin2 tioh8 siat-hoat hou7 in chiah8.몯 In kong2, 몮Goan2 chi2-u7 gou7 ki mi7-pau kap nng7 boe2 hi5 nia7-nia7. Li2 kam2 ai3 goan2 khi3 be2 chiah8-mih8 lai5 hou7 chiah-che7 lang5 chiah8 si7 bo5?몯  14) (Ti7 hia chha-put-to u7 gou7-chheng e5 cha-pou-lang5.) Ia5-sou chiu7 tui3 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2, 몮Kio3 in hun chou che7 loh8-khi3, chit8 chou chha-put-to gou7-chap8 e5 lang5.몯  15) Bun5-tou5 chiau3 an2-ne khi3 cho3, kio3 cheng3-lang5 long2 che7 loh8-khi3.  16) Ia5-sou chiu7 theh8 hit gou7 ki mi7-pau kap hit nng7 boe2 hi5 khi2-lai5, giong2-bong7 thiN lai5 kam2-sia7 Siong7-chu2 siuN2-su3 chiah-e5 chiah8-mih8 liau2-au7, peh cho3 chit8-te3 chit8-te3, theh8 hou7 bun5-tou5, kio3 in pun hou7 cheng3-lang5.  17) Cheng-lang5 long2 chiah8 kah chin pa2, Bun5-tou5 siu-chip8 chiah8 chhun e5 iu3-sap, long2-chong2 u7 chap8-ji7 lang2.

Pi2-tek seng5-jin7 Ia5-sou si7 Bi2-sai3-a: (Ma2 16:13-19; Kho2 8:27-29)
	18) U7 chit8 pai2 Ia5-sou ka-ti7 chit8 e5 teh ki5-to2 e5 si5, chi2-u7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kap I ti7 hia. Ia5-sou chiu7 mng7 in kong2, 몮Cheng3-lang5 kong2 Goa2 si7 sim2-mih lang5?몯  19) In in3 kong2: 몮U7 lang5 kong2 si7 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7, ia7 u7 lang5 kong2 si7 I2-li7-a, iu7-koh u7 lang5 kong2 si7 kou2-cha2 e5 chit8 ui7 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 chai3-se3.몯  20) Ia5-sou mng7 in kong2, 몮TaN Goa2 ai3 chai lin2 e5 khoaN3-hoat. Lin2 kong2 Goa2 si7 sim2-mih lang5?몯 Pi2-tek chiu7 in3 kong2, 몮Li2 si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 bi2-sai3-a.몯

Ia5-sou i7-ko3 I e5 si2-bong5 kap hok8-hoat8: (Ma2 16:20-28; Kho2 8:30-9:1)
	21) Ia5-sou giam5-keh hoan-hu3 in m7-thang ka7 lang5 kong2 chit e5 tai7-chi3.  22) I iu7-koh kong2: 몮Jin5-chu2 tek-khak tioh8 siu7 chin-che7 khou2-lan7, hou7 tiuN2-lo2, che3-si-tiuN2 kap keng-hak8-chia2 khi3-choat8, it-teng7 e7 hou7 in sat-hai7, tan7-si7 te7 saN jit8 Siong7-chu2 it-teng7 e7 hou7 I hok8-hoat8.몯
	23) Ia5-sou koh tui3 cheng3-lang5 kong2: 몮Lang5 na7 ai3-boeh kin-toe3 Goa2, tioh8 pang3-sak ka-ti7, tak8-jit8 gia5 i ka-ti7 e5 sip8-ji7-ke3 lai5 toe3 Goa2.  24) In-ui7 lang5 na7 ai3-boeh kiu3 i ka-ti7 e5 seN3-mia7, tian-to3 e7 song3-sit; tan7-si7 lang5 na7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 lai5 hi-seng i ka-ti7 e5 seN3-mia7, tian-to3 e7 kiu3-tioh8 i e5 seN3-mia7.  25) In-ui7 lang5 sui-jian5 tit-tioh8 choan5 se3-kai3, tan7-si7 na7 song3-sit ka-ti7, a2-si7 hui2-biat8 ka-ti7, u7 sim2-mih li7-ek?  26) Lang5 na7 ui7-tioh8 sin3 Goa2 kap Goa2 e5 oe7 lai5 kam2-kak kian3-siau3, Jin5-chu2 toa3 I ka-ti7 kap Thian-hu7 i2-kip8 seng3 thian-sai3 e5 eng5-iau7 lai5 e5 si5, ia7 e7 ui7 i kam2-kak kian3-siau3.  27) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, khia7 ti7 chia e5 lang5, u7 lang5 iau2-boe7 si2 i2-cheng5, it-teng7 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok.몯

Ia5-sou kai2-pian3 heng5-siong7: (Ma2 17:1-8; Kho2 9:2-8)
	28) Kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 liau2-au7, chha-put-to koe3 chit8 le2-pai3, Ia5-sou chhoa7 Pi2-tek, Nga2-kok kap Iok-han7 peh-chiuN7 chit8 cho7 soaN ki5-to2.  29) I teh ki5-to2 e5 si5, bin7-mau7 pian3-cho3 bo5 kang7-khoan2, lian5 I e5 i-hok8 ia7 pian3 kah peh8 siak-siak.  30) Hut-jian5-kan u7 nng7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se kap I2-li7-a lai5 kap Ia5-sou teh kong2-oe7.  31) In chai7 eng5-iau7 tiong chhut-hian7, teh tam5-lun7 Ia5-sou koh bo5 loa7 ku2 e7 si2 toa3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, lai5 oan5-seng5 Siong7-chu2 e5 ke3-ek8.  32) Pi2-tek kap i e5 tang5-phoaN7 long2 khun3-khi3, chit8-e7 cheng-sin5 khi2-lai5 chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou e5 eng5-iau7, i2-kip8 kap I khia7 cho3-hoe2 hit nng7 e5 lang5.  33) In hit nng7 e5 lang5 boeh li7-khui Ia5-sou e5 si5, Pi2-tek ka7 Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Lau7-su a3, lan2 toa3 chia sit8-chai7 chin ho2! Lan2 lai5 tah saN keng liau5-a2, chit8 keng hou7 Li2, chit8 keng hou7 Mou5-se, chit8 keng hou7 I2-li7-a.몯 (I sit8-chai7 m7-chai i teh kong2 sim2-mih.)  34) I iau2 teh kong2 e5 si5, u7 chit8 phiN3 hun5 chhut-hian7, eng7 iaN2 ka7 in kham3 khi2-lai5. Hit saN ui7 jip8-khi3 hun5-lai7 e5 si5, bun5-tou5 chiu7 khi2 tioh8-kiaN.  35) Tui3 hit phiN3 hun5 e5 lai7-bin7 u7 siaN kong2: 몮Chit e5 si7 Goa2 sou2 keng2-soan2 e5 KiaN2. Lin2 tioh8 thiaN I e5 oe7!몯  36) Hit e5 siaN chit8-e7 tiam7-khi3, kan-taN u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou chit8 e5 ti7 hia nia7-nia7. Bun5-tou5 tui3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 po2-siu2 pi2-bit8. Hit tong-si5 chiong in sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 bo5 ka7 lang5 kong2.

Ia5-sou i-ho2 tioh8-iau e5 gin2-na2: (Ma2 17:14-18; Kho2 9:14-27)
	37) Keh-tng2-jit8, in tui3 soaN-teng2 loh8-lai5 e5 si5, u7 chin-che7 lang5 lai5 geng5-chiap Ia5-sou.  38) Cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan u7 chit8 e5 lang5 hoah kong2: 몮Lau7-su, kiu5 Li2 khoaN3-kou3 goa2 e5 kiaN2; i si7 goa2 e5 kou-kiaN2.  39) I na7 chit8-e7 hou7 iau-mou5 hu7-sin, sui5-si5 chiu7 loan7 hoah. Iau-mou5 hou7 i hoat-choh, chhoah kah phu7 peh8-pho-noa7. Iau-mou5 put-toan7 teh siong-hai7 i, long2 bo5 boeh pang3 i soah.  40) Goa2 u7 chhiaN2 Li2 e5 bun5-tou5 ka7 i koaN2 iau-mou5 chhut-khi3, tan7-si7 in long2 bo5 hoat-tou7.몯  41) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2: 몮Ai a3! Chit e5 se3-tai7 e5 lang5 na2 e7 chiah-nih8 bo5 sin3-sim koh chiah8-nih8 sia5-ok! Goa2 tioh8 koh kap lin2 toa3 loa7 ku2? Goa2 tioh8 koh thun-lun2 lin2 loa7 ku2?몯 Jian5-au7 tui3 hit e5 lang5 kong2, 몮Chhoa7 hit e5 gin2-na2 lai5 Goa2 chia!몯  42) Gin2-na2 teh lai5 e5 si5, iau-mou5 chiu7 ka7 i siak loh8-khi3 thou5-kha, hou7 i hoat-choh. Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou chek-pi7 hit e5 sia5-sin5, ka7 hit e5 gin2-na2 i-ho2 khi3, kau hou7 in lau7-pe7.  43) Cheng3-lang5 long2 kam2-than3 Siong7-chu2 ui2-tai7 e5 leng5-lek8.

Ia5-sou te7-ji7 chhu3 i7-ko3 I e5 si2-bong5: (Ma2 17:22-23; Kho2 9:30-32)
	Cheng3-lang5 iau2 teh kam2-than3 Ia5-sou sou2 teh cho3 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3 e5 si5, Ia5-sou tui3 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2:  44) 몮Goa2 chit-chun7 boeh ka7 lin2 kong2 e5 oe7, lin2 tioh8 chu3-i3 thiaN. Jin5-chu2 teh-boeh hou7 lang5 kau khi3 lang5 e5 chhiu2-thau5 a7.몯  45) Tan7-si7 bun5-tou5 be7-tang3 liau2-kai2 chit ku3 oe7 e5 i3-su3. Chit ku3 oe7 e5 i3-su3 kou3-i3 ka7 in am-kham3 khi2-lai5, hou7 in liah8 be7 tioh8. In ia7 m7-kaN2 mng7 Ia5-sou khoaN3 si7 sim2-mih i3-su3.

Sim2-mih lang5 siong7 ui2-tai7? (Ma2 18:1-5; Kho2 9:33-37)
	46) U7 chit8 pai2 bun5-tou5 tai7-ke cheng-lun7 kong2 in e5 tiong-kan sim2-mih lang5 siong7 ui2-tai7.  47) Ia5-sou chai-iaN2 in e5 sim-lai7 sou2 teh siuN7 e5 tia7-chi3, chiu7 chhoa7 chit8 e5 gin2-na2 lai5, hou7 i khia7 toa3 I e5 sin-piN,  48) ka7 in kong2: 몮Bo5-lun7 sim2-mih lang5, na7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 lai5 hoan-geng5 chit e5 gin2-na2, chiu7-si7 hoan-geng5 Goa2; hoan-geng5 Goa2 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 hoan-geng5 Hit-ui7 chhe-phai3 Goa2 lai5 e5. In-ui7 ti7 lin2 cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan siong7 se3 e5, chiu7 si7 siong7 ui2-tai7 e5.몯

Bo5 hoan2-tui3 lin2 e5, chiu7-si7 chan3-seng5 lin2 e5: (Kho2 9:38-40)
	49) Iok-han7 kong2: 몮Lau7-su a3, goan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 lang5 hong7 Li2 e5 mia5 teh koaN2-kui2, goan2 chiu7 ka7 i chou2-chi2, in-ui7 i m7-si7 kap lan2 kang7-tin7 e5 lang5.몯  50) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2: 몮M7-thang ka7 i chou2-chi2; in-ui7 bo5 hoan2-tui3 lin2 e5, chiu7-si7 chan3-seng5 lin2 e5.몯

Sat-ma2-li7-a e5 hiong-chhoan ki7-choat8 chiap-siu7 Ia5-sou:
	51) Ia5-sou li7-khui se3-kan seng-thian e5 jit8-chi2 teh-boeh kau3 a3. I chiu7 koat-i3 boeh khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  52) I chhe-phai3 su3-chia2 cho3 I e5 thau5-cheng5 khi3. In chiu7 chhut-hoat, jip8-khi3 chit8 e5 Sat-ma2-li7-a-lang5 e5 hiong-chhoan, boeh ka7 Ia5-sou chun2-pi7 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3.  53) Tan7-si7 hiah-e5 chng-thau5 e5 lang5 bo5 boeh hoan-geng5 Ia5-sou, in-ui7 Ia5-sou beng5-beng5 si7 boeh khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5.  54) I e5 bun5-tou5 Nga2-kok kap Iok-han7 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne, chiu7 kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, Li2 ai3 goan2 kio3 hoe2 tui3 thiN-teng2 kang3 loh8-lai5 ka7 in hui2-biat8 bo5?몯  55) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou oat8 koe3-lai5 chek-pi7 hit nng7 e5 bun5-tou5;  56) I chiu7 kap bun5-tou5 koh khi3 pat8 e5 hiong-chhoan.

Cho3 Ia5-sou e5 bun5-tou5 e5 iau3-kiaN7: (Ma2 8:19-22)
	57) In teh kiaN5-lou7 e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 lang5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Li2 bo5-lun7 khi3 tah-ui7, goa2 long2 boeh toe3 Li2 khi3.몯  58) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2, 몮Hou5-li5 u7 khang, poe-chiau2 u7 siu7; tan7-si7 Jin5-chu2 bo5 an-sin e5 sou2-chai7.몯  59) Ia5-sou koh tui3 leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 lang5 kong2, 몮Lai5 toe3 Goa2.몯 Hit e5 lang5 in3 kong2, 몮Sin-seN a3, hou7 goa2 tai7-seng tng2-khi3 bai5-chiong3 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7.몯  60) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, 몮Pang3 hou7 hiah-e5 cheng-sin5 siong7 e5 si2-lang5 khi3 bai5-chong3 in jiok8-the2-siong7 e5 si2-lang5! Li2 tioh8 khi3 soan-kang2 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok.몯  61) Koh u7 chit8 e5 lang5 kong2, 몮Sin-seN a3, goa2 boeh toe3 Li2; tan7-si7 tai7-seng hou7 goa2 tng2-khi3 chhu3-nih kap ke-lai7 e5 lang5 sio-si5 le3.몯  62) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, 몮Chhiu2 hoaN7 toa3 le5 nih8, tiaN7-tiaN7 oat8-thau5 khoaN3 au7-bin7 e5 lang5, be7 kham-tit cho3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 chu2-bin5.몯

Te7 10 ChiuN

Ia5-sou chhe-phai3 chhit-chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5:
	1) Jian5-au7 Chu2 koh leng7-goa7 keng2 chhit-chap8-ji7 e5 lang5, hou7 in nng7-e5 nng7-e5 cho3 chit8 chou, phai3 in cho3 I e5 thau5-cheng5 khi3-kau3 I ka-ti7 teh-boeh khi3 e5 tak8 e5 siaN5-chhi7 kap kok te7-hng.  2) I ka7 in kong2: 몮Tioh8 siu-seng5 e5 ngou2-kok chin hong-hu3, tan7-si7 kang-lang5 chin chio2. Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 chheng2-kiu5 thau5-ke, phai3 khah-che7 kang-lang5 lai5 ka7 i siu-seng5.  3) TaN lin2 tioh8 khi3! goa2 chhe-phai3 lin2 chhut-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 sang3 ko-iuN5 jip8-khi3 long5-kun5 e5 tiong-kan.  4) Lin2 m7-thang toa3 chiN5-te7-a2, m7-thang toa3 li2-heng5-te7, ia7 m7-thang toa3 e5. Ti7 lou7-nih8 ia7 m7-thang ka7 lang5 chheng2-an.  5) Lin2 bo5-lun7 jip8-khi3 tah chit8 keng chhu3, tioh8 tai7-seng kong2, 몬goan7 chit ke e5 lang5 tit-tioh8 peng5-an!몭  6) Ti7 hia na7 u7 ai3 ho5-peng5 e5 lang5, i chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8 lin2 sou2 kong2 e5 peng5-an; na7 bo5, chit e5 peng5-an chiu7 e7 koh to3-tng2 lai5 lin2 e5 sin-nih.  7) Lin2 tioh8 toa3 hit keng chhu3. Ui7-tioh8 lin2 sou2 chun2-pi7 e5 chiah8-mih8, tioh8 ka7 in theh8 khi2-lai5 chiah8, phang5 khi2-lai5 lim; in-ui7 kang-lang5 eng-kai tit-tioh8 in e5 kang-chiN5. Lin2 m7-thang tui3 chit ke soa2 koe3 hit ke.  8) Bo5-lun7 jip8-khi3 tah chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7, lang5 na7 hoan-geng5 lin2, phang5 chhut-lai5 hou7 lin2 e5 chiah8-mih8, lin2 tioh8 ka7 i chiah8.  9) Tioh8 i-ho2 hit e5 siaN5-chhi7 e5 peN7-lang5; ka7 in kong2, 몬Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok teh-boeh kau3 a3.몭  10) lin2 bo5-lun7 jip8-khi3 tah chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7, lang5 na7 bo5 hoan-geng5 lin2, lin2 tioh8 chhut-khi3 ke-lou7 kong2,  11) 몬Lian5 tiau5 ti7 goan2 e5 kha e5 lin2 siaN5-chhi7 e5 thou5-hun2, goan2 ia7 boeh poaN7 hiat-tiau7 lai5 ka7 lin2 khong3-gi7, tan7-si7 lin2 tioh8 chai, Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok teh-boeh kau3 a3.몭  12) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, Sim2-phoaN3 e5 Jit8-chi2 na7 kau3, Sou2-to-ma2-siaN5 e5 mia7-un7 ia7 be7 pi2 hit e5 siaN5-chhi7 khah chheN-chham2!몯

M7 hoe3-kai2 e5 siaN5-chhi7: (Ma2 11: 20-24)
	13) 몮Ko-liap8-sin3-lang5 a3, lin2 e7 u7 chai-ho7! Pek-sat-tai7-lang5 a3, lin2 e7 u7 chai-ho7! In-ui7 ti7 Chhui-lo5 kap Se-tun3 cho3, in cha2-cha2 chiu7 chheng7 moa5-saN, sam2 hoe2-hu che7-teh hoe3-kai2 a3.  14) Sim2-phoaN3 e5 si5, Chhui-lo5 kap Se-tun3 e7 pi2 lin2 siu7 khah khin e5 heng5-hoat8!  15) Iah li2 Ka-pek-long5 a3! Li2 siuN7-boeh siu7 the5-ko kau3 thiN-teng2 a2 m7-si7? Li2 it-teng7 e7 pi7 tan3 loh8 khi3-kau3 im-kan!몯
	16) 몮ThiaN lin2 e5 oe7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7; khi3-choat8 lin2 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 khi3-choat8 Goa2; khi3-choat8 Goa2 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 khi3-choat8 chhe Goa2 lai5 Hit-ui7.몯

Chhit-chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 e5 po3-ko3:
