	17) Hit chhit-chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 hoaN-hoaN-hi2-hi2 tng2-lai5 kong2: 몮Chu2 a3, goan2 hong7 Li2 e5 mia5 chit8-e7 beng7-leng7, lian5 sia5-mou5 ia7 hok8-chiong5 goan2!몯  18) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Goa2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Sat-tan3 chhin-chhiuN7 sih-na2 tui3 thiN-teng2 poah8 loh8-lai5.  19) Goa2 i2-keng u7 su3 lin2 koan5-leng5 hou7 lin2 e7-tang3 eng7 kha tah8 choa5 kap giat-a2, che3-hok8 tek8-jin5 it-chhe3 e5 koan5-lek8; sou2-i2 se3-kan bo5 chit8 hang7 e7 siong-hai7 tioh8 lin2.  20) Tan7-si7 lin2 m7-thang in-ui7 Mou5-kui2 hok8-chiong5 lin2, lin2 chiu7 lai5 hoaN-hi2; lin2 tioh8 in-ui7 lin2 e5 mia5 i2-keng pi7 ki3-chai3 ti7 thiN-teng2 lai5 hoaN-hi2.몯

Ia5-sou e5 hi2-lok8: (Ma2 11:25-27; 13:16-17)
	21) Hit e5 si5, Seng3 Leng5 hou7 Ia5-sou chhiong-moa2 hi2-lok8, kong2: 몮Hu7-chhin, thiN-te7 e5 Chu2-chaiN2 a3! Goa2 kam2-sia7 Li2, in-ui7 Li2 chiong chiah-e5 su7 tui3 u7 ti3-hui7 kap u7 hak8-bun7 e5 lang5 am-kham3 khi2-lai5, tui3 tan-sun5 e5 lang5 khe2-si7 chhut-lai5. Hu7-chhin a3! Goa2 sit8-chai7 kam2-sia7 Li2, in-ui7 che long2 si7 chiau3 Li2 e5 ho2-i3 lai5 cho3 e5.몯
	22) 몮Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 i2-keng chiong it-chhe3 long2 kau-thok Goa2. Thian-hu7 i2-goa7 bo5 lang5 chin-chiaN3 bat KiaN2. KiaN2 kap KiaN2 sou2 khe2-si7 e5 lang5 i2-goa7, bo5 lang5 chin-chiaN3 bat Thian-hu7.몯
	23) Ia5-sou chiu7 oat8-tng2 sin tiam7-tiam7-a2 ka7 bun5-tou5 kong2: 몮U7 bak8-chiu thang khoaN3-kiN3 lin2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5, sit8-chai7 chin u7 hok-khi3!  24) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, in-ui7 i2-cheng5 u7 chin-che7 tai7-gian5-jin5 kap kun-ong5 chin ai3 khoaN3 lin2 sou2 teh khoaN3 e5, tan7-si7 khoaN3 be7 tioh8; chin ai3 thiaN lin2 sou2 teh thiaN e5, tan7-si7 thiaN be7 tioh8.몯

Ho2-sim e5 Sat-ma2-li7-a-lang5:
	25) U7 chit8 pai2, u7 chit8 e5 Lut8-hoat e5 choan-ka oa2-lai5 chhi3-tham3 Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Lau7-su a3! Goa2 tioh8-ai3 cho3 sim2-mih chiah e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 eng2-seng?몯  26) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, 몮Lut8-hoat e5 lai7-bin7 u7 ki3-chai3 sim2-mih? Iah li2 an3-choaN2 kai2-sek?몯  27) Hit e5 lang5 in3 kong2: 몮Li2 tioh8 choan5-sim, choan5-leng5, choan5-lek8, choan5-i3 ai3 Chu2, Li2 e5 Siong7-chu2; ia7 tioh8 ai3 li2 e5 chhu3-piN chhin-chhiuN7 ai3 li2 ka-ti7.몯  28) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2, 몮Li2 in3 liau2 chin tioh8. Chiau3 an2-ne khi3 cho3 chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8 eng2-seng.몯
	29) Tan7-si7 hit e5 Lut8-hoat e5 choan-ka ui7-tioh8 boeh piau2-beng5 i ka-ti7 u7 li2, chiu7 koh mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Sim2-mih lang5 si7 goa2 e5 chhu3-piN?몯  30) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2: 몮U7 chit8 pai2, u7 chit8 e5 lang5 tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 teh-boeh loh8-khi3 Ia5-li7-ko-siaN5 e5 si5, tu2-tioh8 thou2-hui2; thou2-hui2 ka7 i pak kah khang-khang-khang, iu7-koh ka7 i phah kah poaN3-si2, chiu7 ka7 i pang3 le3, cho3 in khi3.  31) Tu2 u7 chit8 e5 che3-si, tui3 hit tiau5 lou7 loh8-lai5, khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 lang5, chiu7 siam2 tui3 lou7 e5 hit peng5 koe3-khi3.  32) Iu7-koh u7 chit8 e5 Li7-bi7-lang5 lai5-kau3 hit e5 sou2-chai7. I khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 lang5 e5 si5, ia7 siam2 tui3 lou7 e5 hit peng5, cho3 i khi3.  33) Koh u7 chit8 e5 Sat-ma2-li7-a-lang5, li2-heng5 tui3 hia keng-koe3, chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 lang5, chiu7 chin ka7 i tong5-cheng5.  34) I oa2-khi3 hit e5 lang5 hia, eng7 chiu2 ka7 i se2, eng7 iu5 ka7 i boah khang-chhui3, ia7 eng7 pou3 ka7 i pau khi2-lai5, au7-lai5 chiu7 hu5 i khi2-khi3 khia5 toa3 i ka-ti7 e5 li5-a2 teng2, chhoa7 i khi3 kau3 li2-koan2 ka7 i chiau3-kou3.  35) Keh-tng2-jit8, i theh8 nng7 e5 gin5-oan5 kau hou7 li2-koan2 e5 thau5-ke, kau-tai3 i kong2: 몬ChhiaN2 li2 ho2-ho2 ka7 i chiau3-kou3; ban7-it chiN5 na7 eng7 bo5 kau3, goa2 to3-tng2-lai5 e5 si5 e7 pou2 li2.몭몯  36) Ia5-sou kong2 chit e5 phi3-ju7 liau2-au7, chiu7 mng7 hit e5 Lut8-hoat e5 choan-ka kong2: 몮chiau3 li2 siuN7, hit saN e5 lang5 tah chit8 e5 si7 tu2-tioh8 thou2-hui2 hit e5 lang5 e5 chhu3-piN?"몯 37) I in3 kong2, "몮i7 hit e5 tui3 i piau2-si7 jin5-chu5 e5.몯 Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2, 몮Li2 khi3, iah chiau3 an2-ne khi3 cho3.몯

Ia5-sou hong2-bun7 Ma2-tai7 kap Ma2-li7-a:
	38) Ia5-sou kap I e5 bun5-tou5 ke3-siok8 li2-heng5. Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 chit8 e5 hiong-chhoan, u7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 mia5 kio3-cho3 Ma2-tai7, hoan-geng5 Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 in chhu3.  39) Ma2-tai7 u7 chit8 e5 sio2-moe7, mia5 kio3-cho3 Ma2-li7-a. I che7 toa3 Chu2 e5 kha-cheng5, teh thiaN I e5 ka3-si7.  40) Tan7-si7 Ma2-tai7 ui7-tioh8 boeh khoan2-thai7 lang5-kheh tai7-chi3 chin-che7, soah sim-koaN loan7 chhau-chhau. Sou2-i2 i chiu7 lai5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Chu2 a3! Goa2 e5 sio2-moe7 pang3 goa2 ka-ti7 chit8 e5 teh chiap-thai7 lang5-kheh, Li2 kam2 e7-cho3-tit si7 bo5? ChhiaN2 Li2 kio3 i lai5 ka7 goa2 tau3-kha-chhiu2!몯  41) Chu2 chiu7 in3 i kong2: 몮Ma2-tai7, Ma2-tai7, li2 ui7-tioh8 chin-che7 tai7-chi3 teh hoan5-lo2 chhau-hoan5;  42) tan7-si7 sou2 su-iau3 e5 chi2-u7 chit8 hang7 nia7-nia7. Ma2-li7-a i2-keng soan2-tioh8 siong7 ho2 e5 hun7, iu7-koh i hit hun7 be7-eng7-tit ka7 i chhiuN2-khi3.몯

Te7 11 ChiuN

Koan-he7 ki5-to2 e5 kau3-hun3: (Ma2 6:9-13; 7:7-11)
	1) U7 chit8 pai2, Ia5-sou ti7 chit8 e5 sou2-chai7 teh ki5-to2, I ki5-to2 soah e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 bun5-tou5 ka7 I kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, chhin-chhiuN7 Iok-han7 u7 ka3 i e5 bun5-tou5 ki5-to2; chhiaN2 Li2 ia7 ka3 goan2 ki5-to2.몯  2) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2, 몮Lin2 ki5-to2 e5 si5, tioh8 an2-ne ki5-to2:
몬Hu7-chhin a3, Goan7 Li2 e5 mia5 hou7 lang5 chun-tiong7 cho3 chi3-seng3 e5. Goan7 Li2 e5 Ong5-kok lai5-lim5.  3) Kiu5 Li2 siuN2-su3 goan2 mui2-jit8 sou2 su-iau3 e5 chiah8-mih8.  4) Sia3-bian2 goan2 e5 choe7, in-ui7 goan2 ia7 sia3-bian2 it-chhe3 tek-choe7 goan2 e5 lang5. M7-thang hou7 goan2 ham7-loh8 iu2-hek8.몭몯
	5) Ia5-sou iu7-koh ka7 bun5-tou5 kong2: 몮Ka2-su2 lin2 tiong-kan u7 chit8 e5 lang5, poaN3-me5 khi2-kau3 peng5-iu2 in tau, ka7 i kong2, 몬Peng5-iu2 a3, mi7-pau saN ki chioh goa2;  6) in-ui7 goa2 u7 chit8 e5 li7-heng5 tiong e5 peng5-iu2 oat lai5 goan2 tau, goa2 bo5 sim2-mih thang chhiaN2 i.몯  7) Ka2-su2 li2 e5 peng5-iu2 tui3 chhu3 e5 lai7-bin7 in3 kong2, 몬Li2 m7-thang lai5 chha2 goa2! Mng5 i2-keng so2 khi2-lai5 a3. Goa2 e5 gin2-na2 kap goa2 i2-keng teh khun3 a3. Goa2 be7-tang3 khi2-lai5 theh8 hou7 li2.몭  8) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, sui-jian5 i be7 tai3-liam7 tioh8 peng5-iu2-cheng5 khi2-lai5 theh8 mi7-pau hou7 li2, ia7 e7 ui7-tioh8 li2 m7-kiaN kian3-siau3 ke3-siok8 ka7 i khun2-kiu5, i chiu7 e7 peh khi2-lai5 theh8 li2 sou2 su-iau3 e5 mih8 hou7 Li2.  9) Sou2-i2 goa2 ka7 lin2 kong, tioh8 kiu5, lin2 chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8; tioh8 chhoe7, lin2 chiu7 e7 chhoe7-tioh8; tioh8 phah-mng5, chiu7 e7 ka7 lin2 khui.  10) In-ui7 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 na7 kiu5, chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8; na7 chhoe7, chiu7 e7 chhoe7-tioh8; na7 phah-mng5, chiu7 e7 ka7 i khui.  11) Lin2 cho3 lau7-pe7 e5 lang5, ka-ti7 e5 kiaN2 ka7 lin2 tho2 hi5-a2 e5 si5, lin2 kam2 e7 liah8 choa5 hou7 i?  12) A2-si7 ka7 lin2 tho2 ke-nng7 e5 si5, lin2 kam2 e7 liah8 giat-a2 hou7 i?  13) Lin2 sui-jian5 si7 phaiN2 e5 lang5, siong7-chhiaN2 e7-hiau2 chiong ho2-mih8 hou7 lin2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, ho5-hong3 lin2 e5 Thian-hu7, I kam2 be7 chiong Seng3 Leng5 lai5 siuN2-su3 hou7 hiah-e5 tui3 I ki5-kiu5 e5 lang5?몯

Ia5-sou kap kui2-ong5 Piat8-se-pok: (Ma2 12:22-30; Kho2 3:20-27)
	14) Ia5-sou teh koaN2 chau2 chit8 e5 e2-kau2 e5 sia5-mou5. Sia5-mou5 chit8-e7 chhut-khi3, hit e5 lang5 chiu7 e7 kong2-oe7. cheng3-lang5 long2 chin tioh8-kiaN.  15) Tan7-si7 ki5-tiong u7 lang5 kong2, 몮I put-ko3 si7 kho3 kui2-ong5 Piat8-se-pok e5 leng5-lek8 lai5 teh koaN2 kui2.몯  16) Ia7 u7 chit8-koa2 lang5 boeh chhi3-tham3 Ia5-sou, iau-kiu5 I cho3 chit8 e5 tui3 thiN-teng2 lai5 e5 sin5-chek hou7 in khoaN3.  17) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou chai-iaN2 in e5 sim-su7, chiu7 tui3 in kong2: 몮Kok-ka na7 khi2 lai7-loan7, it-teng7 e7 biat8-bong5; ka-teng5 na7 khi2 lai7-loan7, it-teng7 e7 long7-ke-soaN3-theh8.  18) Sat-tan3 na7 ka-ti7 kong-kek ka-ti7, an2-ne Sat-tan3 e5 ong5-kok kam2 khia7 e7 tiau5? Lin2 kong2 Goa2 kho3 Piat8-se-pok e5 se3-lek8 lai5 koaN2-kui2.  19) Goa2 na7-si7 kho3 Piat8-se-pok e5 se3-lek8 lai5 koaN2-kui2, an2-ne lin2 e5 tou5-te7 si7 kho3 sim2-mih lang5 e5 se3-lek8 lai5 koaN2-kui2? Lin2 ka-ti7 e5 tou5-te7 e7 hoan2-pok lin2 e5 koan-tiam2!  20) Tan7-si7 Goa2 si7 oa2-kho3 Siong7-chu2 e5 koan5-leng5 lai5 teh koaN2-kui2 e5, an2-ne si7 cheng3-beng5 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok i2-keng lai5-kau3 lin2 e5 tiong-kan a.몯
	21) 몮Iong2-chong3 e5 lang5 na7 oan5-choan5 bu2-chong teh kou3-siu2 ka-ti7 e5 chhu3, i it-chhe3 e5 chai5-but8 chiah e7 an-choan5.  22) Tan7-si7 na7 u7 chit8 e5 pi2 i koh-khah iong2 e5 lang5 lai5 ka7 i kong-kek, phah-iaN5 i, chiu7 e7 chiong i sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 bu2-chong ka7 i pak khi2-lai5, ia7 e7 chiong sou2 chhiuN2 lai5 e5 chai5-but8 pun-pun khi3.몯
	23) 몮Na7 bo5 kap Goa2 kang7 sim-chi3 e5, chiu7-si7 hoan2-tui3 Goa2; bo5 hiap8-chou7 Goa2 e5 kang-chok e5, chiu7-si7 teh pho3-hoai7.몯

Sia5-sin5 to3 tng2-lai5: (Ma2 12:43-45)
	24) 몮Sia5-sin5 li7-khui lang5 liau2-au7, chiu7 khi3 khong3-ia2 si3-ke3 chhoe7 chit8 e5 sou2-chai7 thang boeh hiu-sek. I chit8-e7 chhoe7 bo5 chiu7 kong2, 몬Goa2 boeh to3 tng2-khi3 goa2 chhut-lai5 e5 chhu3.몭  25) I tng2-khi3 kau3 hia, khoaN3-kiN3 chhu3-lai7 sau3 kah chin chheng-khi3, ia7 cheng2-li2 kah chin ho2-se3.  26) I chiu7 koh chhut-khi3, chhoa7 chhit e5 pi2 i khah sia5-ok e5 lai5, jip8-khi3 hia cho3-hoe2 toa3. Hit e5 lang5 e5 kiat-kiok8 chiu7 pi2 i2-cheng5 koh-khah pi-chham2.몯

Chin-sit8 e5 hok-khi3:
	27) Ia5-sou teh kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan u7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, toa7 siaN tui3 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Hoai5-in7 Li2, ka7 Li2 chhi7-leng e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3!몯  28) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou in3 kong2, 몮ThiaN Siong7-chu2 e5 oe7, lai5 chun-siu2 e5 lang5, koh-khah u7 hok-khi3!몯

Iau--kiu5 sin5-chek: (Ma2 12:38-42)
	29) Cheng3-lang5 it-tit8 ui5 oa2-lai5 Ia5-sou e5 seng-khu piN e5 si5, Ia5-sou chiu7 ke3-siok8 ka7 in kong2: 몮Chit e5 se3-tai7 e5 lang5, na2 e7 chiah-nih sia5-ok! In iau-kiu5 Goa2 cho3 sin5-chek hou7 in khoaN3, tan7-si7 Iok-na2 e5 sin5-chek i2-goa7, Siong7-chu2 bo5 boeh siuN2-su3 sin5-chek hou7 chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 khoaN3!  30) Tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 tai7-gian5-jin5 Iok-na2 chiaN5-cho3 chit8 chiong2 e5 sin5-chek lai5 hou7 Ni5-ni5-bi5-lang5 khoaN3, kap an2-ne kang7-khoan2, Jin5-chu2 ia7 e7 chiaN5-cho3 chit8 e5 sin5-chek lai5 hou7 chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 khoaN3.  31) Chai7 sim2-phoaN3 e5 Jit8-chi2, Lam5-hong e5 Li2-ong5 e7 kap chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 cho3-hoe2 oah8 khi2-lai5 khong3-ko3 chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5, in-ui7 i u7 tui3 thiN-piN hai2-kak lai5 thiaN Sou2-lo5-bun5-ong5 ti3-hui7 e5 oe7. Lin2 khoaN3, ti7 chia u7 pi2 Sou2-lo5-bun5-ong5 koh-khah ui2-tai7 e5!  32) Chai7 sim2-phoaN3 e5 Jit8-chi2, Ni5-ni5-bi5-lang5 e7 khia7 khi2-lai5 khong3-ko3 lin2, in-ui7 Ni5-ni5-bi5-lang5 thiaN Iok-na2 e5 thoan5-to7 liau2-au7 long2 u7 hoe3-kai2. Lin2 khoaN3, ti7 chia u7 pi2 Iok-na2 koh-khah ui2-tai7 e5!몯

Bak8-chiu si7 seng-khu e5 kng: (Ma2 5:15; 6:22-23)
	33) 몮Bo5 lang5 tiam2-teng khng3 toa3 bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 sou2-chai7, a2-si7 kham3 toa3 bi2-tau2 lai7; long2 si7 chhai7 toa3 teng-hoe2-tai5, thang hou7 jip8-lai5 e5 lang5 e7-tang3 khoaN3-kiN3 kng.  34) Li2 e5 bak8-chiu chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 e5 seng-khu e5 teng-hoe2. Li2 e5 bak8-chiu na7 kim, li2 kui seng-khu chiu7 e7 kng; tan7-si7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu na7 hoe, li2 kui seng-khu chiu7 e7 ou-am3.  35) Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 chu3-i3 m7-thang hou7 li2 lai7-sim e5 kng ou-am3 khi3.  36) Li2 kui seng-khu na7 chhiong-moa2 kong-beng5, lian5 chit8 tiam2-a2 ou-am3 to bo5, tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 teng-hoe2 teh ka7 lin2 chio3-kng, an2-ne li2 e5 seng-khu chiu7 e7 long2 kng khi2-lai5.몯

Ia5-sou chek-pi7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 kap Keng-hak8-chia2: (Ma2 23:1-36; Kho2 12:38-40)
	37) Ia5-sou chiah-e5 oe7 tu2 kong2 soah e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 chhiaN2 Ia5-sou khi3 in chhu3 chiah8-png7. Ia5-sou chiu7 jip8-khi3 che7-toh.  38) Hit e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou boeh chiah8-png7 i2-cheng5 bo5 chiau3 hoat-tou7 tai7-seng se2 chhiu2, kam2-kak chin ki5-koai3.  39) Chu2 chiu7 ka7 i kong2: 몮Lin2 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 chi2-u7 chiong te5-au-a2 kap oaN2-poaN5 e5 goa7-bin7 chhit kah chin chheng-khi3, m7-ku2 lin2 e5 lai7-bin7 chhiong-moa2 tham-iok8 kap sia5-ok!  40) Lin2 chiah-e5 gong7-lang5 a3! Siong7-chu2 chhong3-cho7 goa7-bin7, kam2 m7-si7 ia7 chhong3-cho7 te2 ti7 lai7-bin7 e5?  41) Lin2 na7 chiong lin2 sou2 u7 e5 lai5 chin2-che3 lang5, an2-ne lin2 e5 it-chhe3 ia7 chu7-jian5 e7 chheng-khi3.몯
	42) 몮Lin2 chiah-e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! In-ui7 lin2 chiau3 koan3-le7 to u7 teh hong7-hian3 chap8-hun chi it e5 phang-liau7 --- chhin-chhiuN7 poh8-ho5, hoe5-hiang-a2 i2-kip8 kok chiong2 e5 ioh8-chhau2 hou7 Siong7-chu2, tan7-si7 lin2 long2 bu5-si7 kong-gi7 kap keng3-ai3 Siong7-chu2. Chiah-e5 ka3-si7 it-teng7 tioh8 sit8-heng5, tan7-si7 thau5-cheng5 sou2 theh8-khi2 e5 koan3-le7 ia7 m7-thang hut-liok8.몯
	43) 몮Lin2 chiah-e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! In-ui7 lin2 ti7 hoe7-tng5 lai7 ai3 che7 toa7 ui7, ti7 ke-chhi7 ai3 hou7 lang5 kiaN5 toa7-le2.  44) Lin2 tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! In-ui7 lin2 chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 lang5 khoaN3 be7 chhut e5 bong7; lang5 tui3 bin7-teng2 kiaN5-koe3 ia7 long2 m7 chai-iaN2.몯
	45) U7 chit8 e5 Lut8-hoat e5 choan-ka ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Lau7-su, Li2 kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 ia7 bu2-jiok8 tioh8 goan2.몯  46) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2: 몮Lian5 lin2 chiah-e5 Lut8-hoat e5 choan-ka ia7 tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! In-ui7 lin2 chiong taN bo5 hoat-tit e5 tang7-taN3 hou7 lang5 taN, tan7-si7 ka-ti7 lian5 chit8 ki chng2-thau5-a2 ia7 m7-kheng2 tin2-tang7, lai5 kiam2-khin in e5 tang7-taN3.  47) Lin2 tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! Lin2 kian3-cho7 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 bong7; tan7-si7 thai5-si2 hiah-e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5, chiu7-si7 lin2 e5 chou2-sian.  48) An2-ne lin2 ka-ti7 lai5 seng5-jin7, ia7 lai5 chan3-seng5 lin2 chou2-sian sou2 cho3 e5; in-ui7 in thai5-si2 tai7-gian5-jin5. lin2 lai5 ka7 in kian3-cho7 bong7.  49) Sou2-i2 Siong7-chu2 e5 tih3ui kong2: 몬Goa2 boeh chhe-phai3 tai7-gian5-jin5 kap su3-tou5 khi3 in hia. Ki5-tiong u7-e5 e7 hou7 in sat-hai7, ia7 u7-e5 e7 hou7 in pek-hai7.'몭 50) An2-ne tui3 chhong3-cho7 se3-kai3 i2-lai5, chiong3 tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 lau5 e5 hoeh, chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 long2 tioh8 heng5 hiat-che3,  51) chiu7-si7 tui3 A-pek sou2 lau5 e5 hoeh khi2, it-tit8 kau3 ti7 che3-toaN5 kap seng3-sou2 e5 tiong-kan siu7 sat-hai7 e5 Sat-ka-li7-a e5 hoeh ui5-chi2. goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 long2 heng5 hiah-e5 lang5 e5 hiat-che3.몯
	52) 몮Lin2 chiah-e5 Lut8-hoat e5 choan-ka, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! In-ui7 lin2 chiong khui ti3-sek e5 mng5 e5 so2-si5 ka7 lang5 giah8 khi2-lai5; lin2 ka-ti7 m7 jip8-khi3 bo5 iau3-kin2, siong7-chhiaN2 hiah-e5 boeh jip8-khi3 e5 lang5, lin2 ia7 ka7 in chou2-tong3.몯
	53) Ia5-sou tui3 hit keng chhu3 chhut-lai5 e5 si5, hiah-e5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 khai-si2 kek8-lek8 kong-kek I, pek I hoe5-tap chin-che7 bun7-te5,  54) lai5 tng-tan2 I kong2 m7-tioh8 oe7, boeh liah8 I e5 oe7-phang7.

Te7 12 ChiuN

Keng2-kai3 gui7-sian7-chia2: (Ma2 10:26-27)
	1) Hit e5 si5, seng5-chhian seng5-ban7 e5 lang5 chhih8 oa2-khi3, soah tai7-ke tah8-lai5 tah8-khi3. Ia5-sou chiu7 tai7-seng tui3 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: 몮Tioh8 hong5-pi7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 kaN3-bo2, i3-su3 chiu7-si7 hong5-pi7 in e5 gui7-sian7.  2) Mui2 chit8 hang7 kham3-bat8 e5 su7, au7-lai5 it-teng7 e7 lou7-hian7 chhut-lai5; mui2 chit8 hang7 pi3-bit8 e5 su7, au7-lai5 ia7 it-teng7 e7 hou7 lang5 chai-iaN2.  3) Sou2-i2 lin2 ti7 am3-tiong sou2 kong2 e5, it-teng7 e7 toa3 kng-thiN peh8-jit8 e5 sou2-chai7 hou7 lang5 thiaN-tioh8. Lin2 ti7 pang5-keng-lai7 kau-thau5 chiap-hiN7 sou2 kong2 e5, ia7 e7 toa3 chhu3-teng2 kong-khai soan-pou3 chhut-lai5.몯

Tioh8 keng3-ui3 Siong7-chu2: (Ma2 10:28-31)
	4) 몮Peng5-iu2 a3! Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, sat-hai7 lang5 e5 jiok8-sin liau2-au7, be7-tang3 cho3 koh-khah ok-tok8 e5 tai7-chi3 e5 lang5, lin2 m7-bian2 kiaN in.  5) Goa2 boeh chi2-si7 lin2 tioh8 ai3 kiaN sim2-mih lang5: tioh8 kiaN Siong7-chu2. I ka7 lang5 thai5-si2 liau2-au7, iau2 u7 koan5-peng3 thang ka7 lang5 hiat loh8-khi3 te7-gak8. Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, tioh8 kiaN Hit-ui7!몯
	6) 몮Gou7 chiah chhek-chiau2-a2 kam2 m7-si7 be7 nng7 kak-gin5? Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 lian5 chit8 chiah ia7 bo5 be7-ki3-tit.  7) Put-tan7 an2-ne, Siong7-chu2 lian5 lin2 e5 thau5-mng5 ia7 long2 chit8-ki chit8-ki ka7 lin2 sng3-koe3 a3.  Sou2-i2 m7-bian2 kiaN; in-ui7 lin2 pi2 kui tin7 e5 chhek-chiau2-a2 koh-khah u7 ke3-tat8!몯

Seng5-jin7 Ki-tok kap ki7-choat8 Ki-tok: (Ma2 10:32-33; 12:32; 10:19-20)
	8) 몮Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, it-chhe3 ti7 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 kong-khai seng5-jin7 Goa2 e5 lang5, Jin5-chu2 ia7 boeh toa3 Siong7-chu2 e5 thian-sai3 e5 bin7-cheng5 seng5-jin7 i.  9) Tan7-si7 it-chhe3 ti7 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 m7 seng5-jin7 Goa2 e5 lang5, Jin5-chu2 toa3 Siong7-chu2 e5 thian-sai3 e5 bin7-cheng5, ia7 m7 seng5-jin7 i.몯
	10) 몮Lang5 na7 kong2-oe7 kong-kek Jin5-chu2, iau2 e7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2, tan7-si7 siat-tok8 tioh8 Seng3 Leng5 e5 lang5, chiu7 be7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2.몯
	11) 몮Lang5 na7 ah lin2 khi3-kau3 hoe7-tng5, a2-si7 thong2-ti7-chia2 kap cheng3-hu2 koaN-oan5 e5 bin7-cheng5, lin2 m7-bian2 hoan5-lo2 boeh an3-choaN2 tap-pian7, a2-si7 boeh kong2 sim2-mih.  12) In-ui7 kau3 hit e5 si5, Seng3 Leng5 e7 ka3 lin2 tioh8 kong2 sim2-mih.몯

Gong7 hu3-hou7 e5 phi3-ju7:
	13) Cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan u7 chit8 e5 lang5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Lau7-su, chhiaN2 Li2 kio3 goa2 e5 a-hiaN chiong goa2 e5 hun7 e5 ui5-san2 pun hou7 goa2.몯  14) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, 몮Li2 chit e5 lang5 a3, sim2-mih lang5 jim7-beng7 Goa2 cho3 lin2 e5 kong-chhin?몯  15) I chiu7 tui3 cheng3-lang5 kong2: 몮Tioh8 chu3-i3, tioh8 keng2-kai3 it-chhe3 e5 tham-iok8, in-ui7 lang5 bo5-lun7 loa7-nih ho2-giah8, i e5 sit8-chai7 e5 seN3-mia7 m7-si7 kai3-chai7 ti7 i e5 chai5-san2.몯  15) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou eng7 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7 ka7 in kong2: 몮U7 chit8 e5 ho2-giah8-lang5, i e5 chhan5-hng5 chin hong-siu.  17) I sim-lai7 khai-si2 siuN7 kong2, 몬TaN boeh an3-choaN2, in-ui7 goa2 soah bo5 kau3 sou2-chai7 thang tun2 goa2 e5 ngou2-kok.몭  18) Choe3-au7 i chiu7 kong2, 몬Goa2 boeh an2-ne cho3, boeh thiah goa2 e5 chhek-chhng, koh khi2 khah toa7 keng e5, lai5 tun2 goa2 e5 ngou2-kok kap it-chhe3 e5 chai5-but8 toa3 hia.  19) Jian5-au7 goa2 boeh tui3 goa2 pun2-sin kong2: li2 u7 tun2-chek chin-che7 chai5-but8, u7 kau3 eng7 chin-che7 ni5; taN thang chheng-eng5 lou3; tioh8 lim tioh8 chiah8, tioh8 hiong2-siu7 lou3!몭  20) Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 ka7 i kong2, 몬Gong7-lang5 a3! Eng-am3 chiu7 boeh siu-hoe5 li2 e5 seN3-mia7; na7 an2-ne li2 ui7-tioh8 ka-ti7 sou2 chek-thiok e5 it-chhe3 boeh lau5 hou7 sim2-mih lang5?몭몯  21) Ia5-sou choe3-au7 kong2, 몮Ui7-tioh8 ka-ti7 chek-thiok chai5-hu3, tan7-si7 chai7 Siong7-chu2 e5 gan2-tiong m7-si7 hu3-ju7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne.몯

Sin3-kho3 Siong7-chu2: (Ma2 6:25-34)
	22) Ia5-sou iu7-koh tui3 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: 몮In-ui7 an2-ne, Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: m7-thang ui7-tioh8 lin2 e5 seN3-mia7 hoan5-lo2 boeh chiah8 sim2-mih, a2-si7 ui7-tioh8 lin2 e5 seng-khu hoan5-lo2 boeh chheng7 sim2-mih.  23) Se3-mia7 pi2 chiah8-mih8 khah u7 ke3-tat8. Seng-khu pi2 saN-khou3 khah u7 ke3-tat8.  24) Lin2 khoaN3 ou-a! Sui-jian5 bo5 cheng3-choh, bo5 siu-seng5, bo5 chhek-chhng, ia7 bo5 chhng-khou3; siong7-chhiaN2 Siong7-chu2 ia7 teh ka7 in iuN2-chhi7! Lin2 kam2 bo5 pi2 hiah-e5 chiau2-a2 ke chin kui3-tiong7?  25) Lin2 sim2-mih lang5 ui7 lin2 e5 hoe3-siu7 lai5 chhau-hoan5 chiu7 e7-tang3 ke oah8 chit8 tiap-a2 ku2?  26) TaN lin2 ki3-jian5 lian5 chiah-nih8 se3-hang7 e5 tai7-chi3 to cho3 be7 lai5, an3-choaN2 tioh8 chhau-hoan5 ki5-tha e5 tai7-chi3?  27) Lin2 siuN7 khoaN3 bai7 le3, ia2-seng e5 pek-hap8-hoe an3-choaN2 teh toa7 chang5: in bo5 phang2-se, ia7 bo5 chit-pou3. Tan7-si7 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, lian5 hiah-nih8 eng5-hoa5 hu3-kui3 e5 Sou2-lo5-bun5-ong5 ma7 m7-bat chheng7-tioh8 pi2 chiah-e5 hoe e5 chit8-lui2 koh-khah sui2 e5 saN.  28) Kin-na2-jit8 teh oah8, bin5-na2-chai3 hou7 lang5 hiat loh8-khi3 hoe2-lou5 e5 ia2-seng e5 hoe-chhau2, Siong7-chu2 siong7-chhiaN2 to an2-ne teh ka7 in chng-chhah, I kam2 be7 koh-khah ka7 lin2 khoaN3-kou3? Lin2 na2 e7 chiah-nih8 bo5 sin3-sim?  29) Sou2-i2 lin2 m7-thang tiaN7-tiaN7 siuN7-boeh chiah8 sim2-mih, lim sim2-mih; ia7 m7-thang chhau-hoan5 khoa3-sim.  30) (In-ui7 chiah-e5 long2 si7 chit se3-kan e5 bi7-sin3-chia2 sou2 teh tui-kiu5 e5.) Lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 chai-iaN2 lin2 u7 su-iau3 chiah-e5 mih8-kiaN7.  31) Lin2 leng5-kho2 tioh8 tui-kiu5 I e5 Kok; I chu7-jian5 ia7 e7 chiong ki5-tha e5 mih8 siuN2-su3 lin2.몯

ThiN-teng2 e5 chai5-hu3: (Ma2 6:19-21)
	32) 몮Lin2 sio2-sio2 e5 iuN5-kun5 a3, m7-bian2 kiaN! In-ui7 lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 hoaN-hi2 boeh siuN2-su3 I e5 Kok hou7 lin2.  33) Tioh8 be7 lin2 e5 chai5-but8 lai5 chin2-che3 san3-chhiah-lang5. Tioh8 ui7-tioh8 lin2 ka-ti7 pi7-pan7 long2 be7 phoa3-khi3 e5 chiN5-te7-a2, iu7-koh tioh8 chek-thiok bu5-kiong5-chin7 e5 chai5-hu3 toa3 thiN-teng2. Ti7 hia bo5 chit8 e5 chhat8-a2 thau-theh8 e7 tioh8, ia7 bo5 chiu3-thang5 e7 lai5 ka7.  34) In-ui7 lin2 e5 chai5-po2 na7 ti7 hia, lin2 e5 sim it-teng7 e7 ti7 hia.몯

Sio2-sim e5 lou5-pok8:
	35) 몮Lin2 e5 saN tioh8 chheng7 hou7 pih-chah, teng tioh8 tiam2 hou7 toh8.  36) Lin2 tioh8 chhin-chhiuN7 pok8-jin5 teh theng3-hau7 chu2-lang5 tui3 hun-ian3 tng2-lai5. Chu2-lang5 tng2-lai5 e5 si5, chit8-e7 phah-mng5, chiu7 sui5-si5 thang ka7 i khui-mng5.  37) Chu2-lang5 tng2-lai5 e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 pok8-jin5 chheN2-chheN2, an2-ne pok8-jin5 chiu7 sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3! Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, chu2-lang5 e7 ka-ti7 ha5 ui5-su-kun5, chhiaN2 in che7 toh, lai5 ka7 in su-hau7.  38) Ka2-su2 chu2-lang5 poaN3-me5 a2-si7 thiN boeh-kng e5 si5 tng2-lai5, khoaN3-kiN3 iong7-lang5 chun2-pi7 pian7-pian7, an2-ne iong7-lang5 sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3!  39) Lin2 tioh8-ai3 chai-iaN2 chit e5 tai7-chi3! Ka2-su2 chu2-lang5 chai-iaN2 kiong5-to7 sim2-mih si5 boeh lai5, i it-teng7 bo5 hou7 kiong5-to7 chhim-jip8 lai5 i e5 chhu3.  40) Sou2-i2 lin2 ia7 tioh8 chun2-pi7 pian7-pian7, in-ui7 lin2 liau7-siong2 be7 kau3 e5 si5, Jin5-chu2 chiu7 e7 lai5.몯

Tiong-sit8 kap bo5 tiong-sit8 e5 lou5-pok8: (Ma2 24:45-51)
	41) Pi2-tek kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, Li2 kong2 chit e5 phi3-ju7 si7 ui7-tioh8 goan2, a2-si7 ui7-tioh8 cheng3-lang5?몯   42) Chu2 in3 kong2: 몮An2-ne, kiu3-keng3 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 lang5 chiah si7 tiong-sit8 koh chhong-beng5 e5 koan2-ke e5? Chiu7-si7, chu2-lang5 jim7-beng7 i lai5 koan2-li2 ki5-tha e5 lou5-pok8, chiau3 si5 hun-phoe3 chiah8-mih8 hou7 in hit e5.  43) I e5 chu2-lang5 tng2-lai5 e5 si5, khoaN3-tioh8 i u7 chiau3 an2-ne teh cho3, hit e5 lou5-pok8 chiu7 sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3!  44) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, chu2-lang5 e7 chiong it-chhe3 e5 chai5-san2 ui2-thok i koan2-li2.  45) Tan7-si7 na7-si7 hit e5 lou5-pok8 ka-ti7 sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2, 몬Goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 tioh8 koh chin ku2 chiah e7 tng2-lai5,몭 i chiu7 khai-si2 phah ki5-tha e5 cha-pou cha-bou2 e5 lou5-pok8, iu7-koh it-tit8 chiah8 it-tit8 lim, lim kah chiu2-chui3.  46) Hit e5 lou5-pok8 bo5 gi5-gou7 e5 jit8, siuN7 be7 kau3 e5 si5, i e5 chu2-lang5 e7 tng2-lai5. Chu2-lang5 e7 tang7-tang7 ka7 i heng5-hoat8, chiong i e5 te7-ui7 ka7 i kang3 loh8-khi3 kap hiah-e5 bo5 tiong-sit8 e5 lang5 kang7-khoan2.몯
	47) 몮Beng5-beng5 chai-iaN2 i e5 chu2-lang5 ai3 i cho3 sim2-mih, ia7 bo5 boeh chun2-pi7, koh bo5 siuN7-boeh chiau3 chu2-lang5 e5 i3-su3 khi3 cho3, chit khoan2 lou5-pok8, chu2-lang5 it-teng7 e7 eng7 piN ka7 i phah kah chin li7-hai7.  48) Tan7-si7 m7 chai-iaN2 chu2-lang5 ai3 i cho3 sim2-mih, khi3 cho3 eng7-kai tioh8 hou7 lang5 phah e5 tai7-chi3, chit e5 lou5-pok8, chu2-lang5 it-teng7 e7 ka7 i phah khah chio2 e7. Siong7-chu2 siuN2-su3 i chin-che7 e5 lang5, e7 tui3 i iau-kiu5 chin-che7; kau-tai3 i lu2 che7 e5 lang5, e7 tui3 i iau-kiu5 lu2 che7.몯

Ia5-sou e7 in2-khi2 hun-liat8: (Ma210:34-36)
	49) 몮Goa2 lai5 si7 boeh tan3 hoe2 toa3 te7-siong7. Hit e5 hoe2 na7 i2-keng toh8 khi2-lai5 a3, m7-chai loa7-nih ho2!  50) Goa2 iau2-ku2 tioh8 siu7 chit8 e5 se2-le2. Chit e5 se2-le2 iau2-boe7 oan5-seng5 i2-cheng5, Goa2 tioh8 loa7-nih siu7-khou2!  51) Lin2 siuN7 kong2 goa2 lai5 si7 boeh hou7 te7-siong7 ho5-peng5 si7 bo5? Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, m7-si7 ho5-peng5, tian-to3 si7 hun-cheng.  52) Tui3 hian7-chai7 khi2, chit8 ke na7 u7 gou7 e5 lang5, in e7 hun-liat8; saN e5 hoan2-tui3 nng7 e5, a2-si7 nng7 e5 hoan2-tui3 saN e5.  53) Lau7-pe7 hoan2-tui3 kiaN2, kiaN2 ngou2-gek8 lau7-pe7; lau7-bo2 hoan2-tui3 cha-bou2-kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2 hoan2-khong3 lau7-bo2; ta-ke hoan2-tui3 sim-pu7, sim-pu7 hoan2-gek8 ta-ke.몯

Liau2-kai2 hit e5 si5 e5 chian5-tiau7: (Ma2 16:2-3)
	54) Ia5-sou iu7-koh ka7 cheng3-lang5 kong2: 몮Lin2 khoaN3-kiN3 hun5 tui3 sai-peng5 khi2-lai5 e5 si5, lin2 sui5-si5 kong2, 몬Teh-boeh loh8-hou7 a7,몭 chiu7 chiaN-sit8 loh8-hou7.  55) Lin2 khoaN3-kiN3 thau3 lam5-hong e5 si5, lin2 chiu7 kong2, 몬Teh-boeh sio-joah8 a7;몭 chiu7 chiaN-sit8 sio-joah8.  56) gui7-sian7-chia2 a3! Lin2 e7-hiau2 hun-piat8 thiN-te7 e5 khi3-siong7, an3-choaN2 be7 liau2-kai2 hian7-chai7 si7 sim2-mih si5-ki5?몯

Tioh8 kap li2 e5 tek8-jin5 ho5-kai2: (Ma2 5:25-26)
	57) 몮Lin2 an3-choaN2 bo5 boeh ka-ti7 phoaN3-toan3 sim2-mih si7 cheng3-tong e5 tai7-chi3?  58) Na7 u7 lang5 khong3-ko3 li2, boeh kap li2 khi3 hoat-iN7, iau2 ti7 lou7-nih8 e5 si5, li2 tioh8 chin7-lek8 siat-hoat kap i ho5-kai2; na7 bo5, i e7 thoa li2 khi3-kau3 phoaN3-koaN e5 bin7-cheng5, phoaN3-koaN e7 chiong li2 kau hou7 hoat-keng3, hoat-keng3 e7 ka7 li2 koaiN loh8 kaN-gak8!  59) Goa2 ka7 li2 kong2, choe3-au7 e5 chit8 sian2-chiN5 li2 na7 bo5 heng5 kah chheng-chheng-chho2-chho2, li2 it-teng7 be7-tang3 tui3 hia chhut-lai5.몯

Te7 13 ChiuN

Tioh8 hoe3-kai2, Na7 bo5, e7 biat8-bong5:
	1) Tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5, u7 kui2-na7 e5 lang5 lai5, tui3 Ia5-sou kong2-khi2 Pi2-liap8-to u7 sat-hai7 chit8-koa2-a2 ti7 che3-toaN5 hian3-che3 e5 Ka-li7-li7-lang5 e5 tai7-chi3.  2) Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: 몮In-ui7 chiah-e5 Ka-li7-li7-lang5 hou7 lang5 an2-ne ka7 in sat-hai7, lin2 chiu7 siuN7 kong2 in e5 choe7-ko3 pi2 ki5-tha it-chhe3 e5 Ka-li7-li7-lang5 khah tang7 si7 bo5?  3) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2; su7-sit8 m70si7 an2-ne. Lin2 na7 m7 hoe3-kai2, long2 e7 chhin-chhiuN7 in an2-ne biat8-bong5.  4) A2-si7 lin2 siuN7 kong2, Se-lo5-a e5 thah to2 loh8-khi3 e5 si5, hou7 i teh-si2 hit chap8-peh e5 lang5, in e5 choe7-ko3 pi2 ki5-tha it-chhe3 toa3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 chu7-bin5 khah tang7 si7 bo5?  5) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2; su7-sit8 m7-si7 an2-ne. Lin2 na7 m7 hoe3-kai2, long2 e7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne biat8-bong5.몯

Bo5 kiat koe2-chi2 e5 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7:
	6) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 in kong2 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7: 몮U7 chit8 e5 lang5, ti7 i e5 phu5-to5-hng5 cheng3 chit8 chang5 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7. I lai5 boeh khoaN3 hit chang5 chhiu7 u7 kiat koe2-chi2 a2 bo5, tan7-si7 chhoe7 long2 bo5.  7) Chiu7 tui3 koan2-li2 phu5-to5-hng5 e5 lang5 kong2,몭Li2 khoaN3, goa2 lian5-lian5 saN ni5 lai5 chit chang5 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7 chhoe7 koe2-chi2, chhoe7 long2 bo5! Tioh8 ka7 i chho3 khi2-lai5! An3-choaN2 tioh8 ka7 i lau5 le2 tin3 sou2 chai7?몭  8) Tan7-si7 hit e5 koan2-li2-jin5 in3 kong2, 몬Thau5-ke a3, koh ka7 i lau5 chit8 ni5, goa2 boeh tui3 si3-piN kut8 kau-a2, loh8 pui5.  9) Me5-ni5 na7 u7 kiat koe2-chi2 chiu7 ho2; na7 bo5, chiah ka7 i chho3 khi2-lai5.몯

Ia5-sou chai7 An-hioh-jit8 i-ho2 chit8 e5 phoa3-siuN3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5:
	10) U7 chit8 e5 An-hioh-jit8, Ia5-sou ti7 chit8 e5 hoe7-tng5 lai7 teh ka3-si7 lang5.  11) U7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 in-ui7 tioh8-iau phoa3-peN7 chap8-peh ni5. I soah khiau-ku, seng-khu chhun long2 be7 tit8.  12) Ia5-sou khoaN3-kiN3 i, chiu7 kio3 i oa2-lai5, ka7 i kong2, 몮Hu7-jin5-lang5 a3! TaN li2 e5 peN7 i2-keng ho2-khi3 a3!몯  13) Ia5-sou chit8-e7 ka7 i an3-chhiu2, i e5 seng-khu chek-si5 chhun-tit8 khi2-lai5, i chiu7 chheng-chan3 Siong7-chu2.  14) Tan7-si7 hoe7-tng5-tiuN2, in-ui7 Ia5-sou chai7 An-hioh-jit8 ka7 lang5 i-peN7, chiu7 chin siu7-khi3, ka7 cheng3-lang5 kong2, 몮Chit8 le2-pai3 e5 tiong-kan u7 lak8-jit8 thang cho3 khang-khoe3, sou2-i2 chai7 chit e5 tiong-kan lin2 thang lai5 i-peN7, tan7-si7 m7-thang chai7 An-hioh-jit8 lai5 hou7 lang5 i-peN7!몯  15) Chu2 in3 i kong2: 몮Gui7-sian7-chia2 a3! Lin2 tiong-kan bo5-lun7 sim2-mih lang5 bo5 tui3 gu5-tiau5 thau2 i e5 gu5 a2-si7 li5-a2, khan khi3 lim-chui2?  16) TaN ti7 chia chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kiaN2-sun. I i2-keng hou7 Sat-tan3 ka7 i sok-pak8 chap8-peh ni5 ku2, chai7 An-hioh-jit8 ka7 i thau2-khui sok-pak8 kam2 m7 eng-kai?몯  17) Ia5-sou kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 e5 si5, I e5 tek8-jin5 long2 kam2-kak chin kian3-siau3, tan7-si7 cheng3-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 I sou2 cho3 e5 ki5-biau7 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 chin hoaN-hi2.

Koa3-chhai3-chi2 e5 phi3-ju7: (Ma2 13:31-32; Kho2 4:30-42)
	18) Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok tau3-te2 chhin-chhiuN7 sim2-mih? Goa2 boeh eng7 sim2-mih lai5 pi2-pheng7?  19) Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 liap8 koa3-chhai3-chi2, lang5 theh8 lai5 ia7 toa3 i ka-ti7 e5 hng5-nih8, koa3-chhai3 chiu7 chiam7-chiam7 toa7 chang5 khi2-lai5, chiaN5-cho3 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 chang5 chhiu7-a2, khong-tiong e5 chiau2-a2 soah poe lai5 toa3 i e5 chhiu7-ki cho3 siu7.몯

KaN3-bo2 e5 phi3-ju7: (Ma2 13:33)
	20) I koh kong2: 몮Goa2 boeh eng7 sim2-mih lai5 pi2-pheng7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok?  21) Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 te3 kaN3-bo2. Hu7-jin5-lang5 theh8 chit e5 kaN3-bo2 khi3 chham toa3 saN tau2 mi7-hun2 e5 lai5-bin7, hou7 i long2 hoat khi2-lai5.몯

Eh8 e5 mng5: (Ma2 7:13-14; 21-23)
	22) Ia5-sou hiong3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 teh li2-heng5 e5 si5, keng-koe3 kok siaN5-chhi7 kok hiong-chhoan ka3-si7 lang5.  23) U7 lang5 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Lau7-su a3! E7 tit-tioh8 kiu3 e5 lang5 si7 chin chio2 si7 bo5?몯  24) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Tioh8 chin7-lek8 tui3 eh8 e5 mng5 jip8-khi3. Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, in-ui7 u7 chin-che7 lang5 e7 siuN7-boeh jip8-khi3, ia7 be7-tang3 jip8-khi3.몯
	25) 몮Chu2-lang5 it-tan7 i2-keng khi2-lai5 koaiN-mng5 liau2-au7, lin2 chiah khia7 toa3 mng5-goa7, it-tit8 phah-mng5 kong2, 몬Chu2 a3, ka7 goan2 khui mng5 le3!몭 Tan7-si7 I e7 in3-tap lin2 kong2, 몬Goa2 m7 chai-iaN2 lin2 si7 tui3 tah-ui7 lai5 e5.몭  26) Hit e5 si5 lin2 chiu7 e7 kong2, 몬goan2 bat kap Li2 cho3-hoe2 lim-chiah8. Li2 ia7 bat ti7 goan2 e5 ke-thau5 hang7-boe2 ka3-si7 goan2.몭  27) Tan7-si7 I e7 koh ka7 lin2 kong2, 몬goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, Goa2 m7 chai-iaN2 lin2 si7 tui3 tah-ui7 lai5 e5. Lin2 chiah-e5 cho3 put-gi7 e5 tai7-chi3 e5 lang5, li7-khui Goa2!몭  28) Lin2 khoaN3-kiN3 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok kap it-chhe3 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 ti7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 lai7-bin7, tan7-si7 lin2 ka-ti7 pi7 hiat toa3 ti7 goa7-bin7 e5 si5, ti7 hia e7 u7 thi5-khau3 kap ka7-ge5 chhiat-khi2 e5 siaN.  29) Lang5 e7 tui3 tang-sai lam5-pak lai5, in e7 chit8-koa2 hian7-chai7 cho3 lou7-boe2 e5, e7 cho3 thau5-cheng5; u7 chit8-koa2 hian7-chai7 cho3 thau5-cheng5 e5, e7 cho3 lou7-boe2.몯

Ia5-sou ui7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 pi-siong: (Ma2 23:37-39)
	31) Tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5, u7 chit8-koa2 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 oa2-lai5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Li2 tioh8 li7-khui chit e5 sou2-chai7 khi3 pat8-ui7, in-ui7 Hi-lut8 teh siuN7-boeh thai5 Li2.몯  32) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Lin2 khi3 ka7 hit chiah ho5-li5 kong2: 몮Kin-na2-jit8 kap bin5-na2-chai3 Goa2 boeh koaN2-kui2 kap i-peN7; kau3 te7-saN jit8, Goa2 chiu7 e7 oan5-seng5 Goa2 e5 kang-chok.몭  33) Sui-jian5 si7 an2-ne, kin-na2-jit8, bin5-na2-chai3 kap au7-jit8, Goa2 tioh8-ai3 ke3-siok8 kiaN5 Goa2 e5 lou7, in-ui7 cho3 chit8 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5, bo5 eng-kai si2 toa3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 i2-goa7 e5 sou2-chai7.몯
	34) 몮Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5 a3, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5! Li2 sat-hai7 tai7-gian5-jin5, eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3-si2 Siong7-chu2 chhe-phai3 lai5 li2 chia e5 su3-chia2! Goa2 tiaN7-tiaN7 siuN7-boeh chu7-chip8 li2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, chhin-chhiuN7 ke-bo2 khou i e5 ke-a2-kiaN2 lai5 aN3 toa3 sit8-kou2-e7! Tan7-si7 lin2 ka7 Goa2 ki7-choat8.  35) Lin2 khoaN3! Lin2 e5 chhu3 it-teng7 e7 hong-hoe3. Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, chiong5-kim i2-au7, lin2 choat8-tui3 be7-tang3 koh khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2, it-tit8 kau3 lin2 kong2, 몬Hong7 Chu2 e5 mia5 lai5 e5, eng-kai siu7 chan3-bi2!몭몯

Te7 14 ChiuN

Chai7 An-hioh-jit8 i-peN7:
	1) U7 chit8 e5 An-hioh-jit8, Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 chit8 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 thau5-lang5 e5 chhu3-nih chiah8-png7; tai7-ke chu3-i3 teh ka7 I koan-chhat.  2) Tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5, ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 u7 chit8 e5 kou2-tiong3-peN7 e5 lang5.  3) Ia5-sou chiu7 mng7 Lut8-hoat e5 choan-ka kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 kong2, 몮An-hioh-jit8 i-peN7 u7 hap8-hoat a2-si7 bo5 hap8-hoat?몯  4) Tan7-si7 in long2 tiam7-tiam7 bo5 in3. Ia5-sou chiu chhoa7 hit e5 lang5 lai5, ka7 i i-ho2, hou7 i tng2-khi3.  5) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Lin2 tiong-kan u7 lang5 ka-ti7 e5 kiaN2 a2-si7 gu5 poah8 loh8-khi3 kou2-cheN2 lai7, sui-jian5 si7 An-hioh-jit8, lin2 kam2 be7 sui5-si5 ka7 i giu2 khi2-lai5?몯  6) In tui3 chit e5 tai7-chi3 long2 bo5 oe7 thang in3 Ia5-sou.

Khiam-pi e5 lang5 e7 siu7 the5-ko:
	7) Ia5-sou khoaN3 tioh8 hiah-e5 lang5-kheh long2 siuN7-boeh che7 toa7 ui7, chiu7 eng7 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7 ka7 in kong2:  8) 몮Hou7 lang5 chhiaN2 khi3 chiah8 hi2-ian3 e5 si5, m7-thang che7 toa7 ui7; kiaN-laiu2 u7 pi2 li2 khah chun-kui3 e5 lang5-kheh ia7 lai5 hou7 i chhiaN2.  9) hit e5 si5, chhiaN2 li2 kap chhiaN2 hit e5 lang5-kheh e5 chu2-lang5 e7 lai5 ka7 li2 kong2, 몬Li2 e5 ui7 niu7 hou7 chit e5 lang5-kheh che7.몭 Hit e5 si5 li2 chiu7 e7 kian3-siau3 ia7 soah tioh8 the3-khi3 che7 siong7 se3e ui7.  10) Li2 hou7 lang5 chhiaN2 e5 si5, leng5-kho2 tioh8 khi3 che7 siong7 se3 e5 ui7. An2-ne chhiaN2 li2 e5 chu2-lang5 e7 lai5 ka7 li2 kong2, 몬Peng5-iu2 a3, chhiaN2 li2 che7 khah khi2-lai5 le3!몭 Hit e5 si5 li2 ti7 kang7 toh e5 cheng5-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 chiah u7 the2-bian7.  11) In-ui7 chu7-ko e5 lang5, it-teng7 e7 siu7 kang3-ke7; chu7-khiam chu7-pi e5 lang5, it-teng7 e7 siu7 the5-ko.몯
	12) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou ka7 chhiaN2 I e5 chu2-lang5 kong2: 몮Li2 chhiaN2 lang5 chiah8 e7-tau3-tng3 a2-si7 am3-tng3 e5 si5, m7-thang chhiaN2 li2 e5 peng5-iu2, a2-si7 hiaN-ti7, a2-si7 chhin-chhek, a2-si7 ho2-giah8 e5 chhu3-piN, in-ui7 kiaN-liau2 e7 oaN7 in chhiaN2 li2. An2-ne , li2 sou2 cho3 e5, chiu7 e7 siu7-tioh8 po3-tap.  13) Li2 chiau-thai7 lang5-kheh e5 si5, leng5-kho2 tioh8 chhiaN2 san3-chhiah-e5, phoa3-siuN3-e5, pai2-kha-e5, a2-si7 chheN-me5-e5.  14) An2-ne li2 chiu7 sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 in bo5 hoat-tou7 thang po3-tap li2. Kau3 gi7-jin5 tui3 si2-lang5 tiong hok8-hoat8 e5 si5, Siong7-chu2 chiu7 e7 po3-tap li2.몯

Toa7 ian3-hoe7 e5 phi3-ju7: (Ma2 22:1-10)
	15) U7 chit8 e5 kang7 toh e5 lang5 thiaN-khi3 chiah-e5 oe7, chiu7 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮E7 toa3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok chiah8-toh e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3!몯  16) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 i kong2: 몮U7 chit8 e5 lang5 boeh pan7 toa7 ian3-sek8, chiau-thai7 chin-che7 lang5-kheh.  17) Kau3 khui-toh e5 si5, i chiu7 chhe i e5 pok8-jin5 khi3 ka7 hiah-e5 sou2 chhiaN2 e5 lang5-kheh kong2, 몬ChhiaN2 lin2 lai5; it-chhe3 long2 chun2-pi7 ho2 a3.몭  18) Tan7-si7 cheng3-lang5 long2 chit8-e5 chit8-e5 khai-si2 the-si5. Te7-it e5 ka7 i kong2,몭goa2 be2 chit8 te3 te7, tek-khak tioh8-ai3 khi3 khoaN3 hit te3 te7. ChhiaN2 li2 goan5-liong7 goa2.몭  19) Koh chit8 e5 kong2, 몬Goa2 u7 be2 gou7 tui3 gu5; goa2 boeh lai5 khi3 sai2 khoaN3 bai7-le3. ChhiaN2 li2 goan5-liong7 goa2.몭  20) Iau2 koh chit8 e5 kong2, 몬Goa2 tu2 chhoa7 bou2, sou2-i2 be7-tang3 khi3.몭  21) Hit e5 pok8-jin5 tng2-lai5 ka7 i e5 chu2-lang5 po3-ko3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3. Hit e5 chu2-lang5 chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3, ka7 i e5 pok8-jin5 kong2, 몬Li2 koaN2-kin2 chhut-khi3 siaN5-lai7 e5 ke-thau5 hang7-boe2, chhoa7 hiah-e5 san3-chhiah-e5, phoa3-siuN3-e5, chheN-me5-e5, pai2-kha-e5 lai5.몭  22) Hit e5 pok8-jin5 kong2, 몬Thau5-ke a3, i2-keng u7 chiau3 li2 sou2 hoan-hu3 e5 khi3 cho3 a3, tan7-si7 iau2-ku2 u7 khang-ui7.몭  23) Chu2-lang5 chiu7 ka7 pok8-jin5 kong2, 몬Lin2 chhut-khi3 kong-lou7 a2-si7 li5-pa-piN kiong5-kiong5 giu2 lang5 jip8-lai5, thang hou7 Goa2 e5 chhu3-lai7 che7 kah moa2.몭  24) Sou2-i2 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, khi2-thau5 sou2 chiau-thai7 hiah-e5 lang5, bo5 chit8 e5 lang5 e7 chiah8-tioh8 Goa2 e5 chheN-chhau.몯

Cho3 bun5-tou5 eng-kai hu3-chhut e5 tai7-ke3: (Ma2 10:37-38)
	25) U7 chin toa7 tin7 e5 lang5 kap Ia5-sou tang5-che5 teh kiaN5-lou7 e5 si5, Ia5-sou oat8 koe3-lai5 ka7 in kong2:  26) 몮Bo5-lun7 sim2-mih lang5, na7 boeh lai5 toe3 Goa2, m7-kheng2 pang3-sak i e5 pe7-bo2, bou2-kiaN2, hiaN-ti7 chi2-moe7, sim7-chi3 pang3-sak i e5 seN3-mia7, chiu7 be7-tang3 cho3 Goa2 e5 bun5-tou5.  27) Bo5 gia5 ka-ti7 e5 sip8-ji7-ke3 lai5 toe3 Goa2 e5 lang5, ia7 be7-tang3 cho3 Goa2 e5 bun5-tou5.  28) Lin2 e5 tiong-kan na7 u7 lang5 boeh khi2 chit8 e5 thah, i kam2 m7-si7 tai7-seng che7 loh8-khi3 kou2-ke3 khoaN3 ai3 loa7-che7 chiN5, koh khoaN3 i u7 kau3 chiN5 thang oan5-seng5 hit e5 kang-theng5 a2 bo5?  29) Na7 bo5, phah te7-ki liau2-au7 soah be7-tang3 oan5-seng5 hit e5 thah, khoaN3-tioh8 an2-ne e5 lang5 chiu7 long2 e7 ka7 i thi2-chhio3.  30) In e7 kong2, 몬Chit e5 lang5 khai-si2 tang7-kang, soah be7-tang3 oan5-seng5!몭  31) Ka2-su2 u7 chit8 e5 kok-ong5 chhoa7 chit8 ban7 e5 peng, boeh khi3 kap u7 nng7 ban7 e5 peng e5 kok-ong5 chian3-cheng e5 si5, i kam2 be7 tai7-seng che7 loh8-khi3 kho2-li7 khoaN3 i e7-tang3 thai5-iaN5 iau2 hit e5 kok-ong5 a2-be7?  32) I na7 chai-iaN2 be7 iaN5, chiu7 tioh8 than3 hit e5 kok-ong5 iau2 li7 hng7-hng7 e5 si5, tioh8 chhe su3-chia2 khi3 kap i kong2-ho5.  33) Kap an2-ne kang7-khoan2, lin2 e5 tiong-kan bo5-lun7 sim2-mih lang5 na7 bo5 pang3-sak i sou2 u7 e5 it-chhe3, chiu7 be7-tang3 cho3 Goa2 e5 bun5-tou5.몯

Sit-bi7 e5 iam5: (Ma2 5:13; Kho2 9:50)
	34) 몮Iam5 si7 chin ho2 e5 mih8, tan7-si7 iam5 na7 sit-bi7, boeh an3-choaN2 koh-chai3 hou7 i u7 kiam5-bi7.  35) Sit-bi7 e5 iam5 ia7 be7-eng7-tit loh8-chhan5, ia7 be7-eng7-tit kauh-pui5; tioh8 hiat chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7. U7 hiN7-khang thang thiaN e5 lang5, tioh8 chu3-i3 thiaN.몯

Te7 15 ChiuN

Sit-be5 e5 iuN5: (Ma2 18:12-14)
	1) U7 chit8 pai2, chin-che7 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 kap choe7-jin5 oa2-lai5 Ia5-sou hia boeh thiaN I e5 to7-li2.  2) Hiah-e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 kap keng-hak8-chia2 khoaN3-tioh8 an2-ne chiu7 kauh8-kauh8-liam7, kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 hoan-geng5 choe7-jin5, sim7-chi3 kap in cho3-hoe2 chiah8-png7!몯  3) Ia5-sou chiu7 eng7 chit e5 phi3-ju7 ka7 in kong2:
	4) 몮Ka2-su2 lin2 e5 tiong-kan u7 lang5 u7 chit8 pah chiah iuN5-a2, phang3-kiN3 chit8 chiah, i kam2 be7 pang3 hit kau2-chap8-kau2 chiah toa3 chhau2-pou khi3 chhoe7 phang3-kiN3 hit chiah, it-tit8 kau3 chhoe7-tioh8.  5) I chhoe7-tioh8 e5 si5, chiu7 hoaN-hi2 kah gia5 toa3 i e5 keng-thau5 teng2,  6) tng2-lai5 kau3 chhu3-nih, kio3 i e5 peng5-iu2 chhu3-piN lai5, ka7 in kong2, 몬Lin2 kap goa2 tau3 hoaN-hi2, in-ui7 goa2 phang3-kiN3 e5 iuN5-a2, i2-keng koh chhoe7-tioh8 a3.몭  7) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, kap an2-ne kang7-khoan2, ui7-tioh8 chit8 e5 choe7-jin5 hoe3-kai2, pi2 kau2-chap8-kau2 e5 m7-bian2 hoe3-kai2 e5 gi7-jin5, ti7 thiN-teng2 koh-khah hoaN-hi2.몯

Phang3-kiN3 e5 gin5-oan5:
	8) 몮Iu7-koh ka2-su2 u7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, u7 chap8 e5 gin5-oan5, phang3-kiN3 chit8 e5 khi3. I kam2 be7 tiam2 teng, chheng-sau3 chhu3-lai7, tak8 sou2-chai7 chu3-i3 chhoe7 thau3-thau3 lai5 chhoe7 kah tioh8?  9) I chhoe7-tioh8 e5 si5, chiu7 kio3 i e5 peng5-iu2 chhu3-piN lai5, ka7 in kong2, 몬Lin2 kap goa2 tau3 hoaN-hi2, in-ui7 goa2 phang3-kiN3 khi3 hit e5 gin5-oan5, i2-keng koh chhoe7-tioh8 a3.몭  10) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, kap an2-ne kang7-khoan2, Siong7-chu2 e5 thian-sai3 e7 ui7-tioh8 chit8 e5 choe7-jin5 hoe3-kai2 lai5 toa7 hoaN-hi2.몯

Hong3-tong7-chu2:
	11) Ia5-sou koh ke3-siok8 kong2: 몮U7 chit8 e5 lang5. I u7 nng7 e5 hau7-seN.  12) Hit e5 se3-han3 e5 ka7 in lau7-pe7 kong2, 몬Pa-pa3, chiong goa2 eng-kai tit e5 chai5-san2 e5 hun7-giah8, chhiaN2 li2 chit chun7 pun hou7 goa2.몭 In lau7-pe7 chiu7 pun chai5-san2 hou7 in nng7 e5.  13) Keng-koe3 bo5 kui2 jit8, hit e5 se3-han3 kiaN2, chiong i sou2 tit-tioh8 hit hun7 chai5-san2 long2 oaN7 cho3 hian7-kim, chiu7 li7-khui chhu3 chhut-goa7 khi3 kau3 chin hng7 e5 sou2-chai7. I toa3 hia koe2 hong3-tong7 e5 seng-oah8, long7-hui3 i e5 chiN5.  14) I sou2 u7 e5 chiN5 long2 khai liau2-liau2 khi3 e5 si5, hit e5 sou2-chai7 tu2 hoat-seng toa7 ki-hng, i chiu7 khai-si2 khun3-khou2.  15) Sou2-i2 i chiu7 khi3 hou7 hit te7-hng e5 chit8 e5 lang5 chhiaN3. Hit e5 lang5 chiu7 chhe i khi3 long5-tiuN5 chhi7 ti.  16) I iau kah tong3 be7 tiau5, siuN7 kong2 na7 e7-tang3 theh8 ti teh chiah8 e5 tau7-a2-khak lai5 chi2-ki m7 chin ho2, tan7-si7 ilong2 bo5 lang5 boeh hou7 i chiah8.  17) Choe3-au7 i chiah kak-chheN2 khi2-lai5, kong2: 몬Goan2 lau7-pe7 sou2 chhiaN3 hiah-e5 lang5, tai7-ke long2 u7 mih8 thang chiah8 kah pa2, siong7-chhiaN2 chiah8 u7 chhun, iah goa2 ti7 chia go7 kah teh-boeh si2-khi3!  18) Goa2 boeh lai5-khi3, boeh tng2 lai5-khi3 chhoe7 goan2 lau7-pe7. Goa2 boeh ka7 i kong2: a-pa, goa2 tek-choe7 tioh8 Siong7-chu2, ia7 tek-choe7 tioh8 li2.  19) TaN goa2 i2-keng bo5 chu-keh thang cho3 li2 e5 kiaN2 a3. ChhiaN2 li2 tui3-thai7 goa2 cho3 li2 e5 iong7-lang5 e5 chit8 e5.몭  20) I chiu7 chhut-hoat, tng2-khi3 in lau7-pe7 hia.몯
	몮I li7 in chhu3 iau2-ku2 chin hng7 e5 si5, in lau7-pe7 chiu7 khoaN3-tioh8 i, khoaN3 chit8-e7 chin m7-kam, kin2 chau2 oa2-khi3 eng7 siang-chhiu2 ka7 i lam2 le3, chhin-bit8 ka7 i chim.  21) In kiaN2 chiu7 ka7 in lau7-pe7 kong2, 몬A-pa, goa2 tek-choe7 tioh8 Siong7-chu2, ia7 tek-choe7 tioh8 li2. TaN goa2 i2-keng bo5 chu-keh thang cho3 li2 e5 kiaN2 a3.몭  22) Tan7-si7 in lau7-pe7 ka7 i e5 pok8-jin5 kong2: 몬KoaN2-kin2 hiahN siong7 ho2 e5 goa7-saN chhut-lai5 ka7 i chheng7, ka7 i koa3 chhiu2-chi2, koh ka7 i chheng7 e5.  23) Jian5-au7 khan hit chiah chhi7 kah chin pui5 e5 gu5-a2-kiaN2 lai5 thai5; lan2 lai5 khui-toh khegn3-chiok8.  24) In-ui7 goa2 chit e5 kiaN2 si2-khi3 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, phang3-kiN3 khi3 koh chhoe7-tioh8.몭 In chiu7 khui-toh lai5 kheng3-chiok.몯
25) 몮Hit e5 si5, i e5 toa7-kiaN2 chhut-khi3 ti7 hng5-nih8. I tng2-lai5 boeh kau3 chhu3-nih e5 si5, thiaN-kiN3 chau3-gak8 kap thiau3-bu2 e5 siaN,  26) chiu7 kio3 chit8 e5 pok8-jin5 lai5 mng7 khoaN3 si7 teh cho3 sim2-mih tai7-chi3.  27) Hit e5 pok8-jin5 in3 i kong2, 몬Lin2 sio2-ti7 tng2-lai5; lin2 lau7-pe7 in-ui7 i peng5-peng5-an-an tng2-lai5, chiu7 thai5 hit chiah chhi7 kah chin pui5 e5 gu5-a2-kiaN2.몭  28) ThiaN-kiN3 an2-ne, hit e5 toa7-kiaN2 hui-siong5 siu7-khi3, soah m7 jip8-khi3 chhu3-lai7. In lau7-pe7 chiu7 chhut-lai5 kou-chiaN5 i jip8-khi3.  29) Tan7-si7 i in3 in lau7-pe7 kong2: 몬Li2 khoaN3, goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 lou5-chai5-a2 ka7 li2 cho3-kang cho3 chiah che7 ni5! Goa2 ia7 m7-bat thai5 kah chit8 chiah iuN5-a2-kiaN2 lai5 hou7 goa2 kap goa2 e5 peng5-iu2 cho3-hoe2 lim-chiah8 khoai3-lok8!  30) Tan7-si7 li2 chit e5 kiaN2, ui7-tioh8 ki-li2 chiong li2 e5 chai5-san2 khai liau2-liau2, i chit8-e7 tng2-lai5, li2 chiu7 tian-to3 ui7-tioh8 i thai5 hit chiah siong7 pui5 e5 gu5-a2-kiaN2!몭  31) In lau7-pe7 in3 i kong2: 몬goa2 e5 kiaN2 a3, li2 si5-siong5 kap goa2 teh cho3-hoe2, iu7-koh goa2 e5 chai5-san2 long2 ma7 si7 li2 e5.  32) Tan7-si7 li2 chit e5 sio2-ti7, in-ui7 i si2-khi3 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, phang3-kiN3 khi3 koh chhoe7-tioh8, lan2 eng-kai tioh8 lai5 khui-toh hoaN-hi2 kheng3-chiok.몭몯

Te7 16 ChiuN

Put-gi7 e5 koan2-ke-e5:
	1) Ia5-sou ka7 i e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: 몮U7 chit8 e5 ho2-giah8-lang5. I u7 chit8 e5 koan2-ke-e5. U7 lang5 tui3 chit e5 chu2-lang5 kiam2-ki2 chit e5 koan2-ke-e5 long7-hui3 chu2-lang5 e5 chai5-san2.  2) Chu2-lang5 chiu7 kio3 i lai5, ka7 i kong2: 몬goa2 na2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 li2 chit khoan2 e5 tai7-chi3? Chiong li2 sou2 teh koan2 e5 oga2 e5 chai5-san2, ka7 goa2 cho7 chheng-chheh chhut-lai5, in-ui7 li2 be7-eng7-tit koh cho3 goa2 e5 koan2-ke-e5.몭  3) Hit e5 koan2-ke-e5 chiu7 ka-ti7 siuN7 kong2: 몬Goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 teh-boeh ka7 goa2 khai-ti5. TaN goa2 tioh8 an3-choaN2 cho3? Boah lai5 kut8-thou5, goa2 iu7 bo5 kau3 lat8; boeh lai5 cho3 khit-chiah8, goa2 iu7 kiaN kian3-siau3.  4) TaN goa2 chai-iaN2 tioh8-ai3 an3-choaN2 lai5 cho3! Na7 an2-ne, goa2 bo5 thau5-lou7 liau2-au7, chiu7 u7 peng5-iu2 thang hoan-geng5 goa2 jip8-khi3 in chhu3.'몭 5) Sou2-i2 i chiu7 kio3 in chu2-lang5 e5 che3-bu7-jin5 chit8-e5 chit8-e5 lai5. I tui3 te7-it e5 kong2, '몬i2 khiam3 goan2 chu2-lang5 loa7-che7?'몭 6) I in3 kong2, '몬hit8 pah thang2 e5 ka-na2-iu5.몭 Koan2-ke-e5 ka7 i kong2, 몬Che si7 li2 e5 chioh-tiau5, theh8-khi3, koaN2-kin2 che7 loh8-khi3 kai2 cho3 gou7-chap8 thang2.몭  7) I iu7-koh ka7 leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 kong2. 몬Iah li2 le3? Li2 khiam3 loa7 che7?몭 I in3 kong2, 몬Chit8 pah chioh8 beh8-a2.몭 Koan2-ke-e5 ka7 i kong2, 몬Che si7 li2 e5 chioh-tiau5. Theh8 khi3 kai2-cho3 peh-chap8 chioh8.몭  8) Chu2-lang5 chiu7 o-lo2 chit e5 put-gi7 e5 koan2-ke-e5 cho3 liau2 chin-chiaN3 khiau2-biau7, in-ui7 se3-siok8-lang5 cho3-su7 pi2 siok8 kong-beng5 e5 lang5 ke chin khiau2-biau7.몯
	9) Ia5-sou ke3-siok8 kong2: 몮Goa2 koh ka7 lin2 kong2: tioh8 eng7 chit se3-siok8 e5 chiN5-chai5 lai5 ui7 li2 ka-ti7 kau-poe5 peng5-iu2. Kau3 chiN5-chai5 bo5 khi3 e5 si5, in chiu7 e7 hoan-geng5 lin2 jip8-khi3 eng2-oan2 e5 chhu3-nih.  10) Tui3 se3 hang7 tai7-chi3 tiong-sit8 e5 lang5, tui3 toa7 hang7 tai7-chi3 ia7 e7 tiong-sit8; tui3 se3 hang7 tai7-chi3 bo5 lau2-sit8 e5 lang5, tui3 toa7 hang7 tai7-chi3 ia7 e7 bo5 lau2-sit8.  11) Sou2-i2 lin2 koan2-li2 se3-siok8 e5 chiN5-chai5 na7 bo5 tiong-sit8, sim2-mih lang5 boeh kau-tai3 lin2 lai5 koan2-li2 chin-chiaN3 e5 chai5-po2.  12) Iu7-koh lin2 na7 koan2-li2 siok8 pat8-lang5 e5 mih8-kiaN7, bo5 tiong-sit8, sim2-mih lang5 boeh chiong eng-kai siok8 lin2 e5, lai5 hou7 lin2?몯
	13) 몮Bo5 chit8 e5 pok8-jin5 e7-tang3 su-hau7 nng7 e5 chu2-lang5; i e7 oan3-hin7 chit e5 lai5 ai3 hit e5, a2-si7 tui3 chit e5 chin7-tiong, lai5 khoaN3 khin hit e5. Lin2 be7-eng7-tit ia7 boeh su7-hong7 Siong7-chu2 ia7 boeh su-hong7 chiN5-chai5.몯

Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok kap Lut8-hoat: (Ma2 11:12-13; 5:31-32; Kho2 10:11-12)
	14) Tham-chai5 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-sou kong2 chiah-e5 oe7, chiu7 thi2-chhio3 I.  15) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 in kong2: 몮Lin2 boeh hou7 lang5 khoaN3-cho3 si7 gi7-jin5, tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 chai-iaN2 lin2 e5 lai7-sim. In-ui7 lang5 siuN7 cho3 chin chun-kui3 e5, tui3 Siong7-chu2 khoaN3 khi2-lai5 si7 tho2-ia3 e5.몯
	16) 몮Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat kap tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 kau3-hun3, kau3 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 e5 si5 ui5-chi2 u7 hau7-lek8. Tui3 hit e5 si5 i2-au7, Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 Hok-im chiu7 thoan5-iong5 chhut-lai5, tak8-lang5 long2 kiong5 boeh chiN jip8-khi3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok.  17) Tan7-si7 thiN-te7 e5 siau-biat8, pi2 boeh hoe3-ti5 Lut8-hoat e5 chit8 tiam2 chit8 oeh8 koh-khah iong5-i7.몯
	18) 몮Bo5-lun7 sim2-mih lang5 na7 kap i e5 bou2 li7-hun, lai5 kap pat8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kiat-hun, chiu7-si7 hoan7 kan-im5 e5 choe7. Na7 u7 lang5 kap chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kiat-hun, ia7-si7 hoan7-tioh8 kan-im5.몯

Ho2-giah8-lang5 kap Liap-sat-lou7:
	19) 몮U7 chit8 e5 ho2-giah8-lang5, chheng7 choe3 ko-kui3 e5 saN, tak8-jit8 seng-oah8 chin chhia-hoa.  20) Ia7 u7 chit8 e5 san3-chhiah-lang5 mia5 kio3-cho3 Liap8-sat-lou7, kui seng-khu seN kah choan5 liap8-a2, to2 ti7 hit e5 ho2-giah8-lang5 e5 mng5-khau2,  21) siuN7-boeh khioh tui3 hit e5 ho2-giah8-lang5 e5 toh-teng3 ka-lauh8 loh8-lai5 e5 chiah8-mih8, lai5 chi2-ki! Siong7-chhiaN2 kau2 ia7 tiaN7-tiaN7 lai5 chiN7 i e5 liap8-a2.  22) Au7-lai5 chit e5 san3-chhiah-lang5 si2-khi3, thian-sai3 chiu7 lai5 chhoa7 i khi3-kau3 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 hoai5-pau. Hit e5 ho2-giah8-lang5 ia7 si2-khi3, hou7 lang5 ka7 i bai5-chong3.  23) Hit e5 ho2-giah8-lang5 toa3 im-kan teh siu7 kek8-tou7 e5 thong3-khou2. I giah8-thau5 chit8-e7 khoaN3, ti7 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 A-pek-lah8-han2, ia7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Liap8-sat-lou7 ti7 i e5 hoai5-pau.  24) Sou2-i2  i chiu7 chhut-siaN kio3 kong2, 몬goa2 e5 chou2-sian A-pek-lah8-han2 a3, lin5-bin2 goa2. ChhiaN2 Li2 chhe-phai3 Liap8-sat-lou7 eng7 chng2-thau5-a2 boe2 un3 chui2 lai5 hou7 goa2 e5 chhui3-chih8 liang5 chit8-e7; in-ui7 goa2 ti7 chit e5 hoe2-iam7 tiong teh siu7 thong3-khou2.몭  25) A-pek-lah8-han2 in3 i kong2: 몬Sio2-kiaN2 a3, li2 tioh8 e7-ki3-tit li2 chai7-seN hiong2-siu7 it-chhe3 e5 khoai3-lok8, tan7-si7 Liap8-sat-lou7 siu7-chin7 it-chhe3 e5 thong3-khou2. TaN i ti7 chia teh hiong2-hok, tan7-si7 li2 ti7 hia teh siu7-khou2.  26) Put-tan7 an2-ne, goan2 kap lin2 e5 tiong-kan u7 chit8 tiau5 chhim-kheN ka7 lan2 keh-khui le, sou2-i2 siuN7-boeh tui3 chia koe3-khi3 lin2 hia e5 lang5, ia7 be7-tang3 koe3-khi3, ia7 bo5 lang5 e7-tang3 tui3 lin2 hia koe3-lai5 goan2 chia.몭  27) Hit e5 ho2-giah8-lang5 chiu7 kong2, 몬Goa2 e5 chou2-sian a3, goa2 kiu5 li2 chhe-phai3 Liap8-sat-lou7 khi3 goan2 lau7-pe7 e5 chhu3-nih.  28) Ti7 hia goa2 u7 gou7 e5 hiaN-ti7. Hou7 i khi3 ka7 in keng2-kou3; chiah be7 hou7 in ia7 lai5-kau3 chit e5 kek8 thong3-khou2 e5 sou2-chai7.몭  29) Tan7-si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 in3 i kong2, 몬Li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 u7 Mou5-se kap tai7-gian5-jin5 thang ka7 in keng2-kou3, hou7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 khi3 thiaN in e5 oe7 chiu7 ho2.몭  30) Hit e5 ho2-giah8-lang5 in3 kong2, 몬Goa2 e5 chou2-sian A-pek-lah8-han2 a3, an2-ne iau2 bo5 kau3-giah8. Ka2-su2 u7 lang5 si2-khi3 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5 khi3 in hia, in chiu7 e7 hoe3-kai2.몭  31) Tan7-si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 ka7 i kong2, 몬In na7 m7 thiaN Mou5-se kap tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 oe7, ka2-su2 u7 lang5 tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, in ia7 m7 sin3.몭몯

Te7 17 ChiuN

M7-thang in2-khi2 lang5 hoan7-choe7: (Ma2 18:6-7, 21-22; Kho2 9:42)
	1) Ia5-sou ka7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: 몮In2-khi2 lang5 hoan7-choe7 e5 tai7-chi3, lan5-bian2 e7 hoat-seng, tan7-si7 hou7 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 hoat-seng hit e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7!  2) Na7 u7 lang5 in2-khi2 chiah-e5 hou7 lang5 khoaN3 siong7 ho5 khi2 e5 chit8 e5 hoan7-choe7, hit e5 lang5 leng5-kho2 tioh8 eng7 chioh8-bo7 pak8 toa3 i e5 am7-kun2, ka7 i tan3 loh8-khi3 hai2-te2 khah ho2.  3) Lin2 tioh8 keng2-kai3 lin2 ka-ti7.몯
	몮li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 na7 hoan7-choe7, li2 tioh8 ka7 i khoan3-kai2; i na7 u7 hoe3-kai2, tioh8 ka7 i sia3-bian2.  4) I na7 chit8 jit8 tek-choe7 li2 chhit pai2, chhit pai2 to3-tng2-lai5 ka7 li2 kong2, 몬Goa2 u7 hoe3-kai2,몭 li2 ia7 tioh8 sia3-bian2 i.몯

Sin3-sim e5 lek8-liong7:
	5) Hiah-e5 Su3-tou5 ka7 Chu2 kong2, 몮Kiu5 Li2 cheng7-ka goan2 e5 sin3-sim!몯  6) Chu2 in3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 na7 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 liap8 koa3-chhai3-chi2 hiah-nih8 toa7 e5 sin3-sim, lin2 e7-tang3 ka7 chit chang5 sng-chai5-chhiu7 kong2, 몬Li2 lian5 kin poeh8 khi2-lai5, khi3 cheng3 toa3 hai2-nih!몭 hit chhang5 ia7 e7 hok8-chiong5 lin2.몯

Pok8-jin5 e5 gi7-bu7:
	7) 몮Ka2-su2 lin2 tiong-kan u7 lang5 u7 chit8 e5 pok8-jin5, teh le5-chhan5 a2-si7 teh kou3 iuN5-a2. Chit e5 pok8-jin5 tui3 hng5-nih8 tng2-lai5 e5 si5, chu2-lang5 kam2 e7 ka7 i kong2, 몬KoaN2-kin2 lai5 chiah8-png7몭?  8) Tian-to3 e7 ka7 i kong2, 몬Chun2-pi7 hou7 goa2 chiah8 am3-tng3; goa2 teh lim-chiah8 e5 tiong-kan, ha5 ui5-su-kun5 lai5 su-hau7 goa2, jian5-au7 li2 chiah thang lim-chiah8.몭  9) Chit e5 pok8-jin5 cho3 chu2-lang5 sou2 hoan-hu3 e5 tai7-chi3, chu2-lang5 kam2 eng-kai ka7 i kong2 to-sai7?  10) Lin2 ia7-si7 kap an2-ne kang7-khoan2; sou2 siu7 kau-thok e5 tia7-chi3 lin2 long2 cho3-liau2 e5 si5, ia7-si7 tioh8 kong2, 몬Goan2 put-ko3 si7 bo5 lou7-eng7 e5 pok8-jin5, kan-taN chin7 goan2 e5 pun2-hun7 khi3 cho3 nia7-nia7.몭몯

Ia5-sou i-ho2 chap8-e5 ba5-hong-peN7-lang5:
	11) Ia5-sou boeh khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 si5, tui3 Sat-ma2-li7-a Seng2 kap Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 e5 kau-kai3 keng-koe3.  12) I tu2 boeh jip8-khi3 chit8 e5 hiong-chhoan e5 si5, u7 chap8-e5 ba5-hong-peN7 e5 lang5 lai5 kiN3 I. In khia7 toa3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2 chai7,  13) toa7 siaN hoah kong2, 몮Ia5-sou a3, Lau7-su a3, lin5-bin2 goan2!몯  14) Ia5-sou chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 in, chiu7 kong2, 몮Lin2 khi3 hou7 che3-si ka7 lin2 giam7!몯 In teh-boeh khi3 e5 si5, ti7 lou7-nih8 chiu7 long2 ho2-khi3.  15) Ki5-tiong u7 chit8 e5, khoaN3-kiN3 ka-ti7 long2 ho2-khi3 a3, chiu7 to3-tng2-lai5 toa7 siaN chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2.  16) I phak toa3 Ia5-sou e5 kha-cheng5, ka7 I kam2-sia7. Chit e5 lang5 si7 Sat-ma2-li7-a-lang5.  17) Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Ho2-khi3 e5 kam2 m7-si7 long2-chong2 chap8-e5 lang5? Iau2 hit kau2 e5 lang5 ti7 tah-ui7?  18) Chit e5 goa7-kok-lang5 i2-goa7, kam2 bo5 lang5 tng2-lai5 kam2-sia7 Siong7-chu2?몯  19) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 hit e5 lang5 kong2, 몮Khi2-lai5, tng2-khi3 lin2 chhu3. Li2 e5 sin3-sim ka7 li2 i-ho2 khi3 a3.몯

Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 lai5-lim5: (Ma2 24:23-28, 37-41)
	20) U7 chit8-koa2 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 mng7 Ia5-sou khoaN3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok sim2-mih si5 e7 lai5-lim5. Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: 몮Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 lai5-lim5 m7-si7 hou7 lang5 khoaN3 e7 tioh8 e5.  21) Bo5 lang5 e7 kong2,몭Li2 khoaN3, ti7 hia! a2-si7 몮Li2 khoaN3, ti7 chia!몭 in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok i2-keng ti7 lin2 e5 tiong-kan a.몯
	22) Ia5-sou ka7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: 몮Lin2 chhiat-bong7 boeh khoaN3 Jin5-chu2 lai5-lim5 e5 jit8-chi2 e5 chit8 jit8, hit e5 si5-jit8 teh-boeh kau3 a3, tan7-si7 lin2 khoaN3 be7-tioh8.  23) U7 lang5 e7 ka7 lin2 kong2, 몬Li2 khoaN3, I ti7 hia!몭 a2-si7 kong2, 몬Li2 khoaN3, I ti7 chia!몭 Lin2 m7-thang chhut-khi3, ia7 m7-thang toe3 in khi3,  24) in-ui7 chhin-chhiuN7 sih-na3 tui3 thiN chit peng5 sih, kng kau3 thiN hit peng5, Jin5-chu2 lai5-lim5 e5 jit8-chi2 ia7 e7 an2-ne.  25) Tan7-si7 I it-teng7 tioh8 tai7-seng siu7 chin-che7 khou2-lan7, ia7 e7 hou7 chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 khi3-choat8.  26) Jin5-chu2 lai5-lim5 e5 jit8-chi2, ia7 e7 chhin-chhiuN7 Na2-a e5 si5 an2-ne.  27) Hit e5 si5, lang5 chiau3-siong5 lim-chiah8 ke3-chhoa7, it-tit8 kau3 Na2-a jip8-khi3 toa7-chun5 hit jit8. Toa7-chui2 chit8-e7 kau3, chiu7 siau-biat8 kah bo5 poaN3 e5 lang5.  28) Ia7 e7 chhin-chhiuN7 Lo5-tek e5 si5, lang5 chiau3-siong5 lim chiah8, be2-be7, cheng3-choh, khi2-chhu3;  29) tan7-si7 Lo5-tek tui3 Sou2-to-ma2-siaN5 chhut-khi3 hit jit8, tui3 thiN loh8 hoe2 kap liu5-ng5 siau-biat8 kah bo5 poaN3 e5 lang5.  30) Jin5-chu2 chhut-hian7 e5 jit8, ia7 e7 hoat-seng kang7-khoan2 e5 tai7-chi3.몯
	31) 몮Hit jit8, tu2 ti7 chhu3-teng2 e5 lang5 m7-thang loh8-lai5 theh8 chhu3-lai7 e5 mih8-kiaN7. Ti7 chhan5-nih8 e5 lang5, ia7 m7-thang tng2-khi3.  32) Lin2 tioh8 e7-ki3-tit Lo5-tek in bou2 e5 tai7-chi3!  33) SiuN7-boeh po2-choan5 i e5 seN3-mia7 e5 lang5, it-teng7 e7 song3-sit; song3-sit seN3-mia7 e5 lang5, it-teng7 e7 po2-choan5.  34) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, hit chit8 am3, u7 nng7 e5 lang5 khun3 kang7 chit8 teng2 bin5-chhng5; chit8 e5 e7 hou7 lang5 chhoa7-khi3, chit8 e5 e7 hou7 lang5 lau5 le7.  35) U7 nng7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 cho3-hoe2 teh e chioh8-bo7-a2; chit8 e5 e7 hou7 lang5 chhoa7-khi3, chit8 e5 e7 hou7 lang5 lau5 le7.  ( 36) U7 nng7 e5 lang5 ti7 chhan5-nih8; chit8 e5 e7 hou7 lang5 chhoa7-khi3, chit8 e5 e7 hou7 lang5 lau5 le7.)몯  37) Bun5-tou5 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, che e7 ti7 sim2-mih sou2-chai7 hoat-seng?몯 Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2, 몮U7 sin-si e5 sou2-chai7, eng-a2 chiu7 e7 chu7-chip8 khi3 hia.몯

Te7 18 ChiuN

KoaN2-hu7 kap phoaN2-koaN e5 phi3-ju7:
	1) Ia5-sou koh tui3 bun5-tou5 kong2 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7 boeh ka3-si7 in tioh8-ai3 siong5-siong5 ki5-to2, m7-thang siuN7 sian7.  2) I kong2: 몮Kou2-cha2 ti7 chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7, u7 chit8 e5 phoaN3-koaN, bo5 keng3-ui3 Siong7-chu2, ia7 bo5 chun-tiong7 lang5.  3) Ti7 kang7 hit e5 siaN5-chhi7 u7 chit8 e5 koaN2-hu7, siong5-siong5 lai5 chhoe7 i kong2: 몬Goa2 u7 chit8 e5 sou3-siong7 e5 tui3-thau5, chhiaN2 li2 chu2-chhi5 kong-to7 lai5 ka7 goa2 iong3-hou7.몭  4) PhoaN3-koaN chin ku2 long2 m7 chhap i; tan7-si7 kau3 choe3-au7 i ka-ti7 siuN7 kong2, 몬Goa2 sui-jian5 bo5 keng3-ui3 Siong7-chu2, ia7 bo5 chun-tiong7 lang5,  5) tan7-si7 in-ui7 chit e5 koaN2-hu7 tiaN7-tiaN7 lai5 chha2 goa2,goa2 boeh ui7 i chu2-chhi5 kong-to7, i chiah be7 tiaN7-tiaN7 lai5 kap goa2 ko-ko-tiN5, lai5 ka7 goa2 chha2-si2.몭몯  6) Chu2 koh kong2: 몮Lin2 tioh8 thiaN chit e5 put-gi7 e5 phoaN3-koaN sou2 kong2 e5 oe7!  7) An2-ne Siong7-chu2 e5 soan2-bin5 na7 me5-jit8 ka7 I ai-kiu5, I kam2 e7 thoa-ian5 chin ku2 chiah lai5 ui7 in chu2-chhi5 kong-to7?  8) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, I e7 koaN2-kin2 ui7 in lai5 chu2-chhi5 kong-to7! Tan7-si7 Jin5-chu2 lai5 e5 si5, I chai7 se3-kan kam2 e7-tang3 chhoe7-tioh8 sin3-giong2?몯

Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 kap thiu-soe3 e5 lang5:
	9) Ia5-sou koh kong2 leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7. Chit e5 phi3-ju7 si7 tui3 chit8-koa2 chu7-chheng cho3 gi7-jin5, lai5 khoaN3-khin pat8-lang5 e5 lang5 kong2 e5.  10) I kong2: 몮U7 nng7 e5 lang5 jip8-khi3 Seng3-tian7 ki5-to2; chit8 e5 si7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, iau2 chit8 e5 si7 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5.  11) Hit e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 khia7 theng5-theng5 ki5-to2 kong2: 몬Siong7-chu2, goa2 kam2-sia7 Li2 hou7 goa2 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 ki5-tha e5 lang5 tham-chai5, put-gi7, houN3-sek, tek8-piat8 ia7 hou7 goa2 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 hit e5 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5.  12) Goa2 chit8 le2-pai3 kim3-chiah8 nng7 pai2. Goa2 hong7-hian3 goa2 sou2 siu-jip8 e5 chap8-hun chi it hou7 Li2.몭  13) Tan7-si7 hit e5 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5, khia7 toa3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7, lian5 thau5-khak ia7 m7-kaN2 giah8 khi2-lai5 khoaN3 thiN, na2 tui5-heng na2 kong2, 몬A3! Siong7-chu2 a3, lin5-bin2 goa2 chit e5 choe7-jin5.몭몯  14) Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, hou7 Siong7-chu2 sia3-choe7 tng2-khi3 chhu3-nih e5, si7 chit e5 lang5, m7-si7 hit e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5. In-ui7 chu7-ko e5 lang5, it-teng7 e7 siu7 kang3-ke; chu7-khiam chu7-pi e5 lang5, it-teng7 e7 siu7 the5-ko.몯

Ia5-sou chiok-hok se3-han3 gin2-na2: (Ma2 19:13-15; Kho2 10:13-16)
	15) In lian5 se3-han3-gin2-na2 ia7 pho7 lai5 boeh hou7 Ia5-sou bong; bun5-tou5 khoaN3-kiN3 chiu7 ka7 in chek-pi7.  16) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou kio3 hiah-e5 se3-han3-gin2-na2 lai5, kong2: 몮Tioh8 hou7 hiah-e5 gin2-na2 lai5 Goa2 chia. M7-thang ka7 in tong3! In-ui7 chhin-chhiuN7 chiah-e5 gin2-na2 e5 lang5, chiah e7-tang3 chiaN5-cho3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 chu2-bin5.  17) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2: lang5 na7 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 se3-han3-gin2-na2 lai5 seng5-siu7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok, choat8-tui3 be7-tang3 jip8-khi3.몯

Ho2-giah8 e5 koaN-oan5: (Ma2 19:16-30; Kho2 10:17-31)
	18) U7 chit8 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 koaN-oan5 lai5 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Ho2 Lau7-su, goa2 tioh8 cho3 sim2-mih chiah e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 eng2-seng?몯  19) Ia5-sou mng7 i kong2: 몮Li2 an3-choaN2 chheng-hou Goa2 si7 ho2 e5? Siong7-chu2 i2-goa7, bo5 chit8 e5 si7 ho2 e5!  20) Li2 tong-jian5 bat chiah-e5 kai3-beng7; chiu7-si7 m7-thang hoan7 kan-im; m7-thang thai5-si2 lang5; m7-thang thau-theh8; m7-thang cho3 gui7-cheng3; tioh8 hau3-keng3 li2 e5 pe7-bo2.몯  21) Hit e5 lang5 kong2, 몮Chiah-e5 kai3-beng7, goa2 chu7 se3-han3 chiu7 long2 u7 teh chun-siu2 a3.몯  22) Ia5-sou thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7, chiu7 ka7 i kong2: 몮Li2 iau2-ku2 khiam3 chit8 hang7, khi3 be7 li2 sou2 u7 e5 it-chhe3, chiong hiah-e5 chiN5 lai5 chin2-che3 san3-chhiah-lang5, an2-ne ti7 thiN-teng2 li2 chiu7 e7 u7 chai5-po2, jian5-au7 chiah lai5 toe3 Goa2.몯  23) Hit e5 lang5 chit8-e7 thiaN-tioh8 chiah-e5 oe7, hui-siong5 pi-siong, in-ui7 i chin ho2-giah8.
	24) Ia5-sou khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 lang5 chin pi-siong, chiu7 kong2: 몮Ho2-giah8-lang5 boeh chin3-jip8 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok si7 hui-siong5 khun3-lan5!  25) Lok8-to5 chng3-koe3 chiam-phiN7, ia7 pi2 ho2-giah8-lang5 chin3-jip8 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok iau2 koh-khah iong5-i7!몯  26) ThiaN-chiong3 chiu7 mng7 I kong2, 몮Na7-si7 an2-ne, sim2-mih lang5 e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 kiu3?몯  27) Ia5-sou in3 kong2, 몮Lang5 sou2 cho3 be7 kau3 e5 su7, Siong7-chu2 long2 cho3 e7 kau3!몯
	28) Pi2-tek kong2, 몮Li2 khoaN3, goa2 i2-keng pang3-sak it-chhe3, lai5 teh toe3 Li2.몯  29) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2: lang5 na7 ui7-tioh8 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok lai5 pang3-sak ka-teng5, a2-si7 pe7-bo2, a2-si7 hiaN-ti7, a2-si7 bou2-kiaN2,  30) chai7 hian7-se3 it-teng7 e7 tit-tioh8 chin-che7 poe7 e5 po3-siuN2, iu7-koh chai7 lai5-se3 ia7 it-teng7 e7 tit-tioh8 eng2-seng.몯

Ia5-sou te7-saN chhu3 i7-ko3 I e5 si2-bong5: (Ma2 20:17-19; Kho2 10:32-34)
	31) Ia5-sou chhoa7 hit chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 khi3 piN-a, ka7 in kong2: 몮TaN lan2 boeh lai5-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2. Ti7 hia tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 ki3-chai3 koan-he7 Jin5-chu2 e5 it-chhe3, tak8-hang7 long2 e7 eng3-giam7,  32) in-ui7 I e7 hou7 lang5 kau hou7 Goa7-pang-lang5. Chiah-e5 Goa7-pang-lang5 e7 ka7 I thi2-chhio3, bu2-jiok8, phui3 chhui3-noa7.  33) In e7 eng7 piN ka7 I phah, soah ka7 I sat-hai7; tan7-si7 te7-saN jit8 Siong7-chu2 it-teng7 e7 hou7 I hok8-hoat8.몯  34) Chiah-e5 oe7 bun5-tou5 long2 thiaN be7 hiau2. In-ui7 chiah-e5 oe7 chin bok8-beng5 ki5-biau7, in long2 m7 chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou teh kong2 sim2-mih.

ChheN-me5 e5 khit-chiah8 koh-chai3 u7 khoaN3-kiN3: (Ma2 20:29-34; Kho2 10:46-52)
	35) Ia5-sou lai5 teh-boeh kau3 Ia5-li7-ko-siaN5 e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 chheN-me5-e5 che7 ti7 lou7-piN teh kiu5-khit.  36) I thiaN-kiN3 chin-che7 lang5 tui3 hia koe3, chiu7 mng7 lang5 khoaN3 si7 sim2-mih tai7-chi3.  37) Lang5 ka7 i kong2, 몮Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou teh-boeh tui3 chia keng-koe3.몯  38) I chiu7 toa7 siaN hoah kong2,몯Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun, Ia5-sou a3! Kho2-lin5 goa2!몯  39) Ti7 thau5-cheng5 teh kiaN5 e5 lang5 chiu7 ka7 i me7, kio3 i tioh8 tiam7-tiam7; tan7-si7 i lu2 toa7 siaN hoah kong2, 몮Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun a3, kho2-lin5 goa2!몯  40) Ia5-sou chiu7 theng5-kha, kio3 lang5 chhoa7 i lai5. I oa2-lai5 e5 si5, Ia5-sou mng7 i kong2,  41) 몮Li2 ai3 Goa2 ka7 li2 cho3 sim2-mih?몯 I kong2, 몮Lau7-su, hou7 goa2 koh-chai3 u7 khoaN3-kiN3.몯  42) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2, 몮Hou7 li2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3. Li2 e5 sin3-sim kiu3-tioh8 li2 a3.몯  43) I chiu7 sui5-si5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, kin-toe3 Ia5-sou khi3. Cheng3-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 tai7-chi3, ia7 long2 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2.

Te7 19 ChiuN

Ia5-sou kap Sat-kai:
	1) Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 Ia5-li7-ko-siaN5, ti7 ke-lou7 teh kiaN5 e5 si5,  2) ti7 hia u7 chit8 e5 lang5 mia5 kio3-cho3 Sat-kai. I si7 thiu-soe3 e5 thau5-lang5, ia7-si7 ho2-giah8-lang5.  3) I ai3-boeh khoaN3 Ia5-sou si7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 lang5, tan7-si7 in-ui7 lang5 chin-che7, iu7-koh i lang5 chin e2, khoaN3 be7 tioh8.  4) Sou2-i2 i chiu7 chau2 cho3-cheng5, peh khi2-khi3 chit8 chang5 sng-chai5-hioh e5 bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7-teng2, boeh khoaN3 Ia5-sou chit8-e7; in-ui7 Ia5-sou e7 tui3 hia keng-koe3.  5) Ia5-sou lai5-kau3 hit e5 sou2-chai7 e5 si5, giah8-thau5 khi2-lai5 khoaN3, ka7 i kong2, 몮Sat-kai, li2 koaN2-kin2 loh8-lai5; in-ui7 Goa2 kin-na2-jit8 it-teng7 boeh khi3 toa3 lin2 hia.몯  6) I chiu7 koaN2-kin2 loh8-lai5, hoaN-hoaN-hi2-hi2 hoan-geng5 Ia5-sou.  7) Cheng3-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne, tai7-ke chiu7 khai-si2 kauh8-kauh8-liam7, kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 soah khi3 toa3 choe7-jin5 e5 chhu3 cho3 lang5-kheh.몯  8) Sat-kai chiu7 khia7 khi2-lai5, tui3 Chu2 kong2, 몮Chu2 a3! Goa2 boeh chiong goa2 e5 chai5-san2 e5 chit8 poaN3 chin2-che3 san3-chhiah-lang5, Goa2 na7 u7 khi-phian3 sim2-mih lang5, goa2 boeh si3-poe7 poe5 i.몯  9) Ia5-sou tui3 i kong2, 몮Kin-na2-jit8 kiu3-in i2-keng lai5-kau3 chit e5 ka-teng5 a7, in-ui7 chit e5 lang5 ia7-si7 a-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kiaN2-sun.  10) In-ui7 Jin5-chu2 lai5, si7 boeh chhoe7 sit-be5 e5 lang5 chhut-lai5, thang lai5 kiu3 in.몯

Chap8 niu2 kim-a2 e5 phi3-ju7: (Ma2 25:14-30)
	11) Cheng3-lang5 teh thiaN chiah-e5 oe7 e5 si5, Ia5-sou chiu7 koh soa3 loh8-khi3 kong2 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7. In-ui7 I teh-boeh kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 a3, sou2-i2 hia e5 lang5 chiu7 siuN7 kong2 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok liam5-piN teh-boeh chhut-hian7 a7.  12) In-ui7 an2-ne, Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮U7 chit8 e5 kui3-chok8 boeh khi3 chin hng7 e5 kok hou7 lang5 hong-cho3 kok-ong5 chiah boeh tng2-lai5.  13) I chiu7 tiau3-chip8 chap8 e5 lou5-pok8 lai5, mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 chit8 niu2 kim-a2 hou7 in, ka7 in kong2, 몬Eng7 chiah-e5 chiN5 khi3 cho3 seng-li2, cho3 kau3 goa2 tng2-lai5.몭  14) Tan7-si7 kap i kang7-kok e5 lang5 oan30hin7 i, sou2 i2 chhe tai7-piau2 toe3 i e5 au7-bin7 khi3 chau3 kong2, 몬Goan2 bo5 ai3 chit e5 lang5 cho3 goan2 e5 ong5.몭몯
	15) 몮Chit e5 kui3-chok8 hou7 lang5 hong-cho3 kok-ong5 tng2-lai5 e5 si5, chiu7 kio3 hiah-e5 i theh8 chiN5 hou7 in e5 lou5-pok8 lai5 i hia, boeh khoaN3 in mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 than3 loa7-che7.  16) Te7-it e5 lai5 i e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2, 몬Thau5-ke a3, goa2 eng7 li2 hit chit8 niu2 kim-a2, koh than3 chap8 niu2 a3.몭  17) Chu2-lang5 ka7 i kong2: 몬Chin ho2, li2 si7 ho2 e5 lou5-pok8! Li2 ki3-jian5 tui3 sio2-sio2 e5 tai7-chi3 cho3 kah chin tiong-sit8, sou2-i2 goa2 boeh hou7 li2 koan2-li2 chap8 e5 siaN5-chhi7.몭  18) Te7-ji7 e5 lai5 kong2, 몬Thau5-ke a3, goa2 eng7 li2 hit chit8 niu2 kim-a2, koh than3 gou7 niu2 a3.몭  19) Thau5-ke ia7 tui3 i kong2, 몬An2-ne goa2 ia7 boeh hou7 li2 koan2-li2 gou7 e5 siaN5-chhi7.몭  20) Te7-saN e5 jit8-lai5 kong2: 몬Thau5-ke a3, li2 hit chit8 niu2 kim-a2 ti7 chia. Goa2 eng7 chhiu2-kin ka7 i pau khi2-lai5 khng3.  21) Goa2 chin kiaN li2, in-ui7 li2 si7 chit8 ui7 khek-pok8 e5 lang5, bo5 kia3 loh8-khi3 ia7 boeh nia2 chhut-lai5, bo5 ia7-cheng2 ia7 boeh siu-seng5.몭  22) Chu2-lang5 in3 i kong2: 몬Li2 chit e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 lou5-pok8! Goa2 boeh chiau3 li2 ka-ti7 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 lai5 ka7 li2 phoaN3-choe7. Li2 ki3-jian5 chai-iaN2 goa2 si7 khek-pok8 e5 chu2-lang5, bo5 kia3 loh8-khi3 ia7 boeh nia2 chhut-lai5, bo5 ia7-cheng2 ia7 boeh siu-seng5.  23) An2-ne li2 an3-choaN2 m7 chiong goa2 e5 chiN5 kia3 toa3 gin5-hang5? Tan2 goa2 tng2-lai5 e5 si5 thang nia2 bo2-chiN5 kap li2-sek.몭  24) Chu2-lang5 chiu7 ka7 khia7 ti7 piN-a e5 lang5 kong2, 몬Ka7 i theh8 hit chit8 nia2 kim-a2 khi2-lai5, kau hou7 hit e5 u7 chap8 niu2 kim-a2 e5.몭  25) In chiu7 tui3 i kong2, 몬Thau5-ke a3, hit e5 lang5 i2-keng u7 chap8 niu2 kim-a2 a3.몭  26) I in3 kong2: 몬Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: na7-si7 i2-keng u7 e5 lang5, boeh koh-khah che7 hou7 i; bo5 e5, lian5 i sou2 u7 e5 chit8-sut-la2, ia7 boeh ka7 i theh8 khi2-lai5.  27) Iah hiah-e5 bo5 ai3 goa2 cho3 in e5 kok-ong5 e5 tek8-jin5, lin2 thoa in lai5 chia, toa3 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 ka7 in sat-hai7.몭몯

Ia5-sou choe3-au7 chin3-jip8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5: (Ma2 21:1-11; Kho2 11:1-11; Iok 12:12-19)
	28) Kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 liau2-au7, Ia5-sou chiu7 cho3-cheng3 ke3-siok8 chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  29) I lai5 teh-boeh kau3 kio3-cho3 Kan-na2-soaN e5 hu7-kin7 e5 Pek-hoat-ki5 kap Pek-tai7-ni5 e5 si5, chiu7 chhe nng7 e5 bun5-tou5,  30) hoan-hu3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 khi3 tui3-bin7 e5 chng-thau5. Chit8-e7 kau3-ui7, chiu7 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 chiah iau2 m7-bat hou7 lang5 khia5-koe3 e5 li5-a2-kiaN2 pak8 ti7 hia. Lin2 ka7 i thau2-khui, khan lai5 chia.  31) Na7 u7 lang5 mng7 lin2 kong2, 몬Lin2 an3-choaN2 boeh ka7 i thau2?몭 lin2 tioh8 ka7 i kong2, 몬chu2 teh khiam3-eng7.몭몯  32) Hit nng7 e5 bun5-tou5 chiu7 khi3. Ko2-jian5 tak8-hang7 tai7-chi3 kap Ia5-sou sou2 kong2 e5 kang7-khang2.  33) In teh thau2 hit chiah li5-a2-kiaN2 e5 si5, li5-a2-kiaN2 e5 chu2-lang5 mng7 in kong2, 몮Lin2 thau2 chit chiah li5-a2-kiaN2 boeh chhong3 sim2-mih?몯  34) In in3 kong2, 몮Chu2 teh khiam3-eng7.몯  35) In chiu7 khan hit chiah li5-a2-kiaN2 lai5 hou7 Ia5-sou, chiong in ka-ti7 e5 goa7-saN phoah8 toa3 li5-a2-kiaN2-teng2, hu5 Ia5-sou khit-khi3 khia5.  36) Ia5-sou khia5 li5-a2-kiaN2 teh kiaN5 e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 chiong ka-ti7 e5 goa7-saN phou toa3 lou7-nih8.  37) Ia5-sou lai5 teh-boeh kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng-siaN5, tu2-boeh loh8 Kan-na2-soaN e5 si5, in-ui7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 it-chhe3 ki5-biau7 e5 tai7-chi3, kui toa7 tin7 e5 bun5-tou5 long2 hoaN-hi2 toa7 siaN chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2,  38) kong2:
몮Goan7 hong7 Chu2 e5 mia5 lai5 e5 Kun-ong5 siu7 chiok-hok! Goan7 ho5-peng5 chai7 thian-siong7 eng5-iau7 chai7 chi3-ko chi thian!몯
	39) Cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, u7 kui2-na7 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Lau7-su, tioh8 chek-pi7 Li2 e5 bun5-tou5, kio3 in tiam7-tiam7!몯  40) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou in3 kong2, 몮Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, chiah-e5 lang5 na7 tiam7-tiam7, hiah-e5 chioh8-thau5 chiu7 e7 toa7 siaN hou-hiam3.몯

Ia5-sou ui7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5 lau5 bak8-sai2:
	41) Ia5-sou lai5 teh-boeh kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5, khoaN3-kiN3 siaN5 e5 si5, ui7-tioh8 chit e5 siaN5-chhi7 lau5 bak8-sai2,  42) kong2: 몮Choe3-chio2 li2 kin-na2-jit8 na7 e7-tang3 chai-iaN2 an3-choaN2 chiah e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 ho5-peng5, m7 chinho2! Tan7-si7 hian7-chai7 li2 khoaN3 be7 chhut!  43) In-ui7 jit8-chi2 teh-boeh kau3 a3, hit e5 si5 li2 e5 tek8-jin5 e7 chai7 li2 e5 chiu-ui5, cho3 po2-lui2 lai5 pau-ui5 li2, tui3 si3-bin7 ka7 li2 hong-so2 khi2-lai5;  44) ia7 e7 chiong li2 kap lin2 hui2-biat8; e7 bo5 chit8 te3 chioh8 kap chioh8 sio-thah8. Che si7 in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 lai5 chin2-kiu3 li2 e5 si5, li2 long2 m7 chai-iaN2 li2 e5 ho2 ki-hoe7.몯

Ia5-sou chheng Seng3-tian7: (Ma2 21:12-17; Kho2 11:15-19; Iok 2:13-22)
	45) Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 Seng3-tian7 chiu7 khai-si2 koaN2 hiah-e5 seng-li2-lang5 chhut-khi3.  46) I ka7 in kong2: 몮Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, 몬Goa2 e5 chhu3 eng-kai tioh8 cho3 ki5-to2 e5 chhu3.몭 Tan7-si7 lin2 ka7 i pian3-cho3 chhat8-siu7.몯
	47) Ia5-sou mui2 chit8 jit8 chai7 seng3-tian7 lai7 ka3-si7 lang5. Che3-si-tiuN2, keng-hak8-chia2 kap peh-seN3 e5 thau5-lang5, ke3-bou5 boeh sat-hai7 Ia5-sou,  48) tan7-si7 chhoe7 bo5 pan7-hoat, in-ui7 cheng3-lang5 long2 chin jiat8-sim teh thiaN I e5 oe7.

Te7 20 ChiuN

Lun7 Ia5-sou e5 koan5-peng3: (Ma2 21:23-27; Kho2 11:27-33)
	1) U7 chit8 jit8, Ia5-sou ti7 Seng3-tian7 lai7 teh ka3-si7 cheng3-lang5, ia7 teh thoan5 Hok-im e5 si5, u7 chit8-koa2 che3-si-tiuN2, keng-hak8-chia2 kap tiuN2-lo2 cho3-hoe2 lai5,  2) mng7 I kong2, 몮Li2 eng7 sim2-mih koan5-peng3 cho3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3? Sim2-mih lang5 hou7 Li2 chit e5 koan5-peng3 lai5 cho3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3?몯  3) Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: 몮Goa2 ia7 boeh mng7 lin2 chit8 ku3 oe7. Lin2 ka7 Goa2 in3-tap:  4) Iok-han7 ka7 lang5 se2-le2 e5 koan5-peng3 si7 tui3 thiN lai5 e5, a2-si7 tui3 lang5 lai5 e5?몯  5) In chiu7 hou7-siong gi7-lun7 kong2: 몮Lan2 na7-si7 kong2, 몬tui3 thiN lai5 e5,몭 I e7 ka7 lan2 kong2: 몬An2-ne lin2 an3-choaN2 bo5 boeh sin3 Iok-han7?몭  6) Tan7-si7 lan2 na7 kong2 si7 몬Tui3 lang5 lai5 e5,몭 cheng3-lang5 e7 eng7 chioh8-thau5 ka7 lan2 tim3-si2, in-ui7 in long2 siong-sin3 Iok-han7 si7 tai7-gian5-jin5.몯  7) Sou2-i2 in chiu7 in3 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Goan2 m7 chai-iaN2 si7 tui3 tah-ui7 lai5 e5.몯  8) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 in kong2, 몮An2-ne Goa2 ia7 bo5 boeh ka7 lin2 kong2 Goa2 si7 eng7 sim2-mih koan5-peng3 lai5 cho3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3.몯

Phu5-to5-hng5 e5 tian7-long5 e5 phi3-ju7: (Ma2 21:33-46; Kho2 12:1-12)
	9) Ia5-sou chiu7 eng7 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7 ka7 cheng3-lang5 kong2: 몮U7 chit8 e5 lang5 u7 chit8 te3 phu5-to5-hng5. I chiong chit te3 hng5 chou hou7 tian7-long5, chiu7 chhut-khi3 goa7-kok li2-heng5 chin ku2.  10) Siu-seng5 phu5-to5 e5 si5-ki5 chit8-e7 kau3, i chiu7 chhe chit8 e5 lou5-pok8 khi3 tian7-long5 hia, boeh tui3 in siu hng5-chou. Tan7-si7 tian7-long5 ka7 i liah8 khi2-lai5 phah, hou7 i khang-chhiu2 tng2-khi3.  11) Chu2-lang5 koh chhe pat8 e5 lou5-pok8 khi3 in hia. In ia7-si7 ka7 i phah, ka7 i bu2-jiok8, iu7-koh hou7 i khang-chhiu2 tng2-khi3.  12) Chu2-lang5 chiu7 chhe te7-saN e5 lou5-pok8 khi3. In ia7 ka7 i siong-hai7, ia7 ka7 i koaN2 chhut-khi3.  13) Choe3-au7 phu5-to5-hng5 e5 chu2-lang5 chiu7 kong2: 몬TaN goa2 m7-chai boeh an3-choaN2 lai5 cho3? Goa2 boeh chhe goa2 sim-ai3 e5 kiaN2 khi3. In tai7-khai3 e7 chun-tiong7 i.몭  14) Tan7-si7 hiah-e5 tian7-long5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 i, chiu7 hou7-siong chham-siong5 kong2: 몬Chit e5 si7 i e5 ke3-seng5-jin5. Lan2 lai5 ka7 i sat-hai7, an2-ne i sou2 boeh ke3-seng5 e5 san2-giap8 chiu7 e7 piN3-cho3 lan2 e5.몭  15) In chiu7 ka7 i tan3 chhut-khi3 phu5-to5-hng5 e5 goa7-bin7, ka7 i thai5-si2.몯
	몮An2-ne, phu5-to5-hng5 e5 chu2-lang5 e7 an3-choaN2 lai5 chhu2-li2 in?  16) I it-teng7 e7 lai5 thai5-si2 chiah-e5 tian7-long5, ji5-chhiaN2 e7 chiong i e5 phu5-to5-hng5 chou hou7 pat8-lang5!몯 Cheng3-lang5 chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7, chiu7 kong2, 몮Chhian-ban7 m7-thang an2-ne!몯  17) Ia5-sou kim-kim ka7 in khoaN3, kong2: 몮Seng3-keng ki3-chai3 kong2:
몬Khi2-chhu3 sai-hu7 sou2 tan3-tiau7 e5 chioh8 soah piN3-cho3 siong7 tiong7-iau3 e5 ki-chioh8!몭
Chit ku3 si7 sim2-mih i3-su3?  18) Na7 poah8 loh8-khi3 hit liap8 chioh8-thau5 teng2 e5 lang5 e7 chhui3-kut hun-sin, hou7 hit liap8 chioh8-thau5 teh-tioh8 e5 lang5, e7 iu3-boah8-boah8.몯

Lap8 soe3-kim e5 bun7-te5: (Ma2 22:15-22; Kho2 12:13-17)
	19) Keng-hak8-chia2 kap che3-si-tiuN2 chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou kong2 chit e5 phi3-ju7 si7 teh chi2 in, chiu7 siuN7-boeh tong-tiuN5 he7-chhiu2 liah8 Ia5-sou, tan7-si7 ia7 kiaN cheng3-lang5.  20) Sou2-i2 in chiu7 teh siong3 ki-hoe7, chhe bit8-tham3 ke2-cho3 lau2-sit8-lang5, boeh liah8 I e5 oe7-phang7, thang kau I hou7 koaN-thiaN kap chong2-tok e5 hoat-koaN.  21) chiah-e5 bit8-tham3 lai5 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Lau7-su, goan2 chai-iaN2 Li2 sou2 kong2 e5 kap sou2 ka3-si7 e5 long2 chin tioh8. Li2 long2 bo5 koan lang5 e5 bin7-sek, chi2-u7 chiau3 chin-li2 lai5 ka3-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 to7-lou7.  22) Lap8-soe3 hou7 Lo5-ma2 e5 Hong5-te3 u7 hah8 lan2 e5 Lut8-hoat a2 bo5?몯  23) Ia5-sou khoaN3-thau3 in e5 kui2-ke3, chiu7 tui3 in kong2,  24) 몮Lin2 theh8 chit8 e5 gin5-oan5 lai5 hou7 Goa2 khoaN3. Hit e5 gin5-oan5 e5 siong7 kap ji7-ho7 si7 sim2-mih lang5 e5?몯 In in3 kong2, 몮Si7 Hong5-te3 e5.몯  25) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 in kong2, 몮Na7-si7 an2-ne, lin2 tioh8 chiong Hong5-te3 e5, lap8 hou7 Hong5-te3, chiong /siong7-chu2 e5, hian3 hou7 Siong7-chu2.몯  26) In ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 be7-tang3 liah8-tioh8 Ia5-sou e5 oe7-phang7, iu7-koh thiaN-tioh8 I e5 in3-tap chin tioh8-kiaN, soah tiam7-khi3.

Si2-lang5 hok8-hoat8 e5 bun7-te5: (Ma2 22:23-33; Kho2 12:18-27)
	27) U7 chit8-koa2 Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 lang5 lai5 chhoe7 Ia5-sou. (In chiu7-si7 chu2-tiuN kong2 si2-lang5 be7 koh-oah8 hiah-e5 lang5.) In mng7 Ia5-sou kong2:  28) 몮Lau7-su, Mou5-se ka7 goan2 kui-teng7 kong2: 몬Na7 u7 lang5 a-hiaN si2-khi3, lau5 i e5 bou2, tan7-si7 bo5 seN-kiaN2, i e5 sio2-ti7 tioh8 chhoa7 in hiaN-so2 cho3 bou2, ui7-tioh8 a-hiaN lai5 thoan5-chong chiap-tai7.몭  29) Khah-cha2 u7 chhit e5 hiaN-ti7, toa7 e5 chhoa7 bou2, bo5 seN-kiaN2 chiu7 si2-khi3.  30) Te7-ji7 e5, chhoa7 in hiaN-so2 cho3 bou2, ia7 bo5 seN-kiaN2 chiu7 si2-khi3.  31) Te7-saN e5 ia7-si7 an2-ne chiap in hiaN-so2 lai5 cho3 bou2. Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne in chhit e5 hiaN-ti7 long2 u7 kap chit e5 hu7-jin5-=lang5 kiat-hun koe3, bo5 lau5 hio7-su5 chiu7 si2-khi3.  32) Choe3-au7 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 ia7 si2-khi3.  33) In-ui7 in chhit e5 long2 bat kap i kiat-hun koe3, taN kau3 hok8-hoat8 hit jit8, si2-lang5 long2 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5 e5 si5, chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kiu3-keng3 si7 tah chit8 e5 lang5 e5 bou2?몯  34) Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: 몮Chit se3-kan e5 lang5 chiah u7 ke3-chhoa7;  35) tan7-si7 hiah-e5 e7-kham-tit tit-tioh8 lai5-se3 e5 seng-oah8 kap e7-kham-tit tui3 si2-lang5 tiong hok8-hoat8 khi2-lai5 e5 lang5, peng3 bo5 ke3-chhoa7.  36) In be7 koh-chai3 si2, in-ui7 in chhin-chhiuN7 thian-sai3. Ki3-jian5 tui3 si2-lang5 tiong hok8-hoat8 khi2-lai5, in si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 kiaN2-ji5.  37) Mou5-se i2-keng ti7 몬Teh toh8 e5 chhi3-phi3몭 hit toaN7, chi2-beng5 si2-lang5 e7 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5. I ti7 hit toaN7 chheng-hou 몬Chu2 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-chu2, I2-sat e5 Siong7-chu2, Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-chu2.몭  38) I m7-si7 si2-lang5 e5 Siong7-chu2, si7 oah8-lang5 e5 Siong7-chu2. In-ui7 tui3 Siong7-chu2 khoaN3 khi2-lai5, lang5 long2 si7 teh oah8 e5."몯 39) U7 kui2-na7 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 tui3 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Lau7-su, Li2 in3 liau2 chin ho2.몯  40) An2-ne in chiu7 long2 m7-kaN2 koh mng7 I sim2-mih.

Iu2-koan Bi2-sia3-a e5 bun7-te5: (Ma2 22:41-46; Kho2 12:35-37)
	41) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Kam2 e7-eng7-tit kong2 Bi2-sai3-a si7 Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun?  42) In-ui7 Tai7-pit8 ka-ti7 ti7 Si-phian e5 lai7-bin7 u7 kong2:
몬Siong7-chu2 tui3 Goa2 e5 Chu2 kong: Che7 toa3 Goa2 e5 chiaN3-peng5,  43) It-tit8 kau3 goa2 hou7 Li2 e5 tek8-jin5 cho3 kha-tiam7 lai5 hou7 Li2 khoe3 kha.몭
44) An2-ne Tai7-pit8 ki3-jian5 chheng-hou I cho3 Chu2, Bi2-sai3-a na2 e7 lai5 cho3 Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun?몯

Tioh8 ti5-hong5 keng-hak8-chia2: (Ma2 23:1-36; Kho2 12:38-40)
	45) Cheng-lang5 teh thiaN e5 si5, Ia5-sou tui3 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2:  46) 몮Tioh8 keng2-kai3 keng-hak8-chia2. In ai3 chheng7 tng5-phau3 si3-ke3 kiaN5, ti7 ke-chhi7 ai3 lang5 ka7 in kiaN5 toa7-le2, ti7 hoe7-tng5 ai3 che7 koan5 e5 ui7, ian3-sek8 che7-toh e5 si5 ai3 che7 toa7 ui7.  47) In thun-chiah8 koaN2-hu7 e5 ke-hoe2, ke2-i3 ki5-to2 chin ku2. In it-teng7 e7 siu7-tioh8 koh-khah giam5-tiong7 e5 heng5-hoat8.몯

Te7 21 ChiuN

Chiu2-koaN2-lang5 e5 hong7-hian3: (Kho2 12:41-44)
	1) Ia5-sou bak8-chiu chit8-e7 khoaN3 koan5, khoaN3-kiN3 ho2-giah8-lang5 teh hiat chiN5 loh8-khi3 hian3-kim-siuN.  2) I ia7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 chin san3 e5 koaN2-hu7 hian3 nng7 e5 tang5-chiN5-a2 loh8-khi3.  3) Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, chit e5 san3-chhiah e5 koaN2-hu7 sou2 hian3 e5, pi2 ki5-tha mui2 chit8 e5 to khah che7.  4) In-ui7 ki5-tha e5 lang5 long2 si7 hian3-chhut in eng7 chhun e5 chai5-hu3 e5 chit8 sio2 pou7-hun7; tan7-si7 chit e5 koaN2-hu7 sui-jian5 chin san3, i chiong sou2 u7 e5 seng-oah8-hui3 long2 hian3 loh8-khi3.몯

Ia5-sou i7-gian5 Seng3-tian7 e5 hui2-biat8: (Ma2 24:1-2; Kho2 13:1-2)
	5) U7 chit8-koa2 lang5 teh tam5-lun7 Seng3-tian7 eng7 hiah-nih8 sui2 e5 chioh8 lai5 khi2, ia7 eng7 hiah-nih8 che7 hong7-hian3 e5 mih8 lai5 chong-sek, sit8-chai7 chin tong5-hong5. Hit e5 si5, Ia5-sou chiu7 kong2:  6) 몮Lin2 hian7-chai7 sou2 teh khoaN3 chiah-e5 it-chhe3, u7 chit8 jit8 ti7 chia bo5 chit8 te3 chioh8 e7 sio-thah8, long2 e7 to2 kah peN5-peN5-peN5.몯

Chai-lan7 e5 khai-si2: (Ma2 24:3-14; Kho2 13:3-13)
	7) In chiu7 mng7 I kong2: 몮Lau7-su, chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 sim2-mih si5 e7 hoat-seng? Chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3 teh-boeh hoat-seng e5 si5, u7 sim2-mih chian5-tiau7?몯
	8) Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Tioh8 chu3-i3 , m7-thang hou7 lang5 be5-hek8 khi3. In-ui7 u7 chin-che7 lang5 e7 mou7-iong7 Goa2 e5 mia5 lai5, kong2, 몬goa2 chiu7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a.몭 iu7-koh kong2, 몬Si5-khek teh-boeh kau3 a3.몭 Lin2 m7-thang toe3 in khi3.  9) Lin2 na7 thiaN-kiN3 u7 chian3-cheng kap kek-beng7 e5 si5, m7-thang tioh8-kiaN! In-ui7 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 it-teng7 tioh8-ai3 tai7-seng hoat-seng; tan7-si7 chiong-kiok8 be7 sui5-si5 kau3.  10) Ia5-sou koh ke3-siok8 kong2: 몮Bin5-chok8 e7 khi2-lai5 kong-kek bin5-chok8, kok-ka e7 kong-kek kok-ka.  11) Tak8 sou2-chai7 e7 hoat-seng toa7 te7-tang7, ki-hng kap un-ek8; thiN-teng2 e7 hian2-chhut hiong-tiau7 kap toa7 chian5-tiau7.  12) Tan7-si7 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 iau2-boe7 hoat-seng i2-cheng5, lin2 chiu7 e7 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3 pek-hai7; chiong lin2 kau hou7 hoe7-tng5, ka7 lin2 koaiN loh8 kaN-gak8. Lin2 e7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 chiah hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3 kok-ong5 kap chong2-tok e5 bin7-cheng5.  13) Che si7 lin2 cho3 kian3-cheng3 e5 ho2 ki-hoe7.  14) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8-ai3 koat-i3, m7-bian2 tai7-seng kho2-li7 boeh an3-choaN2 tap-pian7.  15) In-ui7 Goa2 boeh siuN2-su3 lin2 chin ho2 e5 khau2-chai5 kap ti3-hui7, thang hou7 lin2 e5 tek8-jin5 bo5 chit8 e5 e7-tang3 khong3-pian7, e7-tang3 hoan2-pok.  16) Lian5 lin2 e5 pe7-bo2, hiaN-ti7, chhin-chhek kap peng5-iu2 ia7 e7 chhut-be7 lin2; lin2 e5 tiong-kan u7-e5 e7 hou7 lang5 sat-hai7.  17) Lin2 e7 in-ui7 Goa2 hou7 cheng3-lang5 oan3-hin7.  18) Tan7-si7 lin2 lian5 chit8 ki thau5-mng5 ia7 be7 sit-loh8.  19) Lin2 na7 kian-jim2 tau3-te2, chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8 chin-chiaN3 e5 seN3-mia7.몯

Ia5-sou i7-gian5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 biat8-bong5: (Ma2 24:15-21; Kho2 13:14-19)
	20) 몮Lin2 na7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 hou7 kun-tui7 pau-ui5 khi2-lai5, an2-ne lin2 chiu7 e7 chai-iaN2 chit e5 siaN5 biat8-bong5 e5 si5 teh-boeh kau3 a3.  21) Hit e5 si5, toa3 ti7 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 e5 lang5 tioh8 to5-chau2 khi3 soaN-teng2; ti7 chit e5 siaN5-lai7 e5, tioh8-ai3 li7-khui; ti7 hiong-chhoan e5, m7-thang jip8-khi3 chit e5 siaN5-lai7.  22) In-ui7 che si7 몬Heng5-hoat8 e5 Jit8-chi2,몭 chiu7-si7 boeh eng3-giam7 Seng3-keng sou2 ki3-chai3 e5 it-chhe3.  23) Ti7 hit e5 si5-ki5, u7 sin-in7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kap hou7 eN-a2 chiah8-leng e5 lau7-bo2 sit8-chai7 chin put-heng7! In-ui7 chit e5 te7-hng e7 u7 toa7 chai-lan7. Siong7-chu2 e7 tui3 chit e5 peh-seN3 hoat toa7 siu7-khi3.  24) In e7 hou7 kiam3 thai5-si2, ia7 e7 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3 se3-kai3 kok-kok. Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5 e7 hou7 goa7-pang-lang5 thun2-tah8 kau3 in chiam3-leng2 e5 si5-ki5 moa2.몯

Jin5-chu2 e5 chai3-lim5: (Ma2 24:29-31; Kho2 13:24-27)
	25) 몮Ti7 thian-siong7, jit8, goeh8 kap chheN e7 hian2-chhut i7-tiau7; ti7 te7-siong7, ban7-bin5 e7 in-ui7 toa7-hai2 hong-eng2 e5 hou-hau2, kiaN kah m7 chai boeh an3-choaN2 chiah ho2.  26) Lang5 e7 in-ui7 tan2-thai7 chit se3-kai3 teh-boeh hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3, lai5 kiaN kah hun7 to2 loh8-khi3; in-ui7 thiN-teng2 e5 ban7-siong7 long2 e7 tong7-iau5.  27) Hit e5 si5, lang5 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Jin5-chu2 toa3 toa7 koan5-leng5 kap toa7 eng5-iau7 che7 hun5 lai5-lim5.  28) Chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 khai-si2 hoat-seng e5 si5, lin2 tioh8 theng5-sin giah8-thau5 khoaN3 koan5, in-ui7 lin2 teh-boeh tit-tioh8 kiu3-siok8 a7.몯

Bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7 e5 kau3-hun3: (Ma2 24:32-35; Kho2 13:28-31)
	29) Ia5-sou eng7 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7 ka7 in kong2: 몮Tioh8 chu3-i3 bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7 kap sou2 u7 e5 chhiu7-bak8.  30) Lin2 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 puh-iN2 chhut-lai5 e5 si5, chiu7 chai-iaN2 he7-thiN teh-boeh kau3 a3.  31) Kap an2-ne kang7-khoan2, lin2 na7 khoaN3-tioh8 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 hoat-seng e5 si5, lin2 chiu7 chai-iaN2 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok teh-boeh kau3 a3.몯
