	32) 몮Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 iau2-boe7 si2 i2-cheng5, chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 long2 e7 hoat-seng.  33) ThiN-te7 e7 siau-biat8, tan7-si7 goa2 e5 oe7 choat8-tui3 be7 siau-biat8.몯

Tioh8-ai3 kin2-sin7:
	34) 몮Lin2 tioh8-ai3 kin2-sin7! M7-thang hou7 lin2 e5 sim ui7-tioh8 tham-chiah8, chiu2-chui3 kap se3-siok8 e5 khoa3-li7 lai5 hun-be5-khi3, in-ui7 se3-kai3 e5 Boat8-jit8 e7 hut-jian5-kan lai5-lim5,  35) chhin-chhiuN7 oah8-tauh-a2 piak8 chit8-e7, chiu7 lai5 kau3 choan5 se3-kai3 e5 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 hia.  36) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8-ai3 keng2-seng2, si5-siong5 ki5-kiu5 Siong7-chu2 siuN2-su3 lin2 lek8-tiong7, hou7 lin2 e7 tang3 to5-pi7 chiah-e5 teh-boeh hoat-seng e5 hoan7-lan7, lai5 toa3 Jin5-chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 khia7 chai7-chai7.몯
	37) Ia5-sou mui2-jit8 jit8-si5 toa3 Seng3-tian7 ka3-si7 lang5, me5-si5 chiu7 chhut-khi3 Kan-na2-soaN keh-me5.  38) Cheng3-alng5 long2 thau3-cha2 chiu7 khi3 Seng3-tian7, thiaN I kong2 to7-li2.

Te7 22 ChiuN

Ham7-hai7 Ia5-sou e5 im-bou5: (Ma2 26:1-5; Kho2 14:1-2; Iok 11:45-53)
	1) Bo5-kaN3-cheh, ia7 kio3-cho3 PoaN5-koe3-cheh teh-boeh kau3 a3.  2) Che3-si-tiuN2 kap keng-hak8-chia2 boeh chhoe7 khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih khah ho2 e5 hoat-tou7 thang lai5 sat-hai7 Ia5-sou; in-ui7 in chin kiaN peh-seN3.

Iu5-tai7 tong5-i3 chhut-be7 Ia5-sou: (Ma2 26:14-16; Kho2 14:10-11)
	3) Hit e5 si5, Sat-tan3 chiu7 chin3 jip8-khi3 hit e5 kio3-cho3 Ka-liok8 e5 Iu5-tai7 e5 sim-lai7. I si7 chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 e5 chit8 e5.  4) I chiu7 khi3 kap hiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 i2-kip8 Seng3-tian7 e5 siu2-oe7-tiuN2 chham-siong5 khoaN3 boeh eng7 sim2-mih hoat-tou7 lai5 kau Ia5-sou hou7 in.  5) In chin hoaN-hi2, chiu7 iok boeh chiN5 hou7 i.  6) Iu5-tai7 tong5-i3 liau2-au7, chiu7 khai-si2 chhoe7 khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih ho2 ki-hoe7, mai3 hou7 kun3-chiong3 chai-iaN2, thang chiong Ia5-sou kau hou7 in.

Ia5-sou chun2-pi7 chiah8 PoaN5-koe3-cheh e5 boan2-chhan: (Ma2 26:17-25; Kho2 14:12-21; Iok 13:21-30)
	7) Bo5-kaN3-cheh kau3 a3. Hit jit8 tioh8-ai3 thai5 PoaN5-koe3-cheh e5 iuN5-a2-kiaN2.  8) Ia5-sou chhe-phai3 Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7, ka7 in hoan-hu3 kong2: 몮Lin2 khi3 chun2-pi7 lan2 e5 PoaN5-koe3-cheh e5 boan2-chhan.몯  9) In mng7 I kong2, 몮Li2 ai3 goan2 khi3 sim2-mih sou2-chai7 chun2-pi7?몯  10) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Chu3-i3 thiaN! Lin2 jip8-khi3 siaN5-lai7 chiu7 e7 tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 koaN7 chui2-pan5 e5 lang5. Lin2 tioh8 toe3 i jip8-khi3 i jip8-khi3 hit keng chhu3,  11) mng7 hit ke e5 chu2-lang5 kong2: 몬Lau7-su kau-tai3 goan2 mng7 li2 kong2: Goa2 kap Goa2 e5 bun5-tou5 boeh chiah8 PoaN5-koe3-cheh e5 boan2-chhan e5 kheh-thiaN ti7 sim2-mih sou2-chai7?몭  12) Hit e5 lang5 e7 po3 lin2 khoaN3 lau5-teng2 chit8 keng i2-keng pou3-ti3 ho2-se3 e5 toa7 kheh-thiaN. Lin2 chiu7 toa3 hia chun2-pi7.몯  13) In chiu7 khi3. Tak8-hang7 tai7-chi3 ko2-jian5 chiau3 Ia5-sou sou2 kong2 e5 an2-ne, in chiu7 toa3 hia pi7-pan7 PoaN5-koe3-cheh e5 boan2-chhan.

Chu2 e5 boan2-chhan: (Ma2 26:26-30; Kho2 14:22-26; 1 Ko-lim5-to 11:23-25)
	14) Si5-kan chit8-e7 kau3, Ia5-sou chiu7 kap I e5 Su3-tou5 che7-toh.  15) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Goa2 siu7-lan7 i2-cheng5, chin khat-bong7 kap lin2 chiah8 chit tng3 PoaN5-koe3-cheh e5 boan2-chhan.  16) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, in-ui7 tui3 hian7-chai7 khi2, it-tit8 kau3 chit e5 PoaN5-koe3-cheh e5 i3-gi7 ti7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok eng3-kiam7 hit e5 si5, Goa2 choat8-tui3 be7 koh chiah8 chit khoan2 e5 boan2-chhan.몯  17) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou phang5 poe khi2-lai5, chiok-sia7 liau2-au7, kong2: 몮Lin2 phang5 chit poe khi3 tai7-ke cho3-hoe2 lim.  18) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, in-ui7 tui3 hian7-chai7 khi2, it-tit8 kau3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok lai5-lim5 hit e5 si5, Goa2 choa8-tui3 be7 koh lim phu5-to5-chiu2.몯  19) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou theh8 mi7-pau khi2-lai5, chiok-sia7 liau2-au7 peh-khui pun hou7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: 몮Che si7 Goa2 e5 seng-khu, (si7 ui7-tioh8 lin2 hi-seng e5. Lin2 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ne cho3, lai5 ki3-liam7 Goa2.몯  20) Boan2-chhan au7, I ia7 chiau3 an2-ne phang5 poe khi2-lai5, kong2: 몮Chit poe si7 eng7 Goa2 teh-boeh ui7 lin2 lau5 chhut-lai5 e5 hoeh sou2 lip8 e5 sin e5 beng5-iok.몯)
	21) 몮Lin2 khoaN3! Chhut-be7 Goa2 hit e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2 kap Goa2 e5 chhiu2, ti7 kang7 chit8 te3 toh-teng2!  22) In-ui7 Jin5-chu2 e7 chiau3 Siong7-chu2 sou2 i7-teng7 e5 lai5 si2; tan7-si7 chhut-be7 I e5 lang5 tioh8 u7 chai-ho7!몯  23) In chiu7 khai-si2 hou7-siong mng7 kong2 in tiong-kan kiu3-keng3 tah chit8 e5, e7 cho3 chit khoan2 tai7-chi3.

Sim2-mih lang5 si7 siong7 toa7 e5?
	24) Chai7 bun5-tou5 e5 tiong-kan cheng-lun7 kong2 in tiong-kan sim2-mih lang5 sng3 cho3 si7 siong7 toa7 e5.  25) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Goa7-pang-lang5 e5 kun-ong5 eng7 koan5-peng3 thong2-ti7 in e5 peh-seN3; chip-heng5 koan5-ui e5 tiuN2-koaN, in ka7 i chheng-hou cho3 몬Jin5-bin5 e5 in-chu2.몭  26) Tan7-si7 lin2 e5 tiong-kan m7-thang chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne! Lin2 e5 tiong-kan siong7 toa7 e5, tian-to3 tioh8 chiaN5-cho3 chhin-chhiuN7 siong7 siau3-lian5 e5; cho3 leng2-siu7 e5, tian-to3 tioh8 chhin-chhiuN7 lou5-pok8.  27) Kiu3-keng3 sim2-mih lang5 khah toa7? Si7 hit e5 che7-toh e5, a2-si7 hit e5 chau2-toh e5? Tong-jian5 si7 che7-toh e5. Tan7-si7 Goa2 ti7 lin2 e5 tiong-kan, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hit e5 chau2-toh e5몯
	28) 몮Tan7-si7 lin2 chiah-e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 chai7 Goa2 e5 chhi3-lian7 tiong, si2-chiong kap Goa2 cho3-hoe2 e5.  29) Chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 e5 Hu7-chhin chiong ong5-ui7 su3 hou7 Goa2, Goa2 ia7 boeh chiong ong5-ui7 siuN2-su3 hou7 lin2,  30) hou7 lin2 chai7 Goa2 e5 Ong5-kok lai5 kap Goa2 che7-toh, lim-chiah8; peng3-chhiaN2 che7 toa3 po2-cho7, lai5 sim2-phoaN3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chap8-ji7 chi-phai3.몯


I7-gian5 Pi2-tek m7-jin7 Chu2: (Ma2 26:31-35; Kho2 14:27-31; Iok 13:36-38)
	31) 몮Se-bun5 a3, Se-bun5 a3, tioh8 chu3-i3 thiaN! Sat-tan3 u7 tit-tioh8 in2-chun2, boeh chhin-chhiuN7 long5-hu teh thai beh8-a2 an2-ne ka7 lin2 thai, lai5 ka7 lin2 tai7-ke chhi3-tham3;  32) tan7-si7 Se-bun5, Goa2 i2-keng u7 ui7-tioh8 li2 ki5-kiu5, hou7 li2 be7 song3-sit sin3-sim. Li2 hoe5-sim choan2-i3 liau2-au7, tioh8 kian-kou3 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 e5 sin3-sim.몯  33) Se-bun5 in3 I kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, goa2 kak-gou7 boeh kap Li2 khi3 che7 kaN-gak8, kap Li2 cho3-hoe2 si2.몯  34) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2: 몮Pi2-tek, Goa2 ka7 li2 kong2, kin-na2-jit8 ke iau2-boe7 thi5, li2 chiu7 e7 saN pai2 m7-jin7 Goa2.몯

ChiN5-te7-a2 kap to-kiam3:
	35) Ia5-sou ka7 bun5-tou5 kong2: 몮Khah-cha2 Goa2 chhe-phai3 lin2 khi3 thoan5-kau3 e5 si5, lin2 bo5 toa3 chiN5-te7-a2, ia7 bo5 toa3 li2-heng5-te7, ia7 bo5 toa3 e5, lin2 kam2 u7 khiam3-eng7 sim2-mih?몯 In in3 kong2, 몮Bo5 khiam3 poaN3 hang7.몯  36) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Tan7-si7 hian7-chai7, u7 chiN5-te7-a2 e5 tioh8 koaN7-khi3; bo5 kiam3 e5 lang5 tioh8-ai3 be7 ka-ti7 e5 goa7-saN khi3 be2 chit8 ki.  37) Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, 몬I ia7 hou7 ka7 I sng3-cho3 hoan7-lang5.몭 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, chit ku3 oe7 it-teng7 tioh8 chai7 Goa2 e5 sin-siong7 eng3-giam7. Su7-sit8-siong7 Seng3-keng sou2 ki3-chai3 koan-he7 Goa2 e5 tai7-chi3, i2-keng teh-boeh eng3-giam7 a7.몯  38) In kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, li2 khoaN3, ti7 chia u7 nng7 ki kiam3.몯 Ia5-sou in3 kong2, 몮An2-ne ho2 a3! Ho2-a3!몯

Ia5-sou e5 ki5-tou2: (Ma2 26:36-46; Kho2 14:32-42)
	39) Ia5-sou chhut-mng5, chiau3-siong5 khi3-kau3 Kan-na2-soaN. Bun5-tou5 ia7 toe3 I khi3.  40) Khi3-kau3 I siong5-siong5 khi3 hit e5 sou2-chai7, Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2, 몮Tioh8 ki5-to2, chiah be7 ham7-loh8 iu2-hek8.몯  41) Jian5-au7 I chiu7 li7-khui in, khi3-kau3 hiat chit8 liap8 chioh8-thau5 hiah hng7 e5 sou2-chai7, kui7 loh8-khi3 ki5-to2,  42) kong2: 몮Hu7-chhin a3, Li2 na7 kheng2, chiong chit e5 khou2-poe ka7 Goa2 phang5-chau2! Tan7-si7 m7-thang chiau3 Goa2 e5 i3-su3, tioh8 chiau3 Li2 e5 i3-su3!몯  ( 43) U7 chit8 ui7 thian-sai3 tui3 thiN hian2-hian7 lai5 I hia, lai5 cheng7-ka I e5 lek8-liong7.  44) Ia5-sou sim-lai7 hui-siong7 kan-khou2, lu2 jiat8-sim ki5-to2. I e5 koaN7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8-tih-chit8-tih e5 hoeh tih loh8-khi3 thou5-kha.)
	45) Ki5-to2 soah, Ia5-sou khia7 khi2-lai5, tng2-khi3 bun5-tou5 hia, khoaN3-kiN3 in pi-siong koe3-thau5 soah khun3-khi3.  46) I chiu7 ka7 in kong2, 몮Lin2 na2 e7 teh khun3? Khi2-lai5 ki5-to2, chiah be7 ham7-loh8 iu2-hek8.몯

Ia5-sou hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3: (Ma2 26:47-56; Kho2 14:43-50; Iok 18:3-11)
	47) Ia5-sou iau2 teh kong2-oe7 e5 si5, chiu7 u7 chit8 tin7 lang5 lai5 kau3-ui7; chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 e5 chit8 e5, hit e5 kio3-cho3 Iu5-tai7 e5, cho3-cheng5 teh chhoa7 lou7! I lai5-kau3 Ia5-sou hia boeh ka7 I chim.  48) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2, 몮Iu5-tai7! Li2 chim chit8 e7 boeh lai5 chhut-be7 Jin5-chu2 si7 bo5?몯  49) Kap Ia5-sou cho3-tin7 e5 bun5-tou5, khoaN3-kiN3 teh boeh hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3 chiu7 kong2, 몮Chu2, goan2 thang eng7 kiam3 bo5?몯  50) In ki5-tiong e5 chit8 e5, ka7 Toa7-che3-si e5 lou5-pok8 phut loh8-khi3, chiong i chiaN3-peng5 e5 hiN7-a2 siah khi2-lai5.  51) Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Soah khi3! An2-ne ho2 a3!몯 I chiu7 bong hit e5 lou5-pok8 e5 hiN7-a2, ka7 i i-ho2 khi3.
	52) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 hiah-e5 lai5 boeh liah8 I e5 Che3-si-tiuN2, Seng3-tian7 e5 si7-oe7-tiuN2 kap tiuN2-lo2 kong2: 몮Lin2 kam2 tioh8 giah8 kiam3 kpa thui5-a2 chhut-lai5? Be7 su boeh liah8 chit8 e5 thou2-hui2.  53) Goa2 tak8-jit8 kap lin2 cho3-hoe2 ti7 Seng3-tian7 lai7, lin2 ia7 bo5 siuN7-boeh he7-chhiu2 lai5 liah8 Goa2, tan7-si7 chim2-ma2 si7 lin2 tng ang e5 si5, ia7 si7 ou-am3 e5 thian-ha7!몯

Pi2-tek m7-jin7 Ia5-sou: (Ma2 26:57-58,69-75; Kho2 14:53-54,66-72; Iok 18:12-18,25-27)
	54) In liah8 Ia5-sou, ah I khi3-kau3 Toa7-che3-si e5 kong-koan2. Pi2-tek li7 hng7-hng7 toe3 in khi3.  55) U7 lang5 ti7 tiaN5-nih8 e5 tiong-ngt khi2-hoe2. Pi2-tek ia7 khi3 che7 toa3 hiah-e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan.  56) U7 chit8 e5 li2-pi7 khoaN3-kiN3 Pi2-tek che7 ti7 hia teh hang-hoe2 e5 si5, chiu7 kim-kim ka7 i khoaN3, kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 ia7 si7 kap Ia5-sou tau3-tin7 e5.몯  57)  Tan7-si7 Pi2-tek m7 seng5-jin7, kong2: 몮Cha-bou2-gin2-na2, goa2 lian5 bat I ma7 m7-bat!몯  58) Koe3 bo5 loa7-ku2, leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 i, kong2, 몮Li2 ia7 si7 in tiong-kan e5 chit8 e5.몯 Pi2-tek kong2, 몮Peng5-iu2 a3, goa2 m7-si7.몯  59) Chha-put-to koh koe3 chit8 tiam2-cheng, iu7-koh chit8 e5 lang5 toan3-gian3 kong2: 몮Chit e5 lang5 khak-sit8 ia7 u7 kap I tau3-tin7, in-ui7 i ia7 si7 Ka-li7-li7-lang5.몯  60) Pi2-tek kong2, 몮Peng5-iu2 a3, goa2 m7 chai-iaN2 li2 teh kong2 sim2-mih!몯 I iau2 teh kong2 e5 si5, ke sui5-si5 chiu7 thi5.  61) Chu2 oat8 koe3-lai5 kim-kim khoaN3 Pi2-tek. Pi2-tek chiu7 siuN7-khi2 Chu2 tui3 i sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2, 몮Kin-na2-jit8 ke thi5 i2-cheng5, li2 e7 saN pai2 m7-jin7 Goa2.몯  62) I chiu7 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7, toa7-siaN thi5-khau3.

Hi3-lang7 Ia5-sou: (Ma2 26:67-68; Kho2 14:65)
	63) Hiah-e5 khan3-siu2 Ia5-sou e5 lang5, ka7 I hi3-lang7, koh ka7 I phah.  64) In ng I e5 bak8-chiu, mng7 I kong2, 몮Li2 na7-si7 tai7-gian5-jin5, ioh khoaN3 sim2-mih lang5 ka7 Li2 phah!몯  65) In koh kong2 chin-che7 oe7 ka7 I bu2-jiok8.

Ia5-sou chai7 kong-gi7-hoe7 siu7-sim2: (Ma2 26:59-66; Kho2 14:55-64; Iok 18:19-24)
	66) ThiN chit8-e7 kng, Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 tiuN2-lo2, che3-si-tiuN2 kap keng-hak8-chia2 chiu7 khai-hoe7, chiong Ia5-sou ah khi3 in e5 kong-gi7-hoe7.  67) In ka7 I kong2, "몮i2 na7 chiaN5-sit8 si7 Bi2-sai3-a, Li2 tioh8 sit8-chai7 ka7 goan2 kong2." 몯a5-sou in3 in kong2: "G몮a2 na7 ka7 lin2 kong2, lin2 ia7 m7 sin3 Goa2,  68) Goa2 na7 mng7 lin2, lin2 ia7 m7 in3 Goa2.  69) Tan7-si7 tui3 hian7-chai7 khi2, Jin5-chu2 e7 che7 toa3 Choan5-leng5-chia2 Siong7-chu2 e5 chiaN3-peng5."  몯0) Cheng3-lang5 long2 kong2, "An몮-ne, Li2 chiu7-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2 si7 bo5?" I몯5-sou in3 in kong2, "Si7, chiau3 lin2 kong2 an2-ne.몯  71) In kong2, 몮Lan2 iau2 tioh8 koh su-iau3 sim2-mih cheng3-jin5? Lan2 i2-keng chhin-sin u7 thiaN-tioh8 I chhin-chhui3 kong2 a3!몯

Te7 23 ChiuN

Ia5-sou chai7 Pi2-liap8-to e5 bin7-cheng5: (Ma2 27:1-2, 11-14; Kho2 15:1-5; Iok 18:28-38)
	1) Hit e5 si5, choan5-the2 e5 gi7-oan5 long2 khia7 khi2-lai5, ah Ia5-sou khi3 Pi2-liap8-to e5 bin7-cheng5.  2) In chiu7 khai-si2 khong3-ko3 I kong2: 몮Goan2 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 lang5 be5-hek8 lan2 e5 kok-bin5, chou2-chi2 lang5 lap8-soe3 hou7 Hong5-te3, iu7-koh soan-gian5 I pun2-sin chiu7-si7 Ki-tok, chiu7-si7 kok-ong5.몯  3) Pi2-liap8-to mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Li2 si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 ong5 si7 bo5?몯 Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, 몮Si7, chiau3 li2 kong2 an2-ne.몯  4) Pi2-liap8-to chiu7 tui3 hiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap kun5--chiong3 kong2, 몮Goa2 chhoe7 bo5 li2-iu5 thang ka7 chit e5 lang5 phoaN3-choe7.몯  5) Tan7-si7 in lu2 kian-chhi5 chu2-tiuN kong2: 몬I tui3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 khai-si2, Iu5-thai3 choan5-kok kiaN5 thau3-thau3, lai5-kau3 chia, eng7 I e5 kau3-gi7 sian3-tong7 bin5-chiong3 khi2 pok8-tong7.몯

Ia5-sou chai7 Hi-lut8 e5 bin7-cheng5:
	6) Pi2-liap8-to thiaN-tioh8 an2-ne, chiu7 mng7 khoaN3 chit e5 lang5 si7 Ka-li7-li7-lang5 a2 m7-si7.  7) I chit8-e7 chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou si7 siok8 ti7 Hi-lut8 e5 koan2-hat ha7, chiu7 sang3 Ia5-sou khi3 Hi-lut8 hia. Tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5 Hi-lut8 ia7 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  8) Hi-lut8 chit8-e7 kiN3-tioh8 Ia5-sou chiu7 hui-siong5 hoaN-hi2, in-ui7 i bat thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-sou e5 tai7-chi3, chin ku2 chiu7 it-tit8 siuN7 ai3-boeh kiN3 I; ia7 hi-bong7 boeh khoaN3 I cho3 chit8-koa2 sin5-chek.  9) I chiu7 mng7 Ia5-sou chin-che7 tai7-chi3, tan7-si7 Ia5-sou long2 bo5 ka7 i in3 poaN3-ku3.  10) Che3-si-tiuN2 kap keng-hak8-chia2 kiaN5 chin3-cheng5, kek8-lek8 ka7 I ko3.  11) Hi-lut8 ia7 kap i e5 peng-a2 cho3-hoe2 ka7 I bu2-jiok8, ka7 I hi3-lang7, jian5-au7 koh ka7 I chheng7 chit8 nia2 chin sui2 e5 tng5-phau3, chiah ka7 I sang3 tng2-khi3 hou7 Pi2-liap8-to.  12) Hi-lut8 kap Pi2-liap8-to pun2-lai5 si7 kiat oan-siu5-e5; tui3 hit chit8 jit8 khi2 soah piN3-cho3 ho2 peng5-iu2.

Ia5-sou pi7 phoaN3 si2-heng5: (Ma2 27:15-26; Kho2 15:6-15; Iok 18:39-19:16)
	13) Pi2-liap8-to chiu7 tiau3-chip8 che3-si-tiuN2, koaN-oan5 kap peh-seN3 lai5,  14) ka7 in kong2: 몮Lin2 ah-sang3 chit e5 lang5 lai5 goa2 chia, khong3-ko3 I sian3-tong7 jin5-bin5. TaN goa2 chhin-sin ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 sim2-mng7 e5 kiat-ko2, long2 chha5 bo5 lin2 sou2 khong3-ko3 e5 choe7-chng7.  15) Hi-lut8 ia7 jin7-teng7 I bo5 choe7, chiah chiong I sang3 tng2-lai5 lan2 chia. Kho2-kian3 chit e5 lang5 bo5 cho3 sim2-mih eng-kai siu7 si2-heng5 e5 tai7-chi3.  16) Sou2-i2 goa2 boeh kio3 lang5 eng7 piN ka7 I phah, jian5-au7 chiah pang3 I khi3.몯  ( 17) Mui2-ni5 e5 PoaN5-hoe3-cheh, Chong2-tok tioh8 chiau3 in e5 iau-kiu5 ka7 in pang3 chit8 e5 hoan7-lang5.)  18) Kun5-chiong3 tang5-che5 toa7 siaN hoah kong2, 몮Ka7 I thai5-si2. Ka7 goan2 pang3 Pa-liap8-pa chhut-lai5!몯  19) (Chit e5 Pa-liap8-pa si7 in-ui7 ti7 siaN5-lai7 chok-loan7 sat-jin5 hou7 lang5 koaiN ti7 kaN-gak8 e5.)  20) Pi2-liap8-to in-ui7 siuN7 ai3-boeh pang3 Ia5-sou, chiu7 koh-chai3 tui3 cheng3-lang5 kong2 chit8 pai2.  21) Tan7-si7 in ke3-siok8 hoah kong2, 몮Ka7 I teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3, ka7 I teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3.몯  22) Pi2-liap8-to te7 saN pai2 koh tui3 in kong2: 몮Si7 an3-choaN2? Tau3-te2 chit e5 lang5 u7 hoan7-tioh8 sim2-mih choe7? Goa2 chhoe7 bo5 kin-ki3 thang ka7 I teng7 si2-choe7; sou2-i2 goa2 boeh kio3 lang5 eng7 piN ka7 I phah, jian5-au7 chiah pang3 I khi3.몯  23) Tan7-si7 in it-tit8 ke3-siok8 toa7-siaN hoah, iau-kiu5 i tioh8 ka7 Ia5-sou teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3. Choe3-au7 in hoah e5 siaN tat8-tioh8 bok8-tek.  24) Pi2-liap8-to chiu7 chiau3 in sou2 iau-kiu5 e5, ka7 Ia5-sou teng7-choe7.  25) I chiu7 pang3 in sou2 iau-kiu5 hit e5 ui7-tioh8 chok-loan7 kap sat-jin5 hou7 lang5 koaiN ti7 kaN lai7 e5 hoan7-lang5, chiong Ia5-sou kau hou7 in, chiau3 in e5 i3-su3 khi3 chhu2-li2.

Ia5-sou pi7 teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3: (Ma2 27:32-44; Kho2 15:21-32; Iok 19:17-27)
	26) Peng-su7 ah Ia5-sou khi3 e5 si5, ti7 lou7-nih8 tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 Kou2-li7-nai7-lang5 Se-bun5, tu2-tu2 tui3 chng-kha chhut-lai5. In chiu7 liah8 i lai5, kio3 i gia5 sip8-ji7-ke3, toe3 Ia5-sou e5 au7-bin7-kiaN5.
	27) U7 chit8 toa7-tin7 lang5 teh toe3 Ia5-sou; ki5-tiong ia7 u7 chit8-koa2 hu7-jin5-lang5 ui7 I pi-siong thi5-khau3.  28) Ia5-sou oat8-thau5 tui3 in kong2: 몮Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 a3, lin2 m7-bian2 ui7 goa2 lai5 thi5-khau3; tian-to3 tioh8 ui7 lin2 ka-ti7 kap lin2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 lai5 thi5-khau3.  29) In-ui7 lang5 e7 kong2, 몬Be7 hoai5-in7 e5, m7-bat seN-kiaN2 e5, m7-bat hou7 gin2-na2 chiah8-leng e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3!몭 hit e5 si5 teh-boeh kau3 a3.  30) Hit e5 si5, lang5 e7 khai-si2 tui3 koan5-soaN kong2, 몬Ka7 goan2 hip loh8-lai5!몭 Tui3 ke7-soaN kong2, 몬Ka7 goan2 kham3 khi2-lai5!몭  31) Bo5 eng-kai hiaN5-hoe2 e5 tam5-chha5 na7 tioh8 theh8 lai5 hiaN5-hoe2, hiah-e5 ta-chha5 kiu3-keng3 tioh8 an3-choaN2?몯
	32) Ia5-sou i2-goa7 iau2-u7 nng7 e5 hoan7-lang5, hou7 lang5 ah chhut-lai5 boeh kap Ia5-sou cho3-hoe2 chhu2 si2-heng5.  33) In khi3-kau3 chit8 e5 kio3-cho3 몮Thau5-khak-oaN2 e5 sou2-chai7,몯 chiu7 toa3 hia ka7 Ia5-sou teng3 toa3 sip8-ji7-ke3, ia7 teng3 hit nng7 e5 hoan7-lang5, chit8 e5 toa3 I e5 chiaN3-peng5, chit8 e5 toa3 I e5 to3-peng5.  34) Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Hu7-chhin a3! Sia3-bian2 in, in-ui7 in m7 chai in sou2 cho3 e5 tai7-chi3.몯 In chiu7 thiu khau-a2 lai5 pun Ia5-sou e5 saN.  35) Cheng3-lang5 khia7 ti7 hia teh khoaN3. Hiah-e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 thau5-lang5 ia7 ka7 I thi2-chhio3, kong2: 몮I u7 kiu3 pat8-lang5; I na7-si7 siong7-chu2 sou2 keng2-soan2 e5 Bi2-sai3-a, taN tioh8 hou7 I kiu3 ka-ti7.몯  36) Peng-su7 ia7 ka7 I hi3-lang7, phang5 sng-khi3 e5 chiu2 boeh hou7 I lim,  37) kong2, 몮Li2 na7-si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 ong5, taN tioh8 kiu3 Li2 ka-ti7.몯  38) Ti7 I e5 thau5-khak-teng2 u7 chit8 te3 choe7-chng7 e5 pai5-a2, sia2 kong2: 몮Chit e5 si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 ong5.몯
	39) Hou7 lang5 teng3 ti7 sip8-ji7-ke3 e5 hoan7-lang5 e5 chit8 e5, bu2-jiok8 Ia5-sou kong2: 몮Li2 kam2 m7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a? Tioh8 kiu3 Li2 ka-ti7, ia7 tioh8 kiu3 goan2.몯  40) Tan7-si7 leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 hoan7-lang5 chek-pi7 i kong2: 몮Li2 kam2 long2 m7-kiaN Siong7-chu2? Li2 kap I siu7 kang7-khoan2 e5 phoaN3-heng5.  41) In-ui7 lan2 koe2-khi3 e5 heng5-ui5 eng-kai siu7 chit khoan2 e5 chhu2-heng5. Tan7-si7 chit e5 lang5, long2 m7-bat cho3 m7-tioh8.몯  42) I chiu7 tui3 Ia5-sou kong2, 몮Ia5-sou a3, Li2 cho3 Kok-ong5 lai5 e5 si5, chhiaN2 Li2 e7-ki3-tit goa2!몯  43) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2, 몮Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 li2 kong2: kin-na2-jit8 li2 e7 kap Goa2 cho3-hoe2 toa3 Lok8-hng5.몯

Ia5-sou e5 si2-bong5: (Ma2 27:45-56; Kho2 15:33-41; Iok 19:28-30)
	44) Hit e5 si5 chha-put-to si7 tiong-tau3, jit8-thau5 sit kng, choan5 te7 long2 pian3-cho3 ou-ou-am3-am3, it-tit8 soa3 kau3 e7-pou-si5 chha-put-to saN tiam2.  45) Koa3 ti7 Seng3-tian7 lai7 e5 pou3-li5 lih8 cho3 nng7 peng5.  46) Ia5-sou chiu7 toa7 siaN kio3 kong2, 몮Hu7-chhin a3, Goa2 chiong Goa2 e5 leng5-hun5 kau-thok Li2.몯 An2-ne kong2 soah khui3 chiu7 tng7-khi3.  47) Lian5-tiuN2 khoaN3-kiN3 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2 kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 chin-chiaN3 si7 bo5-choe7 e5 lang5.몯  48) Chu7-chip8 lai5 khoaN3 chit e5 tiuN5-bin7 e5 cheng3-lang5, khoaN3-tioh8 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3, tai7-ke chiu7 ian5-lou7 tui5 sim-koaN tng2-khi3.  49) Hiah-e5 bat Ia5-sou e5 lang5, i2-kip8 hiah-e5 tui3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 toe3 I lai5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, long2 khia7 ti7 hng7-hng7 teh khoaN3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3.

Ia5-sou e5 bai5-chong3: (Ma2 27:57-61; Kho2 15:42-47; Iok 19:38-42)
	50) U7 chit8 e5 lang5 kio3-cho3 Iok-sek. I si7 kong-gi7-hoe7 e5 gi7-oan5, ia7 si7 chit8 e5 sian7-liong5 cheng3-gi7 e5 lang5.  51) I bo5 chan3-tong5 ki5-tha e5 gi7-oan5 e5 ke3-bou5 kap heng5-tong7. I si7 Iu5-thai3 e5 siaN5-chhi7 A-li7-ma2-thai3 e5 lang5, peng5-sou3 u7 teh ki5-thai7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 lai5-lim5.  52) Chit e5 lang5 khi3 kiN3 Pi2-liap8-to, ka7 i chheng2-kiu5 siu-bai5 Ia5-sou e5 sin-si.  53) I chiong sin-si tui3 sip8-ji7-ke3-teng2 pang3 loh8-lai5, eng7 iu3-te7-a2-pou3 ka7 I pau khi2-lai5, jian5-au7 ka7 I an-chong3 toa3 phah chioh8-piah cho3-pian7 e5 bong7-lai7. Chit e5 bong7 long2 iau2 m7-bat bai5-chong3 lang5.  54) Hit jit8 chiu7-si7 Pai3-gou7, An-hioh-jit8 teh-boeh kau3 a3.
	55) Tui3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 toe3 Ia5-sou lai5 hiah-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, toe3 Iok-sek khi3. In chu3-i3 khoaN3 hit e5 bong7, iu7-koh khoaN3 an3-choaN2 teh an-ti3 Ia5-sou e5 sin-si.  56) In chiu7 tng2-khi3 chun2-pi7 phang-liau7 kap phang-iu5 boeh boah Ia5-sou e5 sin-si. An-hioh-jit8 in chiu7 chiau3 Lut8-hoat e5 kui-teng7 hioh-khun3.

Te7 24 ChiuN

Ia5-sou e5 hok8-hoat8: (Ma2 28:1-10; Kho2 16:1-8; Iok 20:1-10)
	1) Le2-pai3 chai2-khi2 thau3-cha2, hiah-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 toa3 in sou2 pi7-pan7 e5 phang-liau7 lai5 kau3 Ia5-sou e5 bong7-nih8.  2) In khoaN3-kiN3 hit liap8 chioh8-thau5 i2-keng tui3 bong7-khau2 lian3 khui-khi3 a3.  3) In chit8-e7 jip8-khi3, chhoe7 bo5 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 si-the2.  4) In iau2 ti7 hia teh be7 liau2-kai2 chit e5 tai7-chi3 e5 si5, hut-jian5-kan u7 nng7 e5 lang5, chheng7 kng iaN3-iaN3 e5 saN, lai5 khia7 toa3 in e5 piN-a.  5) In toa7 tioh8-kiaN, bin7 phak loh8-khi3 thou5-kha, tan7-si7 hit-nng7 e5 lang5 ka7 in kong2: 몮Lin2 an3-choaN2 ti7 si2-lang5 e5 tiong-kan teh chhoe7 chit8 e5 oah8-lang5?  6) I bo5 ti7 chia. I i2-keng hok8-hoat8 a7. Lin2 tioh8 e7-ki3-tit I iau2 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 e5 si5, ka7 lin2 kong2 e5 oe7,  7) kong2: 몬Jin5-chu2 it-teng7 e7 hou7 lang5 kau hou7 choe7-jin5 e5 chhiu2-thau5. In e7 ka7 I teng3 toa3 sip8-ji7-ke3, tan7-si7 te7 saN jit8, e7 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5.몭몯  8) hiah-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 siuN7 khi2 Ia5-sou e5 oe7.  9) In li7-khui bong7 tng2-khi3, chiu7 chiong chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 long2 tui3 chap8-it e5 Su3-tou5 kap ki5-tha long2-chong2 e5 lang5 po3-ko3!  10) Chiah-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7-si7 Boat8-tai7-liap8-lang5 Ma2-li7-a, kap Iok-a-na2, i2-kip8 Nga2-kok e5 lau7-bo2 Ma2-li7-a. Kap in tau3-tin7 e5 ki5-tha e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, ia7 long2 chiong chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 tui3 Su3-tou5 po3-ko3.  11) Su3-tou5 siuN7 kong2 chiah-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 bo5-iaN2-bo5-jiah, soah m7 sin3 in.  12) Tan7-si7 Pi2-tek peh khi2-lai5, chau2 khi3-kau3 bong7-nih8; aN3 loh8-khi3 khoaN3 lai7-bin7 e5 si5, chi2-u7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit te3 iu3-te7-a2-pou3, i2-goa7 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 poaN3 hang7. I chiu7 tng2-khi3, tui3 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3, kam2-kak bok5-beng5 ki5-biau7.

Boeh khi3 I2-ma2-ngou2 e5 lou7-siong7: (Kho2 16:12-13)
	13) Kang7 hit jit8, bun5-tou5 e5 tiong-kan u7 nng7 e5 lang5 teh-boeh khi3 chit8 e5 kio3-cho3 I2-ma2-ngou2 e5 chng-kha. Chit e5 sou2-chai7 li7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chha-put-to u7 chhit eng-li2.  14) In na2 kiaN5 na2 teh tam5-lun7 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3.  15) In tu2 teh tam5-lun7 lai5 tam5-lun7 khi3 e5 si5, Ia5-sou chhin-sin oa2-lai5 kap in cho3 tin7 kiaN5,  16) tan7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 u7 sim2-mih lai5 chou2-gai7 in e5 bak8-chiu, lai5 hou7 in be7 jin7-tit I si7 Ia5-sou.  17) Ia5-sou tui3 in kong2, 몮Lin2 na2 kiaN5 na2 teh gi7-lun7 sim2-mih tai7-chi3?몯 In chiu7 khia7 tiaN7-tiaN7, bin7 chin iu-chhiu5.  18) Ki5-tiong u7 chit8 e5 kio3-cho3 Kek-liu5-pa, in3 I kong2: 몮Toa3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 lang5, bo5-tiaN7-tioh8 kan-taN Li2 chit8 e5 m7 chai-iaN2 chit kui2 jit8 ti7 hia sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3!몯  19) Ia5-sou mng7 in kong2, 몮Si7 sim2-mih tai7-chi3?몯 In chiu7 ka7 I kong2: 몮Chiu7-si7 Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou e5 tai7-chi3! I si7 chit8 ui7 tai7-gian5-jin5, bo5-lun7 Siong7-chu2 kap peh-seN3 long2 khoaN3 I sou2 kong2 e5, sou2 cho3 e5, chin u7 koan5-leng5.  20) Lan2 chiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap leng2-siu7, ka7 I sang3-khi3 hou7 lang5 phoaN3 si2-heng5, soah ka7 I teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3.  21) Goan2 teh ki5-thai7 I si7 Hit-ui7 boeh lai5 kai2-kiu3 I2-sek-liat8 e5. M7-na7 an2-ne, chit e5 tai7-chi3 hoat-seng liau2-au7, kau3 kin-na2-jit8 i2-keng si7 te7-saN jit8 a7!  22) Tan7-si7 goan2 e5 tiong-kan u7 kui2-na7 e5 hu7-jin5-=lang5 hou7 goan2 toa7 tioh8-kiaN. In thau3-cha2 chiu7 khi3 bong7-nih8,  23) tan7-si7 chhoe7 bo5 I e5 sin-si. In tng2-lai5 po3-ko3 kong2 in u7 khoaN3-kiN3 thian-sai3 hian2-hian7, lai5 ka7 in kong2 I teh oah8!  24) Goa2 tiong-kan ia7 u7 kui2-na7 e5 lang5 khi3 bong7-nih8, khoaN3-kiN3 tak8-hang7 tai7-chi3, khak-sit8 kap hu7-jin5-lang5 sou2 po3-ko3 e5 long2 kang7-khoan2, tan7-si7 in bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou.몯
	25) Ia5-sou tui3 chit nng7 e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: 몮Ou3, lin2 na2 chiah-nih8 gong7, lin2 na2 chiah-nih8 tun7, be7-tang3 siong-sin3 tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7!  26) Bi2-sai3-a kam2 m7-si7 tioh8-ai3 tai7-seng siu7 chiah-e5 khou2-lan7, chiah lai5 chin3-jip8 I e5 eng5-iau7?몯  27) Ia5-sou chiu7 chiong Seng3-keng sou2 u7 koan-he7 I e5 tai7-chi3 ka7 in soat-beng5, chiu7-si7 tui3 Mou5-se sou2 kong2 e5 khai-si2, it-tit8 kong2 kau3 chiong3 tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 kong2 e5, chit8-toaN7 chit8-toaN7 ka7 in soat-beng5.
	28) In teh-boeh kau3 in sou2 boeh khi3 e5 chng-kha e5 si5, Ia5-sou na2 chhin-chhiuN7 boeh ke3-siok8 it-tit8 khi3 e5 khoan2;  20) tan7-si7 hit nng7 e5 kiong5 ka7 I lau5, kong2, 몮ChhiaN2 Li2 kap goan2 toa3 chia keh-me5, in-ui7 jit8 teh-boeh loh8 a7, thiN teh-boeh am3 a3.몯 Ia5-sou chiu7 jip8-khi3 kap in toa3.  30) Ia5-sou kap in che7-toh e5 si5, chiu7 theh8 mi7-pau khi2-lai5 chiok-hok, jian5-au7 peh cho3 chit8-te3 chit8-te3, pun hou7 in nng7 e5.  31) In e5 bak8-chiu chiah khui, chiu7 jin7-tioh8 I si7 Ia5-sou; tan7-si7 hit e5 si5, i2-keng bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou a.  32) In chiu7 hou7-siong kong2: 몮I ian5-lou7 kiaN5 ian5-lou7 kap lan2 kong2-oe7, ka7 lan2 kai2-sek Seng3-keng e5 si5, lan2 e5 sim lai7 kam2 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 hoe2 teh toh8.몯
	33) In chiu7 sui5-si5 chhut-hoat, to3 tng2-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2. In khoaN3-kiN3 hit chap8-it e5 Su3-tou5 kap ki5-tha e5 lang5 chu7-chip8 ti7 hia,  34) teh tam5-lun7 kong2, 몮Chu2 chin-chiaN3 hok8-hoat8 a7! I i2-keng hian2-hian7 hou7 Se-bun5 khoaN3-kiN3 a3!몯  35) Hit nng7 e5 chiong ti7 lou7-nih8 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3, kap khoaN3-kiN3 I teh peh mi7-pau chiah jin7-chhut I si7 Chu2 e5 tai7-chi3 ka7 in po3-ko3.

Ia5-sou hian2-hian7 hou7 I e5 Su3-tou5 khoaN3: (Ma2 28:16-20; Kho2 16:14-16; Iok 20:19-23; Heng5-toan7 1:6-8)
	36) Hit nng7 e5 iau2 teh kong2 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 e5 si5, Ia5-sou chhin-sin lai5 khia7 toa3 in e5 tiong-kan, tui3 in kong2, 몮Goan7 lin2 peng5-an!몯  37) Tan7-si7 in chin tioh8-kiaN, siuN7-cho3 in khoaN3-tioh8 kui2.  38) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 in kong2: 몮Lin2 an3-choaN2 teh put-an, an3-choaN2 sim-lai7 khi2 giau5-gi5?  39) Lin2 khoaN3 Goa2 e5 chhiu2, Goa2 e5 kha; m7-si7 pat8-lang5, sit8-chai7 si7 Goa2 pun2-sin. Lin2 bong khoaN3-bai7 le3 chiu7 e7 chai-iaN2, in-ui7 kui2 si7 bo5 bah bo5 kut e5. Lin2 khoaN3, Goa2 long2 u7!몯  40) I an2-ne kong2 liau2-au7, chiu7 po3 in khoaN3 I e5 kha-chhiu2.  41) In-ui7 in koe3-thau5 hoaN-hi2, kam2-kak bok8-beng5 ki5-biau7, soah iau2-ku2 be7-tang3 siong-sin3. Sou2-i2 Ia5-sou chiu7 mng7 in kong2, 몮Lin2 chia u7 sim2-mih thang chiah8 bo5?몯  42) In chiu7 theh8 chit8 te3 hang e5 hi5 hou7 I.  43) I chiap koe3-lai5, toa3 in e5 bin7-cheng5 chiah8 hou7 in khoaN3.
	44) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 in kong2: 몮Goa2 iau2 kap lin2 cho3-hoe2 e5 si5, i2-keng u7 chiong chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 ka7 lin2 kong2 a3! Chiu7-si7 kong2 ti7 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat kap tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 ki3-liok8 i2-kip8 Si-phian e5 lai7-bin7 sou2 ki3-chai3 koan-he7 Goa2 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 tioh8-ai3 eng3-giam7.몯  45) Ia5-sou chiu7 khui in e5 sim-gan2, hou7 in e7-tang3 liau2-kai2 Seng3-keng.  46) Koh tui3 in kong2: 몮Che chiu7-si7 Seng3-keng sou2 ki3-chai3 ek5ong: Bi2-sai3-a tioh8 siu7 khou2-lan7, tan7-si7 te7-saN jit8 Siong7-chu2 it-teng7 e7 hou7 I tui3 si2-lang5 e5 tiong-kan koh-oah8 khi2-lai5.  47) Iu7-koh ki3-chai3 kong2: tioh8 hong7 I e5 mia5, chiong hoe3-kai2 lai5 tit-tioh8 sia3-choe7 e5 to7-li2, tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khai-si2, it-tit8 thoan5-iong5 kau3 choan5 se3-kai3.  48) Lin2 chiu7-si7 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 e5 kian3-cheng3-jin5.  49) Goa2 pun2-sin boeh chiong Goa2 e5 Hu7-chhin sou2 eng3-un2 e5 sang3 hou7 lin2; tan7-si7 lin2 tioh8-ai3 toa3 chit e5 siaN5-lai7, theng3-hau7 kau3 lin2 tit-tioh8 tui3 teng2-bin7 lai5 e5 koan5-leng5.몯

Ia5-sou seng-thian: (Kho2 16:19-20; Heng5-toan7 1:9-11)
	50) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou chiu7 chhoa7 in tui3 hit e5 siaN5-chhi7 chhut-khi3 kau3 Pek-tai7-ni5, chiu7 giah8 siang-chhiu2 khi2-lai5 ka7 in chiok-hok.  51) Teh ka7 in chiok-hok e5 tiong-kan, chiu7 li7-khui in, hou7 Siong7-chu2 ka7 I the5-seng khi3 thiN-teng2.  52) In chiu7 phak loh8-khi3 ka7 I pai3, hoaN-hoaN-hi2-hi2 tng2-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 SiaN5,  53) tak8-jit8 toa3 seng3-tian7 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2.
